
-----title
宁波 (出生地)

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1223&endYear=1225')">1223-1225年</a>　居乡。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='8a2baff478ca49899f6464d45f62e853_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8a2baff478ca49899f6464d45f62e853");'><span id='8a2baff478ca49899f6464d45f62e853_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　居乡，从学乡先生吴参倚。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a605fb9e885f405fa2e7cf4f04535912_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a605fb9e885f405fa2e7cf4f04535912");'><span id='a605fb9e885f405fa2e7cf4f04535912_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1252&endYear=1255')">1252-1255年</a>，30-33岁</div><div id='a605fb9e885f405fa2e7cf4f04535912' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1252&endYear=1252')">1252年12月3日</a>　父卒于温州任，丁父忧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年</a>　居乡丁父忧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1254')">1254年</a>　仍在丁父忧，皇子忠王赵祺行成人礼，作表。作品：代贺皇子忠王行冠礼表。<div id='poem_1318165' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318165' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318165?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代贺皇子忠王行冠礼表<span class='inlineComment2'>（宝祐二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1254年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318165")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318165_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318165'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318165'>上圣贻谋，茂毓成人之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318165_comment'></div>初阳展采，肇称冠阼之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318165_comment'></div>华夏胪欢，宗祊锡美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318165_comment'></div>窃以十五志于学，备体所以正容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318165_comment'></div>万亿年之休，重本在于谨始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318165_comment'></div>铺观旧典，莫盛祥符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318165_comment'></div>元衮介圭，锡命甲寅之岁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318165_comment'></div>华缨峨弁，筮辰令月之冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318165_comment'></div>遹骏有声，克开厥后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318165_comment'></div>恭惟体元首物，立爱始亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318165_comment'></div>庆垂万世之基，教子必以礼乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318165_comment'></div>忠为百行之冕，稽古建尔国家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318165_comment'></div>眷言复七日之刚，卜协震荐雷之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318165_comment'></div>主于尊属，酌开元太极之彝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318165_comment'></div>宾以辅臣，轶五凤孟春之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318165_comment'></div>有仪可象，爰字孔嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318165_comment'></div>重曜宣光，盼璧珠于紫极；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318165_comment'></div>三加荐醴，节金石于黄钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318165_comment'></div>受周祉之无疆，卜汉储之早定，天迪从保，邦永孚休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318165_comment'></div>臣越在迩藩，颂聆亿铄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318165_comment'></div>既冠而明有敬，奚烦贾谊之规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318165_comment'></div>会邸而称无双，莫预黄香之列。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1318165_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1255&endYear=1255')">1255年2月</a>　丁父忧，服阕待命。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='106dc30d2a08414f9279bf56d145bb7d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("106dc30d2a08414f9279bf56d145bb7d");'><span id='106dc30d2a08414f9279bf56d145bb7d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1274')">1272-1274年</a>，50-52岁</div><div id='106dc30d2a08414f9279bf56d145bb7d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年9月丁丑</a>　母陈太硕人卒。丁母忧，归居于鄞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年6月</a>　丁母忧，撰辑《周易郑康成注》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年7月癸未</a>　嘉国公即位。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='3618a50a566b4741af02ebbf86072bdb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3618a50a566b4741af02ebbf86072bdb");'><span id='3618a50a566b4741af02ebbf86072bdb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1296')">1275-1296年</a>，53-74岁</div><div id='3618a50a566b4741af02ebbf86072bdb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年11月甲午</a>　东归。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年12月丁未</a>　遣中使谭纯德以翰林学士宣召不赴。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　宋亡，应麟闭门不出，朝夕坐堂上，取经史诸书讲解论辩。子昌世甫十岁，听受无倦。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年3月乙亥</a>　元兵至鄞，袁镛與战死，作诗。作品：悼袁进士镛诗（大柱不可折）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　戴表元执弟子礼来受学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1277&endYear=1277')">1277年</a>　袁洪遣其子桷来授业，桷年十二岁，居门下十年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1279')">1278-1279年</a>　居家。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1280&endYear=1280')">1280年8月</a>　著《通鉴地理通释》成。<div id='poem_1318206' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318206' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318206?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通鉴地理通释后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1280年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318206")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318206_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318206'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318206'>太极肇分，天先成而地后定，天依形，地附气，地囿于天者也，而言地理者难于言天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318206_comment'></div>何为其难也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318206_comment'></div>日月星辰之度终古而不易，郡国山川之名屡变而无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318206_comment'></div>是故图以经之，书以纬之，仰观俯察，其用一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318206_comment'></div>《虞书》「九共」，先儒以为九丘，其篇轶焉，传于今者，《禹贡》、《职方》而止耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318206_comment'></div>若《山海经》、《周书·王会》、《尔雅》之《释地》、《管氏》之《地员》、《吕览》之《有始》、《鸿烈》之《地形》，亦好古爱奇者所不废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318206_comment'></div>然诸儒之传注异，历代之区宇殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318206_comment'></div>禹之九河，班《志》仅得其三；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318206_comment'></div>商之八迁，孔《疏》未闻其四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318206_comment'></div>汉水东西之分，积石大小之辨，荆山之于荆豫，梁岐之于冀雍，潜在荆者未见，蔡在圻内者未详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318206_comment'></div>三江九江，五邦三亳，则《书》之说异焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318206_comment'></div>还之为营，祢之为坭，以著为齐地，以韩城为涿郡，自土之为自杜，倭迟之为郁夷，驺虞之为梁邹，二南之为南郡、南阳，则《诗》之说异焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318206_comment'></div>扬纡在冀，而《尔雅》以为秦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318206_comment'></div>卢水在济北，而康成读为雷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318206_comment'></div>漳水之为潞，吴山之为岳，五湖混于具区，颍湛列于荆浸，此《职方》之疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318206_comment'></div>豫章在江南，而江北之地未知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318206_comment'></div>中牟在河南，而河北之地难考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318206_comment'></div>许田，鲁地，而非近许；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318206_comment'></div>鄢，郑邑，而非鄢陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318206_comment'></div>谷、小谷之有别，父城、城父之不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318206_comment'></div>此《春秋》之疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318206_comment'></div>二地而一名者，若王城、葵丘、酒泉、贝丘、钟离之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318206_comment'></div>一地而二名者，若白羽、夹谷、夷、垂葭、发阳之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318206_comment'></div>方城、细柳、丹水之有三，涂山、历山、东阳、武城之有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318206_comment'></div>「瞻彼洛矣」，与东都之洛异；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318206_comment'></div>「导洛自熊耳」，与宜阳之熊耳殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318206_comment'></div>首阳、空桐、新城、石门、石城、丹阳、白沙、硖石之属，其地非一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318206_comment'></div>毕万之魏为河中之永乐，而以元城为大名，失矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318206_comment'></div>「自庐振廪」为襄阳之中庐，而以合肥为庐国，失矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318206_comment'></div>潘岳赋《西征》，不知成师之曲沃在河东；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318206_comment'></div>韩皋论广陵散，不知魏之扬州治寿春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318206_comment'></div>韩文公南阳人，在河内之脩武，而误曰邓州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318206_comment'></div>《史记》郧关在汉中之长利，而误曰洵阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1318206_comment'></div>杜子美诗三奇戍在彭州之导江，而误改曰三城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1318206_comment'></div>荀卿兰陵非常州也，孔明渡泸非泸州也，公琰屯涪非涪州也，公瑾赤壁非黄也，元规南楼非鄂也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1318206_comment'></div>郢都白雪误于郢州，东海二疏误于海州，以涂山为会稽，以齧桑为采桑，以大别为安丰，以东陵为庐江，以楚丘为成武，以街亭为南郑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1318206_comment'></div>袭讹踵缪，不可殚纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1318206_comment'></div>汉沔一也，而或二之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1318206_comment'></div>吴会二也，而或一之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1318206_comment'></div>江统误酂于沛郡，皇甫谧误商丘于濮阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1318206_comment'></div>颜师古误邛都于邛州，青衣于嘉州，南陵于宣州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1318206_comment'></div>注《文选》不知夷庚，注《本草》不知沙苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1318206_comment'></div>博见彊志者犹或失之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1318206_comment'></div>旧迹湮没，如济绝于荥，碣石沦于海，昆明凿而镐京为池，隋城立而汉都为苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1318206_comment'></div>南北侨置，如青有太原，豫有广陵，六合之为秦郡，项城之为秣陵，玉门之为会稽，寻阳在蕲而移柴桑，当涂在濠而寓姑孰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1318206_comment'></div>郡名非古，如云之云中，平之北平，蓟之渔阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1318206_comment'></div>县名非古，如京兆之武功，丰州之九原，皆非秦汉之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1318206_comment'></div>或若异而同，或似是而非，不可谓博识为玩物而不之考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1318206_comment'></div>余閒居观《通鉴》，将笺释其地名，举纲提要，首以州域，次以都邑，推表山川，参以乐毅、王朴之崇论宏议，稽《左氏》、《国语》、《史记》、《战国策》、《通典》所叙历代形势，以为兴替成败之鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1318206_comment'></div>大《易》设险守国，《春秋》书下阳、彭城、虎牢之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1318206_comment'></div>河湟复而唐衰，燕代割而辽炽，述其事终焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1318206_comment'></div>若昔对白题羊肠，帝丘内黄，问松亭柳河者，以该洽见称，今岂无其人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1318206_comment'></div>孤陋寡闻，未免阙误，以俟博雅君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1318206_comment'></div>山河不改，陵谷娄迁，亦以发揽古之一慨云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1318206_comment'></div>上章执徐岁橘壮之月，子王子书《通释》后。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1318206_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1280&endYear=1280')">1280年</a>　长子良学卒，官至两浙运干，年三十三。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年5月</a>　作《汉制考》成。<div id='poem_1318193' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318193' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318193?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汉制考序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1281年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318193")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318193_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318193'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318193'>汉制载于史者，先儒考之详矣，其见他书者未之考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318193_comment'></div>尝谓法始乎伏牺而成乎尧，三代损益，至周大备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318193_comment'></div>夫子「从周」与「从先进」之言，所谓百世可知者，其法著于《春秋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318193_comment'></div>东迁之初，先王典章概有存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318193_comment'></div>义和秬鬯之赉，王命犹重也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318193_comment'></div>司徒缁衣之美，王官犹贤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318193_comment'></div>祭仲论京不度，过制之城犹未众也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318193_comment'></div>无骇卒始请族，世官之敝犹未远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318193_comment'></div>泰山有祊，则巡守之迹犹可复也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318193_comment'></div>九宗五正有后，则封建之制犹可寻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318193_comment'></div>师服之言建国，臧僖伯之谏观鱼，则据经守古之士犹多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318193_comment'></div>《春秋》何为而作乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318193_comment'></div>宰咺归赗，天衷民彝大泯乱，《春秋》所以始欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318193_comment'></div>于献六羽，于税亩，皆曰「初」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318193_comment'></div>于丘甲，于三军，皆曰「作」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318193_comment'></div>于南门，于雉门及两观，皆曰「新作」，夫子盖伤之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318193_comment'></div>秦作西畤，胪于郊祀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318193_comment'></div>鲁惠公请郊禘，史角实往而祀，礼始僭矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318193_comment'></div>其后齐作内政而兵制变，晋作爰田而田制变，晋作执秩而官制变，郑铸刑书而刑制变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318193_comment'></div>大夫奏肆夏，季氏旅泰山，晋不知殽烝，鲁不知尚羔，礼几亡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318193_comment'></div>然名卿大夫讲问故实，三代文献蔼如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318193_comment'></div>纳鼎有谏，观社有谏，申繻名子之对，里革断罟之规，御孙别男女之贽，管仲辞上卿之飨，柳下季之述祀典，单襄公之述夏令秩官，魏绛之述夏训虞箴，郯子能言纪官，州鸠能言七律，子革、倚相能诵《祈招》懿戒，观射父之陈祭祀，闵马父之称《商颂》，格言猷训，粲然可睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318193_comment'></div>齐虞人之守官，鲁宗人之守礼，懔懔秋霜夏日之严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318193_comment'></div>刘子所云天地之中，子产所云天地之经，胥臣敬德之聚，晏子礼之善物，又皆识其大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318193_comment'></div>统纪相承，渊源相续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318193_comment'></div>得夏时坤乾，见《易》象、鲁《春秋》而知三代之礼，所以扶持于未坠者岂一人之力哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318193_comment'></div>战国去籍之馀，孟子言井地曰「大略」，言班爵禄曰「闻其略」，言诸侯丧礼曰「未学而尝闻」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318193_comment'></div>若其宏纲丕式，因略而致详，推旧而为新，圣人复起，不能易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318193_comment'></div>《春秋》大复古，讥变古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318193_comment'></div>井牧变而阡陌，畿服变而郡县，车乘变而步骑，什一变而箕敛，佩玉变而带剑，簋席变而杯案。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318193_comment'></div>生民之理有穷，则圣王之法可改，古其不可复乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318193_comment'></div>是意惟太史公知之，于《夏》、《殷纪》举孔子正夏时、善殷辂，卓然见损益之要指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318193_comment'></div>于《高帝纪》曰「朝以十月，车服黄屋，左纛」，盖叹其袭秦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1318193_comment'></div>汉之止于为汉，自高帝之袭秦始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1318193_comment'></div>虽然，两汉之制，文中子奚取焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1318193_comment'></div>吁，三代远矣，汉诏令人主自亲其文，犹近于《书》之典诰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1318193_comment'></div>郎卫执戟之用儒生，犹近于王宫之士庶子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1318193_comment'></div>司徒府有百官朝会殿以决大事，犹近于外朝之询众也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1318193_comment'></div>牧守有子孙，郡国有辟举，庶几建侯之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1318193_comment'></div>丞相进见，御坐为起，在舆为下，庶几敬臣之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1318193_comment'></div>三老掌教化，孝悌力田置常员，乡遂之流风遗韵亦间见焉，是之取尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1318193_comment'></div>君子尚论古之人，以为汉去古未远，诸儒佔毕训故之学，虽未尽识三代旧典，而以汉制證遗经，犹幸有传注在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1318193_comment'></div>冕服、车旗、彝器之类，多以叔孙通礼器制度为据，其所臆度无以名之，则谓若今某物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1318193_comment'></div>及唐儒为疏义，又谓去汉久远，虽汉法亦不可考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1318193_comment'></div>盖自西晋板荡之后，见闻放失，习俗流败，汉世之名物称谓知者鲜焉，况帝王制作之法象意义乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1318193_comment'></div>此汉制之仅存于传注者，不可忽不之考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1318193_comment'></div>愚少尝有闻，老弗敢坠，因䌷次为编，以俟后之君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1318193_comment'></div>自流溯源，三代之礼，庶乎其可识矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1318193_comment'></div>辛巳夏五子王子序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1318193_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年</a>　作《四明七观》<div id='poem_1318032' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318032' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318032?labeling=true' target='_blank'>四明七观</a><span class='authorDate'>（1282年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318032")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318032_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318032'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318032'>东野先生韬光环堵，根极深宁，慕白贲以息影，玩素履以洗心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318032_comment'></div>有南州公子，俨然蹐门，言曰：「窃怀太史公之志，广揽四方之恢恑谲怪，升高能赋，山川能说，庶几一二于君子之九能」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318032_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1318032'>《诗·定之方中》传：「建邦能命龟，田能施命，作器能铭，使能造命，升高能赋，师旅能誓，山川能说，丧纪能诔，祭祀能语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318032_comment'></div>君子能此九者，可谓有德音，可以为大夫也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318032_comment'></div>能，叶奴代切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318032_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1318032'>今至是邦也，愿启我以伟观，博我以奇概。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318032_comment'></div>先生曰：「余卧游诗书之囿，视不踰几席，敢诵旧闻，吾子自择焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318032_comment'></div>昔尝观宛委之简，见神禹之《山经》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318032_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1318032'>《吴越春秋》：「禹东巡登衡岳，梦见赤绣衣男子，自称玄夷苍水使者，谓禹曰：『欲得我山书者，斋于黄帝之岳』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318032_comment'></div>禹退斋三日，登宛委山，发石得金简玉字，言治水之要」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318032_comment'></div>《山海经》十二篇，相传为夏禹所记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318032_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1318032'>东有山曰句馀，寔惟四明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318032_comment'></div>南馀姚、北句章，二县以为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318032_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1318032'>《山海经·南山经》：「又东四百里，曰句馀之山」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1318032_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年</a>　作《乾道四明图经辨证》作品：辨乾道四明图经。<div id='poem_1318219' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318219' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318219?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辨乾道四明图经</a><span class='authorDate'>（1282年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318219")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318219_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318219'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318219'>唐卢潘作《庐江四辨》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318219_comment'></div>余观《四明志》首卷有疑，则辨以俟博雅君子择焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318219_comment'></div>《志序》云：「大观初置九域志局，令州县各编纂以进」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318219_comment'></div>余考《会要》、《实录》，景德四年二月庚辰，真宗因览西京图经有所未备，诏诸路州、府、军、监以图经校勘，编入古迹，选文学之官纂修校正，补其阙略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318219_comment'></div>及诸路以图经献，诏知制诰孙仅、待制戚纶、直集贤院王随、大理评事宋绶、邵焕校定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318219_comment'></div>仅等以体制不一，遂重修，命翰林学士李宗谔、知制诰王曾领其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318219_comment'></div>又增张知白、晏殊及李乘、韩熙等参其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318219_comment'></div>大中祥符三年十二月丁巳书成，凡一千三百六十六卷，上之，命宗谔为序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318219_comment'></div>又诏重修大小图经，令职方牒诸州谨其藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318219_comment'></div>尝见《吴郡图经》载李宗谔序，盖景德、祥符所修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318219_comment'></div>郡志以大观为据，时史学废绝，其误多矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1318219_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1283&endYear=1284')">1283-1284年</a>　居家。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1285&endYear=1285')">1285年2月</a>　梦前宰辅。以太学所上书作跋语，寤而识之以诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1286&endYear=1286')">1286年正月</a>　著《践阼篇集解》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1286&endYear=1286')">1286年</a>　孔昭孙为庆元儒学正，以通家子执疑证讹，请益于门。时教授某恣睢自负，语侵先生。昭孙愤然疏其谬诞数十事，鸣于宪府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1287&endYear=1287')">1287年4月</a>　为广平书院作记，称颂舒文靖治学之道。作品：舒文靖先生璘广平书院记。<div id='poem_1318233' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318233' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318233?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广平书院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1287年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318233")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318233_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318233'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318233'>乾道、淳熙间，正学大明，朱子在建，张子在潭，吕子在婺，陆子在抚，学者宗之，如日月江汉，光润所被，皆为名儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318233_comment'></div>于是明有四先生，其一曰广平先生文靖舒公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318233_comment'></div>先生之学讲于张而成于陆，考德问业于朱、吕，心融神会，精知力践，其躬行有尚絅之实，其诲人有时雨之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318233_comment'></div>沈、杨、袁三先生道同志合，化东海之滨为洙泗，位不配德而教行于乡，声闻于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318233_comment'></div>淳祐中贲以易名，先生有孙泌明经世其学，与计偕，上春官，屡不偶，晚始对策集英，典教象山县庠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318233_comment'></div>德祐初元请于郡太守，谓年七十有一，愿挂衣冠，归老故里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318233_comment'></div>留置阃幕，不就，退而抽楹书，启迪后昆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318233_comment'></div>惟昔先生尝题户丹曰广平书塾，游于斯，讲于斯，群叟聚辨于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318233_comment'></div>先生殁，门人敬事不怠，肖像祠于塾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318233_comment'></div>乃遹追先志，奂饰堂序，帅子若孙暨宗族之秀，朝益暮习，春秋舍菜先圣，岁时朔望谒祠，齿拜讲说，冠履翼如，弦诵蔼如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318233_comment'></div>某闻而叹曰：古道庶几复兴乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318233_comment'></div>古者士有常心，家无殊俗，八岁入小学，十年就外傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318233_comment'></div>二十五家为闾，闾有左右塾，里中之老有道德者为左右师，坐两塾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318233_comment'></div>洒扫应对是谨，诗书礼乐是习，孝弟忠信是修，蒙养豫教，薰陶涵濡，是以人有士君子之行，士之子常为士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318233_comment'></div>汉唐之盛，流风犹存，经生守家法，世族重宗谱，子弟彬彬多贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318233_comment'></div>然金籯之谚，城南之劝，识者谓诱以利禄，非天爵之贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318233_comment'></div>惟我国朝师道之立，上接邹鲁，冢宰所降之德，司徒所教之伦，父兄训诏必是焉先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318233_comment'></div>其修于家者若睢阳戚氏，子孙世德之久，南丰曾氏称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318233_comment'></div>若墨庄刘氏，自太宗时至中兴，忠孝雍睦之风不坠，朱子纂次其家传，概举一二言之，可为士族法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318233_comment'></div>今文靖之孙亦服祖训不违，若稽家有塾之谊，绍衣德言，弗佚前人光，用淑艾于家庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318233_comment'></div>我有乔木，殖德培之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318233_comment'></div>我有嘉苗，种学楙之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318233_comment'></div>侁侁胄子，在斯塾也，于墙于羹，如见先哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318233_comment'></div>昏定晨省，入孝出恭，无非教；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318233_comment'></div>受业讲贯，习复计过，无非学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318233_comment'></div>张子序《孟子》说曰：为己者，无所为而然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318233_comment'></div>陆子讲《鲁论》义利之章曰：学者当辨其志，是训是行，服膺勿失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318233_comment'></div>因二先生之言，得文靖之心，百年如一日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318233_comment'></div>国人称曰：文靖之后，世世有人焉，岂惟一家之光，一国之仁逊将自一家始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318233_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「有斐君子，终不可谖兮」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318233_comment'></div>又曰：「维其有章兮，是以有庆兮」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318233_comment'></div>文靖有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318233_comment'></div>子子孙孙弗替引之，后之人其懋哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1318233_comment'></div>遂书以为记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1318233_comment'></div>是岁乙亥夏四月初吉，鄞后学王某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1318233_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1288&endYear=1288')">1288年</a>　居家。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1289&endYear=1289')">1289年</a>　台州胡元叙创建宁海赤城先生罗德业祠，作记。作品：赤城书堂记。<div id='poem_1318244' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318244' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318244?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赤城书堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1289年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318244")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318244_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318244'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318244'>台之宁海，其先贤曰赤城先生罗公，德业为元祐名臣，道义为一乡师表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318244_comment'></div>教思无穷，踰二百年，清风肃然，闻者兴起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318244_comment'></div>旧祠于学，犹未特祀，邑之宿儒前进士胡君元叔倡率乡人，仿古闾塾之制，即公游息之地创为书堂，合乡之俊秀子弟而淑艾之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318244_comment'></div>诹诸乡评，延笃学多闻之彦、前进士舒君岳祥为之长，前进士孙君钧、赵君孟礼、胡君三省、前太学陈君应嵩、刘君庄孙为之录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318244_comment'></div>训之以孝弟敬逊，其规约如蓝田、丽泽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318244_comment'></div>而稽经订史，种学积文，以为有用之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318244_comment'></div>衿佩济济，弦诵洋洋，邹鲁之风蔼如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318244_comment'></div>某闻而叹曰：美哉，教学之意乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318244_comment'></div>古者立教始于乡，仕焉而已者归教闾里，谓之乡先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318244_comment'></div>上老、庶老朝夕坐于塾，是为左右师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318244_comment'></div>入而事亲从兄，出而诵诗读书，小而洒扫应对，大而明德新民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318244_comment'></div>上帝之衷，蒸民之彝，师徒所教之伦，冢宰所降之德，少而习焉，不见异物而迁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318244_comment'></div>是以礼义兴，风俗淳，成人小子皆士君子之行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318244_comment'></div>昔有正素戚先生，讲道睢阳，始建学舍，文忠富公、文正范公皆游习于斯，为一世伟人，家法之粹，延及后昆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318244_comment'></div>正素子孙若维、纶，若舜宾、舜臣，世学相承，睢阳遂为四书院之冠，简策有光焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318244_comment'></div>今宁海耆德鸿生，咸克宪慕前哲，启迪后进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318244_comment'></div>俾之尊德性，求放心，以进于诚明，养其原而即理以应事，孝弟忠信培其根，而馀力以学，师道立，善人多，庶几见睢阳之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318244_comment'></div>《诗》云「有斐君子，终不可谖兮」，罗公有焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318244_comment'></div>「高山仰止，景行行止」，学子其懋哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318244_comment'></div>某病耄不能文，然居相迩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318244_comment'></div>他日海濒为沂泗，门人若安定，孝友睦姻任恤如成周之时，家稷契而户曾闵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318244_comment'></div>行其野则冀缺之耨、茅容之耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318244_comment'></div>攸介攸止，日多髦士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318244_comment'></div>推家之教为天下法，将自兹始，故乐为之书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1318244_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a>　城中握兰桥旁民家穿土得志石一片，作诗纪之。作品：唐开成年墓誌石。<div id='poem_71652' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_71652' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/71652?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐开成年墓志石</a><span class='authorDate'>（1290年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_71652")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_71652_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_71652'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_71652'>鸿濛肇开辟，变嬗几成毁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_71652'>寥寥断竹歌，瓦堲溯姚姒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_71652'>周坟典以族，讵认青乌子。<div id='poem_sentence_2_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_71652'>公琴记咎繇，邢山称东里。<div id='poem_sentence_3_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_71652'>葛淯失之矫，璠玙过于侈。<div id='poem_sentence_4_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_71652'>焉知宫夹墓，莫识龟言水。<div id='poem_sentence_5_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_71652'>铜槃字十六，铭自比于始。<div id='poem_sentence_6_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_71652'>延陵有孔篆，乌宁半辞止。<div id='poem_sentence_7_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_71652'>汉砖犹简朴，石章寖华靡。<div id='poem_sentence_8_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_71652'>无愧惟有道，媚俗多虚美。<div id='poem_sentence_9_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_71652'>七松谈士良，何以惩不轨。<div id='poem_sentence_10_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_71652'>载笔鲜南董，袭浮谬臧否。<div id='poem_sentence_11_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_71652'>岂悟冢中人，三百年不死。<div id='poem_sentence_12_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_71652'>妇名弗出阃，古未有碑诔。<div id='poem_sentence_13_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_71652'>谥见春秋初，志起典午氏。<div id='poem_sentence_14_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_71652'>簪蒿隐士妻，芳刻垂千祀。<div id='poem_sentence_15_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_71652'>杨高托不朽，习之文中理。<div id='poem_sentence_16_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_71652'>或犯葵丘禁，息国事何耻。<div id='poem_sentence_17_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_71652'>蛾眉为黄土，磨灭更谁纪。<div id='poem_sentence_18_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_71652'>宰如比何人，维邑之士女。<div id='poem_sentence_19_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_71652'>逸民孺仲裔，冰雪濯纨绮。<div id='poem_sentence_20_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_71652'>采俪古鄞州，俭勤终莫齿。<div id='poem_sentence_21_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_71652'>试问几何年，颇与铜人似。<div id='poem_sentence_22_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_71652'>虽微黄绢辞，亦质而不俚。<div id='poem_sentence_23_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_71652'>丘夷池又平，蓬颗今廛市。<div id='poem_sentence_24_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_71652'>聚庐寒劫灰，馀光辉泥滓。<div id='poem_sentence_25_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_71652'>曰德巢由俦，闺曰莱鸿比。<div id='poem_sentence_26_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_71652'>我行松柏下，势荣朝菌尔。<div id='poem_sentence_27_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_71652'>隆碣牛砺角，翁仲卧荆杞。<div id='poem_sentence_28_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_71652'>兰艾均一尘，玉珉同一燬。<div id='poem_sentence_29_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_71652'>孤竹梦泡然，柳下垄孰是。<div id='poem_sentence_30_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_71652'>片石幸有传，诗以贻彤史<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_31_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_71652'></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_71652_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_71652'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_31_71652_0'>⑴ 以上宋陈思《两宋名贤小集》卷三七八《王尚书遗集》</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_71652_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1290&endYear=1290')">1290年</a>　奉化令丁济重修社稷坛，作记。作品：奉化社稷坛记。<div id='poem_1318235' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318235' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318235?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉化社稷坛记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1290年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318235")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318235_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318235'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318235'>奉化社稷坛旧在县南，令秦辨之徙置西南三百步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318235_comment'></div>其后圮而复修，迨今百三十馀年，垓壝弗饬，鞠为荆榛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318235_comment'></div>邑剧事繁，自钱谷狱讼谓之不急，旧仪空存，嘉气湮郁，旱潦札瘥，民罔克乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318235_comment'></div>至元二十六年冬，襄贲丁侯济为尹，寅念民人社稷之寄，自古逌重，敢不祗肃，稽经诹礼，规制一新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318235_comment'></div>社东稷西，崇广如式，风雨雷师，鼎列其次，圭石有严，植木有仪，奠瘗之位、斋祓之庐，毖祠揭虔，勿替敬典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318235_comment'></div>明年正月告成，乃率僚寀，洁牲醴，为民迓续丰年之贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318235_comment'></div>雨旸时若，穑人成功，咸曰耿耿祉哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318235_comment'></div>于是耆老畯民属应麟为记以识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318235_comment'></div>某耄矣无能，然俎豆之事尝闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318235_comment'></div>窃惟祀典行乎郡县，惟先圣先师暨社稷，达天下，亘万世，是尊是奉，实为政教之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318235_comment'></div>古循吏之先务，而俗以为缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318235_comment'></div>夫天生时，地生财，莫大乎土谷，而有神司之，后土后稷以妥以侑，明斯礼以治国，其如示诸掌乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318235_comment'></div>风散雨润，箕毕主焉，《周官》之所以槱燎也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318235_comment'></div>鼓以雷霆，庶物生焉，唐礼之所以同坛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318235_comment'></div>是皆天道之至教、神气之流形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318235_comment'></div>春祈秋报，曰民力之普存，三时之不害，亦惟德馨香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318235_comment'></div>祀清心正，躬对越无愧，吉圭荐信，洋洋如在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318235_comment'></div>储休锡羡，燕及黎庶，非知礼之原，其能急流俗之所缓欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318235_comment'></div>盖庸敬在心，斯须之敬在祭本乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318235_comment'></div>地者亲下，幽则有神，令于民最亲，政有否臧，神应如响，神之格思，诚不可掩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318235_comment'></div>昔者古灵陈公宰百里，每过社稷坛、孔子庙，必下而趋，化行习美，兴于礼义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318235_comment'></div>今丁侯治邑三年，师法前猷，庠声序音，弦诵诗书，以淑艾我士子，又能务农重谷，敬恭明神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318235_comment'></div>政教兼善，蔼然学道之遗风，可书也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318235_comment'></div>乃书以遗邑人，俾刻诸丽牲之石，用诏无怠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1318235_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1291&endYear=1291')">1291年冬</a>　肃政廉访副使陈祥分治庆元路，时慕先生名德，屡为造廬式之。时先生闭门不纳客，为之尊礼开说，俾学者师事之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1291&endYear=1291')">1291年</a>　陈祥造船十有四，联贯巨缆。修州治城东东津浮桥，作记。作品：修东津桥记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：《四明文献集》题名作《济南陈公修东津桥记》）</span><div id='poem_1318247' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318247' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318247?labeling=true' target='_blank'>济南陈公修东津桥记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1291年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318247")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318247_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318247'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318247'>四明自唐长庆初迁州治于鄮城东门之外，濒江，民病涉，刺史应彪始建浮桥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318247_comment'></div>有虹景见云表，即其地维舟，随潮汐上下，故桥以灵名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318247_comment'></div>其长为丈五十有五，广寻有六尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318247_comment'></div>宋更名桥曰「东津」，屡圮屡修，郡乘备焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318247_comment'></div>由长庆癸卯迨今四百六十有九载，桥之名虽存，舟漏木朽，铁绳断，竹索腐，行人肩摩趋苇杭以济，迅飙骇浪，瞬息沦为鱼糜，莫或省忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318247_comment'></div>济南陈公祥咨诹民瘼，闻之嗟戚惨怛，若己纳之沟，更旧图新，以身帅之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318247_comment'></div>牧守掾属，协力竞助，士庶风动，不约而从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318247_comment'></div>饬材庀工，治舟易木，鼓铁为纚，楗竹为笮，规制巩壮，民不知劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318247_comment'></div>昔之畏涂，今履康庄，波臣受职，罔有昏垫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318247_comment'></div>漕舻琛舶，凑集城下，夸奓创见，仁人之利溥哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318247_comment'></div>公犹为永久之虑，择民户十有六家，蠲徭役科调，隶局任桥事，未敝而修，费约工省，不止一时之谋，而贻无穷之利，仁心远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318247_comment'></div>邦人䜣䜣，谓惠行政举，郑子产有愧焉，百世之泽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318247_comment'></div>尝读《易》之《中孚》曰「利涉大川，乘木舟虚也」，盖信发于中，诚感于物，上至诚以顺于下，下有孚以从其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318247_comment'></div>惟悦而巽可以化邦，可以济险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318247_comment'></div>公之新斯桥也，其得《中孚》之义乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318247_comment'></div>造舟为梁，岐周肇端；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318247_comment'></div>富平成桥，元凯垂绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318247_comment'></div>曰渭曰河，非有江之险也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318247_comment'></div>江与海接，至险不测，风涛震荡，鲸奔蛟横，是以桥难立而易圮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318247_comment'></div>君子敬保受民命，兴利御患，推恻隐之心，克施有政，作事于始，必将为法于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318247_comment'></div>使继者皆如始作之心，朝计夕思，日葺月缮，用惠我无疆，遗爱在民，与江不竭，若洛阳桥大书深刻，孰曰不宜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318247_comment'></div>乃识其事，俾后人勿坏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1318247_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1292&endYear=1292')">1292年3月</a>　山长曹汉炎倡建书院于慈湖先生杨文元旧宅故址成，作记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1292&endYear=1292')">1292年4月</a>　作观文殿学士史宇之墓志铭。作品：故观文殿学士正奉大夫史宇之墓志铭。<div id='poem_1318280' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318280' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318280?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故观文殿学士正奉大夫史宇之墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1292年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318280")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318280_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318280'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318280'>《诗》、《书》所称世臣之美盛矣，惟宋丰芑涵育之仁逾三百年，父子为相者三家，鄞史氏与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318280_comment'></div>燕及后昆，茀禄昌衍，盖世德之积也厚，而承德用誉，亦在其子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318280_comment'></div>故观文殿学士正奉公，其淳德有常者欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318280_comment'></div>越在内服，靖共厥位；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318280_comment'></div>越在外服，惠政施于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318280_comment'></div>涉世变，守素履，耄耋弗更，其操近古，所谓吉人长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318280_comment'></div>公既葬，前进士黄君翔龙纂次行事，子嘉卿等请著石章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318280_comment'></div>应麟尝执事太史，窃观先朝盛际，上以礼义遇其臣，下以忠厚世其家，于法宜书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318280_comment'></div>瞻彼乔木，岿然故国，纂乃祖、乃考，铭于烝彝鼎，其可使遗老无传？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318280_comment'></div>兹后死者之责，不敢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318280_comment'></div>公讳宇之，字子发，世为明之鄞人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318280_comment'></div>高大父诏，以八行举于乡，赠太师越国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318280_comment'></div>曾大父师仲，赠太师越国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318280_comment'></div>大父浩，相孝宗，为太师、保宁军节度使，封越王，谥忠定，侑享庙廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318280_comment'></div>父弥远，相宁宗、理宗，为太师、保宁昭信军节度使，封卫王，谥忠献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318280_comment'></div>母潘氏，齐鲁国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318280_comment'></div>公忠献季子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318280_comment'></div>粹温端悫，忠献以福艾期之，谓他日亢吾宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318280_comment'></div>初命承事郎，绍定五年中吏部铨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318280_comment'></div>自宝章阁至右文殿修撰，奉佑神祠，除将作少监，赐同进士出身，迁枢密副都承旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318280_comment'></div>忠献薨，服阕，除司农太府少卿、集英殿修撰，仍畀佑神祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318280_comment'></div>即家授沿海制置使参议官，进宝章阁待制，赐金带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318280_comment'></div>升华文阁，知处、严、温三州，皆力辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318280_comment'></div>理宗眷受遗定策之勋，日笃不忘，公兄忠清公宅之既践扬中外，入式枢机，公怡默自持，淡于荣进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318280_comment'></div>上欲试之治民，乃以敷文阁待制守婺，时淳祐八年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318280_comment'></div>婺比岁旱饥，出橐装籴浙右米三万石往赈贷，民罔捐瘠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318280_comment'></div>易守处州，始至，狱多淹系，阅实，上部使者谳决，圜扉一清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318280_comment'></div>赋税三年，民苦之，公倚阁其一年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318280_comment'></div>版部期会苛迫，以己俸代民输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318280_comment'></div>未几督趣如故，公以累年之逋一朝求足，民必重困，奏以三十年最高者为数，疲氓感悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318280_comment'></div>忠清之丧，以在原急难谒告奔赴，得请遂行，耄稚遮道攀留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318280_comment'></div>召为兵部侍郎，辞不拜，进待制宝文阁，提举佑神观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318280_comment'></div>擢工部侍郎，权尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1318280_comment'></div>愿就散秩，陟宝章阁学士，提举万寿观，奉朝请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1318280_comment'></div>宝祐二年，召为兵部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1318280_comment'></div>以焕章阁学士知绍兴府、浙东安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1318280_comment'></div>惟祖惟兄，遗爱在越，公来镇棠阴，耆老驩迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1318280_comment'></div>念绍先哲，壹以宽和，抚柔此民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1318280_comment'></div>初，忠定作牧，创义田，为士大夫贤而贫者丧嫁之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1318280_comment'></div>岁久实惠不沾，至是柅弊栉蠹，始复旧规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1318280_comment'></div>越为南阳乡，公宽而有制，无所回挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1318280_comment'></div>郡大阅，一夫径造厅事，乃卒伍怙王邸势者，公曰：「犯阶级有常刑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1318280_comment'></div>执而黥流之，军民慑服，咸曰仁者之勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1318280_comment'></div>甫期，治最转闻，玺书褒美，升徽猷阁学士，因任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1318280_comment'></div>寻除工部尚书，五年进长兵部，兼工部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1318280_comment'></div>宗祀明堂，为桥道顿递使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1318280_comment'></div>礼成，拜端明殿学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1318280_comment'></div>时畀执政恩数，恳避至再，御章批答曰：「卿继忠孝，谨牧养，予维宠嘉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1318280_comment'></div>祖孙父子昆弟先后列政涂，惟吕氏暨卿门，式克钦承，以为邦家光」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1318280_comment'></div>景定二年，进资政殿大学士、知建宁府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1318280_comment'></div>承叶公梦鼎、陈公昉之后，廉明勤俭，遵其成规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1318280_comment'></div>南方多岚雾，日高乃视事，公常夙兴见吏民，不以素贵少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1318280_comment'></div>夏潦，崇安松溪水汎滥，民惩壬子灾厄，携扶入郛，公盛服露祷，为民请命，移时澄霁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1318280_comment'></div>桥梁岌焉几坠，民凛凛沈垫，亟募舟筏拯之，有阻渡剽攘者罚无贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1318280_comment'></div>黎明水退，民以更生胥庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1318280_comment'></div>建俗禨鬼，恶少身殉淫祠，愚氓神事之，公捕为首者正其罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1318280_comment'></div>溪流湍悍，竞渡斗争多覆溺，严为科禁，俗遂革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1318280_comment'></div>阅岁再召，进观文殿学士，提举万寿观，奉朝请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1318280_comment'></div>居生母齐韩国夫人林氏忧，哀毁过礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1318280_comment'></div>咸淳二年终制，以旧职知宁国府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1318280_comment'></div>郡上供米隶淮东、西两饷，俾其属受委输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1318280_comment'></div>淮西使者治建康地，追符尤峻，或转馈江北，跋涉耗失，纲欠数十万计，而郡官兵饩廪常不继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1318280_comment'></div>公控吁于朝，始得专隶淮东，郡以稍纾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1318280_comment'></div>明年祈閒，提举洞霄宫，优游里第垂十载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1318280_comment'></div>自是閟光韬华，若未始有轩冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1318280_comment'></div>晚岁阖门养疾，一榻萧然，人希识其面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1318280_comment'></div>至元三十年，病革却药，遂不起，春二月十三日也，年七十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1318280_comment'></div>阶自初命至正奉大夫，爵自鄞县开国至奉化郡公，食邑四千六百，实封户六百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1318280_comment'></div>娶洪氏，再娶高平郡主赵氏，皆先卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1318280_comment'></div>子男五：吉卿，承议郎，太府寺丞，知武冈军，先一年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1318280_comment'></div>沂卿，承事郎，为兄待制后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1318280_comment'></div>嘉卿、彭卿，命承事郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1318280_comment'></div>韦卿幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1318280_comment'></div>女子六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1318280_comment'></div>孙男六：辰孙、观孙、景孙、庆孙、增孙、满孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1318280_comment'></div>孙女四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1318280_comment'></div>曾孙男一，公颐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1318280_comment'></div>曾孙女二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1318280_comment'></div>是年四月丁酉，葬于鄞县阳堂乡金岙，与高平合兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1318280_comment'></div>公性孝友，敬保先绪，粥粥如弗胜，佩训言罔敢坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1318280_comment'></div>忠献冢木已拱，隧碑未立，论撰先德，属吴公渊状其行，进彻乙览，理宗用至道、熙宁铭两忠献故事，亲制文，题其额曰「公忠翊运定策元勋之碑」，奎藻汉章，贲耀松槚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1318280_comment'></div>孝子扬父之美，公有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1318280_comment'></div>别墅在钱唐西湖，密迩枋臣私第，欲得之，怵以荣利，公以先人旧业，终不与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1318280_comment'></div>姊适故户部侍郎赵公汝梅，早卒，窆奉化，邻山有讼，公割田易之，争者遂息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1318280_comment'></div>乐善不倦，故家流风犹存，名誉以谦，亦允蹈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1318280_comment'></div>处乡党恂恂，似不能言，与人交，臧否不出诸口，而胸中有泾渭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1318280_comment'></div>自奉菲薄，服用如臞儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1318280_comment'></div>治五郡，护根本，缓茧丝，虽无赫赫名，一念爱民，隐然膏泽之润，纯终领闻，集享备福，克对前人光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1318280_comment'></div>于戏贤哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1318280_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_89_1318280'>史以官氏，相肇于唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1318280_comment'></div>迨宋昌大，台衮相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1318280_comment'></div>有若甘盘，有若伊陟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1318280_comment'></div>奕叶钧衡，太常纪绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1318280_comment'></div>象贤维公，胙乃旧勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1318280_comment'></div>用彰厥善，不专为恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1318280_comment'></div>佩玉徐趋，翔于常伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1318280_comment'></div>处贵无骄，在丰能约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1318280_comment'></div>迪简眷知，职联辅臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1318280_comment'></div>素有世旧，岂伊异人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1318280_comment'></div>公拜稽首，对扬明命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1318280_comment'></div>绍闻衣言，秉心无竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1318280_comment'></div>始政于婺，终政于宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1318280_comment'></div>振乏平赋，民瘼以蠲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1318280_comment'></div>禹会价藩，维祖赐履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1318280_comment'></div>憩棠勿剪，二季涖止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1318280_comment'></div>爱民厚俗，汉吏之循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1318280_comment'></div>安静悃愊，善不近名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1318280_comment'></div>岩居川观，殊庭燕佚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1318280_comment'></div>仁者之寿，秀眉华发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1318280_comment'></div>时行则止，脱屣浮云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1318280_comment'></div>一其初终，驹皎鸿冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1318280_comment'></div>嗣守维艰，前修所叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1318280_comment'></div>允矣君子，归飞无憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1318280_comment'></div>曰晋遗老，曰殷故家，胡不百年，乡闾之嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1318280_comment'></div>古碣苍苍，视此铭诔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1318280_comment'></div>忠定之孙，忠献之子。</div><div id='poem_sentence_115_1318280_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1292&endYear=1292')">1292年8月</a>　丁济重修奉化县治成，作记。作品：奉化县重修县治记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：《四明文献集》题名作《奉化重修县治记》）</span><div id='poem_1318242' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318242' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318242?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉化重修县治记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1292年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318242")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318242_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318242'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318242'>越之东境为鄞，汉属会稽，唐合鄞于鄮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318242_comment'></div>开元中州以四明山名，始建县曰奉化，其地则汉之鄞也，古鄞城在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318242_comment'></div>鄞有大里黄公，列于四皓，卓乎千载人物之冠冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318242_comment'></div>先贤风流所被，其俗纯如，其士邠如，在《九域志》是谓望县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318242_comment'></div>迪简墨绶，长吏保绥受命民，非才足以拨烦、廉足以砥俗、仁足以摩拊疲瘵，不轻以百里畀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318242_comment'></div>县治燬于丙子，师旅饥馑相仍，遗黎蒿焉困悴，令长迫期会，急茧丝，虑弗及远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318242_comment'></div>王君宗信仅克创听事三楹，李尹天益才缮吏舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318242_comment'></div>襄贲丁君济宰兹邑，惟武城之室、单父之堂所以疏视瀹听，清应物之原，若昔董安于治晋阳，一墙一柱犹不茍，匪贲轮奂以为华，壮栋宇以自奉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318242_comment'></div>爰契我龟，经之营之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318242_comment'></div>任城王君泽为丞，比善协志，而新是谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318242_comment'></div>邑士大夫咸劝趋之，庶工丕作，民不知劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318242_comment'></div>始事辛卯之冬，考成壬辰之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318242_comment'></div>丁君以书曰：「一日必葺，古有明训；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318242_comment'></div>百堵皆兴，诗人咏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318242_comment'></div>听事东西吾名以『节爱』、『清安』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318242_comment'></div>两庑翼焉，吾名以『一清』、『四畏』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318242_comment'></div>堂曰『得物』，以息以燕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318242_comment'></div>亭曰『清斯』，有沼有荷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318242_comment'></div>挹爽西山，扁以高清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318242_comment'></div>殖殖其楹，䡾䡾其门，胥吏攸处，下逮圜扉，粲然一新，曷敢视官舍如遽传而怠厥事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318242_comment'></div>愿谂后之人，俾勿坏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318242_comment'></div>余病髦不能文，尝谓君子为政，其本自相在尔室始，千室之邑易治也，一室之自治为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318242_comment'></div>子程子之视民如伤，子张子之训民善俗，以一邑为天下之式，其本焉在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318242_comment'></div>惟暗室之不欺而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318242_comment'></div>岩谷深窈，欲其疾痛必闻，如接几席；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318242_comment'></div>胥徒嚣悍，欲其隐微必察，如在户庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318242_comment'></div>堂上之一笑嚬，堂下之万休戚系焉，若保赤子，心诚求之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318242_comment'></div>推是心达于政，蒲、密、中牟之化可复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318242_comment'></div>《诗》曰「无已太康，职思其居」，然则居此室可不敬欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318242_comment'></div>闻丁君律己首公，爱民来吏，日涖庠序，惠训不倦，多士䜣䜣，诵子产之诲我弟子，是能知本矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318242_comment'></div>耆寿俊民相与言曰：「兹不可不书」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318242_comment'></div>乃不敢固辞，书其事诒永久，用勉夫字民者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318242_comment'></div>至元二十九年八月，前进士王应麟记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1318242_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1292&endYear=1292')">1292年9月</a>　庆元路肃政廉访使陈祥重建儒学成，作记。作品：庆元路重建儒学记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：《四明文献集》题名作《重修县儒学记》）</span><div id='poem_1318231' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318231' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318231?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庆元路重建儒学记<span class='inlineComment2'>（此乃尊经阁记）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1292年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318231")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318231_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318231'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318231'>四明自唐为州，始有夫子庙，宋始建学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318231_comment'></div>规模丰敞，栋宇穹崇，庠声序音，冠于浙左，英俊之域，绂冕所兴，文献盖彬彬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318231_comment'></div>至元十九年春，学燬于融风，教授潘梦桂、黄裳、吴宗彦、史复伯历载缮葺经始，礼殿门庑斋舍寖以略具，讲经有席，养蒙有堂，皆草创未就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318231_comment'></div>二十八年冬，肃政廉访副使陈公祥下车，谓博士、诸生曰：「化民成俗，劝学为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318231_comment'></div>尝闻畴昔轮奂之盛，意不止是，曷饬工抡材，以复旧观」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318231_comment'></div>顾仪门卑隘弗称，从事容服弗严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318231_comment'></div>越明年夏，鼎新高闳，贲饰貌像，六旬而毕，二堂亦告成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318231_comment'></div>又惟斯文与天地并，必华榱岑楼，式毖厥藏，因重建尊经阁五楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318231_comment'></div>里士䜣然竞助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318231_comment'></div>教授苏君焱撙约学廪，续其不给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318231_comment'></div>同知府事阮公麟翁提其纲，庶工丕作，居不知劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318231_comment'></div>幕掾韩君居仁叶画展勤，不愆于素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318231_comment'></div>秋九月阁成，嶪峨壮伟，衿佩耸瞻，咸曰：「六经如日月，陟降庭止，惠我光明，恢人文以迪化原，维贤使者之德」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318231_comment'></div>且将以旧门及堂更立先贤祠，正录序，缭以垣墉，制度于焉大备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318231_comment'></div>苏君请识成事于石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318231_comment'></div>某耄不能文，惟诸侯之学载于礼详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318231_comment'></div>在《易·临》之象曰：「君子以教思无穷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318231_comment'></div>泽上有地，犹君子之近民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318231_comment'></div>近民则礼达而教行，建其牧，立其监，有师保之义，凡以存天理，正人心而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318231_comment'></div>矧是邦为诗书之乡，逸民之黄，纯孝之董，文士之任，自汉以来为美谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318231_comment'></div>庆历诸老，模范后进，淳熙大儒，阐明正学，惟圣贤是式，惟德性是尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318231_comment'></div>少而洒扫应对，大而格物致知，耳濡目染，充然有得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318231_comment'></div>每岁孟春，衣冠济济，齿位秩秩，司徒之教伦，党正之礼饮，流风遗泽，于今未坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318231_comment'></div>南丰曾公、忠肃陈公继为守贰，表率薰陶，东诸侯莫逮焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318231_comment'></div>《春秋》大复，古学之复，道之泰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318231_comment'></div>夫不农不工，何以谓之士？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318231_comment'></div>非老非释，何以谓之儒？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318231_comment'></div>行己有耻，尚志仁义，士之实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318231_comment'></div>为君子儒，夙夜强学以待问，儒之实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318231_comment'></div>游于斯，肄于斯，盖亦践其实、副其名乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318231_comment'></div>郡国有学昉于汉，二千石所察惟曰好文学，敬长上，肃政教，顺乡曲，三代考行之意蔼如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318231_comment'></div>升堂闻金石之音，入宫墙见宗庙之美，因作新之几而日新其德业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318231_comment'></div>孝弟忠信为根本，明诚敬义为准的。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1318231_comment'></div>始于离经辨志，终于知类通达，用仰承《菁莪》乐育之仁，不在兹时欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1318231_comment'></div>昔鲁僖公能修泮宫，教泽浃于海邦，其俗秉周礼，守经学，一变至道，圣人称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1318231_comment'></div>谁谓鲁远，道无古今，师友渊源，绪接洙泗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1318231_comment'></div>颂其诗，尚论古之人，罔俾克广德心，专美鲁之多士，凡我同志懋敬哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1318231_comment'></div>欧阳子有言：善教者以不倦之意，须迟久之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1318231_comment'></div>礼行俗淳，然后为学之成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1318231_comment'></div>是用记其始成，以诏永久，俾无怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1318231_comment'></div>是岁冬十月己亥，前进士王某记<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1318231_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1318231'>学：原脱，据四库本、清抄本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1318231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1318231'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_40_1318231_0'>⑴ 《四明文献集》卷一。又见《延祐四明志》卷一三，《敬止录》卷一五，《四明文献录》，成化《宁波郡志》卷六。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1318231_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1292&endYear=1292')">1292年9月</a>　陈祥建医学成，作记。作品：庆元路建医学记。<div id='poem_1318239' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318239' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318239?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庆元路建医学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1292年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318239")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318239_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318239'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318239'>医之兴也，其于上古乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318239_comment'></div>巫彭初作医，曷为本于三皇？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318239_comment'></div>古三坟书倚相后无闻，《易》以筮传，《本草》、《内经》以医传，天之牖民至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318239_comment'></div>《本草》、《内经》，医之原也，《易》何与于医？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318239_comment'></div>坎离阴阳，《参同》、《纳甲》发其缊，养生者宗焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318239_comment'></div>是以言医必曰羲、农、黄帝云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318239_comment'></div>成周医有师，江左元嘉昉建学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318239_comment'></div>唐州郡有学，助教掌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318239_comment'></div>宋崇观间置学京师，在外附职侯頖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318239_comment'></div>自古昔方技为王官之一守，今朝廷崇奖蠲复，悉与儒等，诸路设校立师教育之，将跻斯民寿域，德至渥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318239_comment'></div>惟四明学犹阙，至元二十八年冬，肃政廉访副使陈公祥揽辔来临，察民嚬呻，尤以医为重，顾讲习无所，喟然思作新兴起之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318239_comment'></div>相攸胥宇，鸠工经始，毖祀三皇，礼仪肃，堂宇门庑奂奕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318239_comment'></div>学成，属予以记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318239_comment'></div>余闻之前修，医之为道推本五行六气、寒暑日星，考验风土山川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318239_comment'></div>其于人也，骨节经络、揲荒腧穴，内则藏府焦鬲井谷，精微奥妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318239_comment'></div>虽国工高手弗能究，岂庸夫俗子可与知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318239_comment'></div>世不轻试而茍得者鲜矣，此学医者人费，可不谨乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318239_comment'></div>是故医不可无学，岐伯之师曰僦贷、季泰，越人之师曰长桑君，太仓公之师曰公孙光、阳庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318239_comment'></div>盖下学可以言传，上达必由心悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318239_comment'></div>诵言未明于心，读古人之糟魄，斲轮犹议之，矧寿夭生死所系乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318239_comment'></div>然则学孰为要，一言蔽之曰仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318239_comment'></div>程子谓「医书以痿痹为不仁，最善名状仁者」，又云「切脉可观仁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318239_comment'></div>仁，人心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318239_comment'></div>天地生生之心，人得之以为心，心仁则疾痛切身，若保赤子，万物一体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318239_comment'></div>不仁则善不胜利，理汩于欲，肝胆楚越也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318239_comment'></div>陟降庭止，前圣临之在上，以仁存心，以心合天，如涪翁之不求报，宋清之不为市，庞安常之好施，许叔微之阴功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318239_comment'></div>精义入神，将得不传之妙于筌蹄之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318239_comment'></div>惟贯道器德艺于一致者可以语此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318239_comment'></div>其或专己臆决，乃曰医者意也，是犹废学古入官之训，而曰何必读书，其害不止误注《本草》而已，殆非敩学师古之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318239_comment'></div>虽然，余言耄矣，傥以为然，愿以为学者之箴石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318239_comment'></div>是岁九月旦日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1318239_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1293&endYear=1293')">1293年8月</a>　陈祥建鄞县儒学成，壬寅，作记。作品：鄞县重建儒学记。<div id='poem_1318238' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318238' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318238?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重修鄞县儒学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1293年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318238")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318238_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318238'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318238'>鄞在汉为鄮，属会稽郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318238_comment'></div>唐属明州，建夫子庙于县东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318238_comment'></div>五代改鄮为鄞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318238_comment'></div>宋始立学，王文公宰县，因庙为学，教养县之子弟，风以诗书，衣冠鼎盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318238_comment'></div>后迁县西南，兵燬久未复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318238_comment'></div>主簿吕康年请于郡，相旧址，创礼殿，设跪像，堂曰「养正」，为斋者四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318238_comment'></div>至元十九年增二斋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318238_comment'></div>二十六年郡城灾，兹学岿若鲁灵光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318238_comment'></div>斯文未坠，道其泰乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318238_comment'></div>二十八年，济南陈公祥为肃政廉访副使，分治于明，崇庠序之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318238_comment'></div>明年，新郡学，顾邑校风摧雨圮，榱槛将压，殿虽更，坐像庳陋，未合古制，爰命撤旧宇而新是图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318238_comment'></div>夏六月，鸠工经始，规模崇闳，视昔增焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318238_comment'></div>县尹张君孝安提其纲，丞王君闰捐禄米以助，主簿任君谦亦赞画焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318238_comment'></div>多士竞劝，佐厥费，事钜用不给，檄县以义役租续之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318238_comment'></div>揭石为门，六扇有伉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318238_comment'></div>抡材为殿，隆栋翚飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318238_comment'></div>清池泱泱，芹藻春意，自堂及序，以次缮修，实惟礼乐之使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318238_comment'></div>居德善俗，启迪化原，以恢宫墙之壮观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318238_comment'></div>逢掖来游，诵公教泽，永永无斁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318238_comment'></div>始，教谕赵必燮庀役，未克就，严得桂继之，出私橐帅先，吴应酉联事协力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318238_comment'></div>既成，请识石章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318238_comment'></div>应麟居是邦，不敢以髦疾辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318238_comment'></div>惟古者百里有师，教以道艺孝弟仁义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318238_comment'></div>斯民也三代所与共学也，闾为左右塾，党以正齿位，时会于州序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318238_comment'></div>去民愈近，施教愈密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318238_comment'></div>自武城弦歌弗闻，急茧丝而缓教化，先政刑而后诗书，若密令举善而教，新城长延聚生徒，何其寂寥哉，无以表倡之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318238_comment'></div>我思古人有行部先即学宫见诸生试论，有行县学宫，处士执经对讲，谁其嗣之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318238_comment'></div>贤使者新斯学也，岂徒美宫室云尔，将新士以新民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318238_comment'></div>昔鄞有杜先生醇，学行望一乡，县大夫再书然后起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318238_comment'></div>其书谓「斯道我先得之，必推馀于古人，愿赐临以为之师」，其自重难致如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318238_comment'></div>师道立，善人多，渊源有自，为师者盍以为法乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318238_comment'></div>鄮士《汉书》仅一见，虞仲翔之言可考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318238_comment'></div>陆士龙称鄮之俗礼节恭谨，盖素履行愿，修其天爵，是为入德之基、进道之阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1318238_comment'></div>自学校之建，俊乂兴起，乡先生前后九人，其四出于鄞，皆以忠信为本，践履为实，仰高蹈景，其人若存，为士者不自勉乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1318238_comment'></div>师知所以教，士知所以学，朝而受业，昼而讲贯，夕而复习，思无愧于儒之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1318238_comment'></div>前哲有云：学所以学为人，学为君子，学为忠与孝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1318238_comment'></div>服膺三言，是训是行，化海濒为洙泗，以一邑为天下式，将自吾鄞始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1318238_comment'></div>谨书其事，诒夫敩学者，式克用劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1318238_comment'></div>三十年秋八月壬寅记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1318238_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1293&endYear=1293')">1293年</a>　重录《四明七观》旧稿，跋藏于箧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1294&endYear=1294')">1294年12月丙子</a>　狄桂属部博士戴友复九先生祠祀。甲午，作记。作品：先贤祠祀堂记。<div id='poem_1318234' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318234' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318234?labeling=true' target='_blank'>先贤祠堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1294年12月丙子）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318234")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318234_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318234'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318234'>古之有道德者教于乡里，谓之乡先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318234_comment'></div>在乡而祠于学，犹在国之祭于瞽宗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318234_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「有斐君子，终不可谖兮」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318234_comment'></div>《大学》以为盛德至善，民之不能忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318234_comment'></div>秉彝好德之良心，千载一日，况其迩者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318234_comment'></div>明自唐为州，文风寥寥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318234_comment'></div>宋庆历中始诏州县立学，山林特起之士卓然为一乡师表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318234_comment'></div>或受业乡校，或讲道闾塾，本之以孝弟忠信，维之以礼义廉耻，守古训而不凿，修天爵而无竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318234_comment'></div>养成英才，纯明笃厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318234_comment'></div>父兄师友，诏教琢磨，百年文献，益盛以大，五先生之功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318234_comment'></div>淳熙大儒疏涧瀍之源而达之洙泗，是邦诸老之学始得江西之传，而考德问业于朱、吕、张子之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318234_comment'></div>以尊德性、求放心为根本，以颜、曾四勿三省为准的，阐绎经训，躬行践履，致严于进退行藏之际，致察于善利理欲之几，明诚笃恭，俯仰无所愧怍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318234_comment'></div>学者知操存持养以入圣贤之域，四先生之功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318234_comment'></div>前后九贤，教行于一时，泽被于百世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318234_comment'></div>郡学有祠旧矣，因郁攸而废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318234_comment'></div>至元甲午冬十一月，洛阳狄公桂持廉问之节，行部至明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318234_comment'></div>既即庠序见诸生，思所以启迪斯文，俾多士知所矜式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318234_comment'></div>有言坠典之未举，公喟然曰：「兹立教善俗之原，其可缓」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318234_comment'></div>乃属郡博士戴君友复旧毖祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318234_comment'></div>十二月丙子朔，公率守贰寮寀，是妥是奉，以风厉士子丕远，惟耇老成人，宅心知训，庶几绍闻衣德言，人有士君子之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318234_comment'></div>衿佩竦瞻，莫不忻忻曰：「善教得民心，明使君有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318234_comment'></div>是祠之复，其作新士习之机欤」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318234_comment'></div>觉有先后，道无古今，高山仰止，景行行止，非徒慕之，亦允蹈之，将有闻风兴起者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318234_comment'></div>惟昔沛、三辅有《耆旧》《节士序》，鲁、庐江有《名德》《先贤赞》，并采摭旧闻，述为小传，事有据依，词无溢美，用谂乡之善士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318234_comment'></div>尚式时先哲之猷训，永永无斁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318234_comment'></div>是月甲午，后学王某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1318234_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1294&endYear=1294')">1294年</a>　狄桂属部博士戴友复九先生祠祀。甲午，作传。作品：九先生传。<div id='poem_1318243' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318243' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318243?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九先生祠堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1294年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318243")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318243_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318243'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318243'>古之乡先生祭于社，近世祠于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318243_comment'></div>社所以养，学所以教，而教之功尤大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318243_comment'></div>秉彝好学之良心，百世犹旦暮，况其迩者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318243_comment'></div>诵其诗，读其书，尚友古之人，非一乡之望也，天下之望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318243_comment'></div>四明乡先生有九人焉：宋庆历建学之初，杨、杜、二王、楼公以道德文行师表后进，或授业乡校，或讲道闾塾，衣冠文献，益盛以大，五先生之功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318243_comment'></div>淳熙之舒、沈、杨、袁诸公，以尊德性求放心为根本，阐绎经训，躬行实践，学者知操存持养以入圣贤之域，四先生之功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318243_comment'></div>郡泮旧有祠，因郁攸而废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318243_comment'></div>至元甲午季冬朔旦，廉访使者秋公桂属郡博士戴君友始复毖祀，观者兴起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318243_comment'></div>元贞丙申月正元日，廉访使者完颜公贞至学宫，谓祠宇狭陋未称，相攸尊经阁之右，规模一新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318243_comment'></div>府牧月列公提其纲，帅属协力庀事，以迄于成，妥侑如礼，多士䜣䜣，周爰咨诹，章善扶教，以谷我子弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318243_comment'></div>惟二使者之赐，亦惟承流宣化之贤，立师道以美风俗，皆宜书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318243_comment'></div>凡我同志，盍亦修孝弟忠信，尚礼义廉耻，学必正大，行必笃敬，式时前哲训，用对作新盛德，可不懋欤！</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1318243_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1294&endYear=1294')">1294年</a>　与舒阆风、刘正仲、陈西麓相倡酬于梅墟陈氏之世纶堂，辑为《世纶堂雅集诗卷》，有洛社耆英之遗意。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1295&endYear=1295')">1295年春</a>　与奉化陈著相见，“相看话旧，耿耿何如，虽不尽言，有不尽意。”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1295&endYear=1295')">1295年4月16日</a>　王应麟为舒集作序，盛赞岳祥大节特立，诗文有本。该序提到岳祥著作有《避地》、《篆畦》、《蝶轩》、《三史纂言》，独不及《阆风集》，知《阆风集》毁于丙子兵火。四库馆臣从《永乐大典》辑出之《阆风集》是岳祥第四子叔献的复刊本，而不是毁于丙子兵火的《阆风集》，故现存于《阆风集》的诗文几乎全是丙子之后所作。作品：阆风集序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1295&endYear=1295')">1295年8月</a>　曾官建宁路松溪县兼劝农司安庶决意修建天兴庙，作记。作品：天兴庙记。<div id='poem_1318245' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318245' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318245?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天兴庙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1295年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318245")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318245_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318245'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318245'>句章汉县也，隋省入鄮，唐以鄮为明州，其后名乡曰句章，镇曰小溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318245_comment'></div>山水清远，地灵旁薄，丞相文节魏公杞、国史吏部安公刘居焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318245_comment'></div>吏部之子松阳主簿庶谓余曰：「镇之土神，自唐迄宋，分派它山，庙食朝阳里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318245_comment'></div>耋老相传，号为天兴，惠我嘉师，祥庆飨答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318245_comment'></div>建炎兵燬，祠宇岿存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318245_comment'></div>嘉熙庚子，札瘥胥渐，乃禬乃禳，若有呵护，家用平康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318245_comment'></div>咸淳甲戌旱暵，苗将槁，吁祷之，翌日云油雨沛，甫田登成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318245_comment'></div>明年盗弄锄梃，津涂梗塞，阖境帖妥，繄神之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318245_comment'></div>其弭灾御患施及邻壤，匪直福一方而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318245_comment'></div>庶先君子率乡士民，控于郡守、部使者，转闻于朝，下仪曹、奉常议，奏赐庙额曰『天兴』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318245_comment'></div>敕牒将颁，而世故纷缊，弗获被成命，然旧绩具在，愿书以诏永久」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318245_comment'></div>余昔者长春官，实与闻斯事，曷敢不诺？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318245_comment'></div>相古先民，有周命祀，达于乡遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318245_comment'></div>水旱之不时，于党鄙乎禜之，而正师涖焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318245_comment'></div>疾疠之弗蠲，于族酂乎酺之，而师长涖焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318245_comment'></div>正辞荐信，义之修而礼之藏，惟以保艾受民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318245_comment'></div>自里社废，乡里缺，越望非鬼之祭，杂糅贯渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318245_comment'></div>是故有功于民则祀之，著于《祭法》，职在秩宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318245_comment'></div>教民祈报，勿替敬典，无从匪彝，无即慆淫，礼之大经也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318245_comment'></div>惟兹有神，式克敷祐天氓，销沴为和，易歉为丰，咸曰耿耿祉哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318245_comment'></div>夫神聪明正直，而壹依人而行，士竞乎教，农力乎穑，修其孝弟忠信，为德馨者愈加肃畏矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1318245_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1296&endYear=1296')">1296年正月</a>　廉访使婉言贞改建九先生祠堂于鄞县尊经阁之右，作记。作品：九先生祠堂记。<div id='poem_1318243' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318243' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318243?labeling=true' target='_blank'>九先生祠堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1294年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318243")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318243_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318243'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318243'>古之乡先生祭于社，近世祠于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318243_comment'></div>社所以养，学所以教，而教之功尤大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318243_comment'></div>秉彝好学之良心，百世犹旦暮，况其迩者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318243_comment'></div>诵其诗，读其书，尚友古之人，非一乡之望也，天下之望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318243_comment'></div>四明乡先生有九人焉：宋庆历建学之初，杨、杜、二王、楼公以道德文行师表后进，或授业乡校，或讲道闾塾，衣冠文献，益盛以大，五先生之功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318243_comment'></div>淳熙之舒、沈、杨、袁诸公，以尊德性求放心为根本，阐绎经训，躬行实践，学者知操存持养以入圣贤之域，四先生之功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318243_comment'></div>郡泮旧有祠，因郁攸而废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318243_comment'></div>至元甲午季冬朔旦，廉访使者秋公桂属郡博士戴君友始复毖祀，观者兴起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318243_comment'></div>元贞丙申月正元日，廉访使者完颜公贞至学宫，谓祠宇狭陋未称，相攸尊经阁之右，规模一新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318243_comment'></div>府牧月列公提其纲，帅属协力庀事，以迄于成，妥侑如礼，多士䜣䜣，周爰咨诹，章善扶教，以谷我子弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318243_comment'></div>惟二使者之赐，亦惟承流宣化之贤，立师道以美风俗，皆宜书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318243_comment'></div>凡我同志，盍亦修孝弟忠信，尚礼义廉耻，学必正大，行必笃敬，式时前哲训，用对作新盛德，可不懋欤！</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1318243_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1296&endYear=1296')">1296年6月12戊申</a>　卒。先期自为墓铭。作品：浚仪遗民自志文。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ceb154563e43425fafca323e549ee081_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ceb154563e43425fafca323e549ee081");'><span id='ceb154563e43425fafca323e549ee081_link'
