href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年</a>　其父性严急，每授题，命应麟坐堂下，在蜡烛上刻时限，如稍慢，就受到训斥，故先生文益敏捷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年4月</a>　史嵩之依前右丞相兼枢密使，父撝乞补外以避，通判婺州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年8月</a>　试国子监，中选。作品：试题为安人天民之福赋、整翮当云霄诗、下逮庄骚太史所录论。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1241&endYear=1241')">1241年2月</a>　别院省记奏名。作品：试题为□道德赋、当春乃发生诗、统纪法度如何□□论。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1241&endYear=1241')">1241年4月</a>　御史台覆试。作品：试题为人君之道无私论。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1241&endYear=1241')">1241年5月</a>　廷试乙科，登徐俨夫榜进士，赐及第出身。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1241&endYear=1241')">1241年6月</a>　闻喜宴，宋理宗赐诗。作品：御制诗。<div id='poem_1318168' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318168' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318168?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代先君谢赐御制周易彻章诗表</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳祐十二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318168")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318168_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318168'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318168'>宝跗掞藻，写羲画之粹精；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318168_comment'></div>翠琰垂芳，备虞廷之赓载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318168_comment'></div>辉腾奎璧，荣被簪绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318168_comment'></div>若稽皇朝，深造《易》学，便殿集乾元之刚健，成均陈泰道之感通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318168_comment'></div>祥符制三章而示儒臣，绍兴书二卦而赐宰辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318168_comment'></div>洪惟上圣，允迪前猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318168_comment'></div>朋来益助之龟，日新其德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318168_comment'></div>惠浃书夏之燕，情见乎词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318168_comment'></div>发阴阳阖辟之关，播日月光华之咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318168_comment'></div>穗书再刻，瑶轴俯颁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318168_comment'></div>恭惟极深研几，精义致用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318168_comment'></div>蓄天在山中之德，学懋缉熙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318168_comment'></div>涣风行水上之文，心潜经纬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318168_comment'></div>圣蕴达忘筌之妙，宸章昭镂玉之传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318168_comment'></div>于赫贲观，敷同晋锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318168_comment'></div>臣胸无色线，袖有骊珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318168_comment'></div>七言属和于柏梁，莫陪俊彦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318168_comment'></div>百咏辑成于离正，徒仰文明。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1318168_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='7d0c3b469f224b79bbe2451ad0ad6202_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7d0c3b469f224b79bbe2451ad0ad6202");'><span id='7d0c3b469f224b79bbe2451ad0ad6202_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1245&endYear=1245')">1245年</a>，23岁</div><div id='7d0c3b469f224b79bbe2451ad0ad6202' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1245&endYear=1245')">1245年</a>　侍父入朝，调官，部使者郑霖用不平常的眼光看待他。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1245&endYear=1245')">1245年秋</a>　为了使寺庙的无量功德和历史流传下去，故书其事于石。作品：广恩崇福寺记。<div id='poem_1318248' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318248' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318248?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广恩崇福寺记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1245年秋）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318248")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318248_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318248'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318248'>浙河以东，山水名天下，四明为最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318248_comment'></div>出四明西门至林村，行六七里，曰桃源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318248_comment'></div>循源而入，虬腾驷奔，气势奇峭，紫岩为最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318248_comment'></div>溪清谷窈，楸槚郁茂，是为太师袁卫公之阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318248_comment'></div>公笃厚好善，用昌大厥家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318248_comment'></div>嗣子尹神京，贰枢庭，相攸紫岩之阳，俶建梵宇，遹承先志，奉大士像而《法华》手泽藏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318248_comment'></div>请于朝，赐名「广恩崇福」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318248_comment'></div>秀概瑰观，甲于诸方，奥殿穹堂，俨然宝地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318248_comment'></div>林霏岚翠，献状几席，松风涧泉，与钟鱼相答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318248_comment'></div>创基鸠役，匠成于心，则住持僧可仁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318248_comment'></div>轮奂之美、田畴之辟，仁皆躬服其劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318248_comment'></div>雅人胜士来游而嘉叹之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318248_comment'></div>惟古者礼貌大臣，推本德善之积，庙祀其祖祢，施于烝尝彝鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318248_comment'></div>近世又即缁庐寓《蓼莪》寒泉之思，于是锡命以宠灵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318248_comment'></div>盖君子谨终追远，无不用其极，而遇大臣之礼亦至矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318248_comment'></div>夫秉彝好德，人之良心，释氏以空寂为教，若外乎伦纪，然其书有《大报恩篇》，言孝与儒合，是故致严致悫而宫室之，以荐苾芬于九原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318248_comment'></div>礼可以义起也，观于斯者爱敬之心油然生矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318248_comment'></div>余谓善必有庆，如殖斯穫，非以徼福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318248_comment'></div>教子以食其报，可谓使为善者劝，一宜书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318248_comment'></div>仰飞云而俯拱木，著存不忘，于以诏万世子孙，勿替引之，二宜书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318248_comment'></div>披坏壤经营，用力勤，刻意专，南丰所为称学佛者将以勉吾儒也，三宜书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318248_comment'></div>寺经始于绍定庚寅之孟秋，越淳祐乙巳季夏考成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318248_comment'></div>是岁之秋，可仁请识岁月，诏永久，遂书其事于石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318248_comment'></div>郡人王应麟记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1318248_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='00b82f0d79454c8f9062d8affa473a11_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1252&endYear=1252')">1252年</a>，30岁</div><div id='00b82f0d79454c8f9062d8affa473a11' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1252&endYear=1252')">1252年4月</a>　差浙西提举常平茶盐司主管。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1252&endYear=1252')">1252年7月</a>　考试临安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1252&endYear=1252')">1252年8月辛巳</a>　诏改明年为宝祐元年，应麟作表。作品：代贺改元宝祐表。<div id='poem_1318164' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318164' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318164?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代贺改元宝祐表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1252年8月辛巳）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318164")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318164_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318164'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318164'>宝龟申命，延洪必世之休；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318164_comment'></div>凤历更元，迓续丕平之运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318164_comment'></div>风雷鼓舞，日月光华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318164_comment'></div>窃以汉武改元朔之名，适当癸亥之岁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318164_comment'></div>孝宣颁地节之诏，越在壬子之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318164_comment'></div>或即旧而鉴新，或惧灾而应变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318164_comment'></div>孰如昭代，稽若先猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318164_comment'></div>恭惟睿知有临，严恭自度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318164_comment'></div>更化善治，三十年政教之清；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318164_comment'></div>燕翼诒谋，亿万年基图之永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318164_comment'></div>眷言岁纪，已浃星终，将顺革以明时，爰体乾而首物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318164_comment'></div>俭慈为宝，永底蒸民之生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318164_comment'></div>保右自天，庶几二祖之烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318164_comment'></div>嘉名有俶，峻命惟凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318164_comment'></div>某幸际泰亨，耸聆孚号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318164_comment'></div>法《春秋》而谨始，敢贡愚忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318164_comment'></div>与士夫而励精，钦承德意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1318164_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='143421343c49485cb78306bbd1a1759d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("143421343c49485cb78306bbd1a1759d");'><span id='143421343c49485cb78306bbd1a1759d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年2月12日</a>　以从事郎、扬州州学教授，试宏词科，第一场，题二首。作品：昭庆军承宣使左金吾卫大将军荆湖北路安抚副使兼知鄂州授宁武军节度使神龙卫四厢都指挥使夔路安抚使兼知夔州兼提领措置屯田兼控扼瀘叙昌合四州边面加食邑食实封制；周山川图记。<div id='poem_1318064' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318064' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318064?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭庆军承宣使左金吾卫大将军荆湖北路安抚副使兼知鄂州授宁武军节度使龙神卫四厢都指挥使夔路安抚使兼知夔州兼提领措置屯田兼控扼泸叙昌合四州边面加食邑食实封制<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年2月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318064")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318064_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1318064_0'>① 词科试中第一场首选宝祐四年丙辰二月十二日</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318064'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318064'>门下：建节旄而启镇，密联厢部之班；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318064_comment'></div>分阃帅以留田，兼饬边城之备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318064_comment'></div>乃眷承流之隽，夙参宅牧之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318064_comment'></div>兵农方急于坤维，表里载更于师律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318064_comment'></div>王言作命，士听无哗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318064_comment'></div>某官沈毅而善谋，忠纯而知义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318064_comment'></div>临机料敌，明四种之兵书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318064_comment'></div>御众牧人，备五材之将略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318064_comment'></div>率先爪士，屡奏肤公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318064_comment'></div>有嘉卫社之勤，寖服执金之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318064_comment'></div>贰荆州之方面，江介肃清；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318064_comment'></div>殿鄂渚之雄藩，民心靖谧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318064_comment'></div>治效已闻于南纪，朕衷尤轸于西陲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318064_comment'></div>念蜀道之孔艰，恃夔门之坚守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318064_comment'></div>远连夷徼，先江阳、僰水之捍防；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318064_comment'></div>近护风寒，谨昌元、巴川之控御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318064_comment'></div>欲整军而经武，必彻土以峙粻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318064_comment'></div>惟尔之能，敌王所忾，是用易苕霅宣风之秩，新葭萌赐节之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318064_comment'></div>十乘以先启行，植中权之牙纛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318064_comment'></div>四邻若防制水，壮列郡之喉襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318064_comment'></div>由副帅以褒升，进上游而绥抚，畀端拱使名之宠，总绍兴穑事之纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318064_comment'></div>虏可胜而奏屯田，亟上便宜之十二；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318064_comment'></div>蛮来威而伐猃狁，往陈师旅之三千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318064_comment'></div>钦哉实亩以实墉，于以维藩而维翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318064_comment'></div>申陪采赋，增贲戎昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318064_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318064_comment'></div>按德裕南道之图，慨想筹边习农之绩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318064_comment'></div>览孔明平沙之阵，毋忘渡泸耕渭之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318064_comment'></div>务本所以省转输，设险所以严保障。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318064_comment'></div>祗若予训，式固尔猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318064_comment'></div>可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318064_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1318064_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318227' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318227' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318227?labeling=true' target='_blank'>周山川图记<span class='inlineComment2'>（词科第一场，二月十二日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年2月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318227")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318227_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318227'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318227'>相古先民，有周德隆泽洽，用造区夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318227_comment'></div>章亥所步，莫不砥砺，建櫜戢武，斧藻王度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318227_comment'></div>四岳河海，咸秩无文，名颂曰《般》，裒时之对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318227_comment'></div>郑玄释「允犹翕河」之语，谓按《山川图》次序祭之，孔氏《正义》谓其为一图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318227_comment'></div>虽畿籍方志湮轶亡传，谨敷绎旧闻而为记曰：太极肇分，有浮而清，有沈而奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318227_comment'></div>卷石之积，结为巍巍，云蒸雨霈，万物育焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318227_comment'></div>勺水之积，融为浩浩，源迤流衍，万物润焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318227_comment'></div>圣人有作，乃封乃浚，乃刊乃涤，肇称明祀，为民祈禠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318227_comment'></div>若封禅于黄，望秩于虞，旅祭于禹，维见可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318227_comment'></div>然风后受图，九州始布，山海有经，为篇十三，图牒犹未详也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318227_comment'></div>苍姬开统，宪章稽古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318227_comment'></div>以地图知山川之数，职于司书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318227_comment'></div>以地图辨山川之名物，职于大司徒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318227_comment'></div>以九州图知山川之阻，职于司险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318227_comment'></div>天下之图，职方逌掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318227_comment'></div>其山镇曰会稽、衡、华，曰沂岱岳及医无闾、霍、常、□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318227_comment'></div>其大川曰三江、江、汉，曰荥、雒、淮、泗，曰河、泲、泾、汭，及漳、滹池、呕夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318227_comment'></div>又有山师、川师掌其名，山虞、川衡掌其守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318227_comment'></div>艮兼兑丽，目击掌运，抑犹以为略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318227_comment'></div>卑高大小，则其位殊，次主屏摄，则其数异，我是以有秩祭之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318227_comment'></div>河先海后，辨源委也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318227_comment'></div>九河合一，同等列也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318227_comment'></div>岳视三公，渎视诸侯，礼文别也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318227_comment'></div>天子四望，诸侯三望，名分严也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318227_comment'></div>按图定序，因序蒇事，于是宗伯为坛，典瑞奉璋，牧人毛牲，校人饰驹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318227_comment'></div>乃奏蕤宾，歌函钟，舞大夏，服毳冕而祀焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318227_comment'></div>上下有章，无越望之僭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318227_comment'></div>祝史荐信，无矫举之愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318227_comment'></div>山泽通气，歆馨降嘏，百嘉鬯楙，四极艾宁，盛哉铄乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318227_comment'></div>遹观《诗序》，祀于巡守，时迈其邦，爰及柴望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318227_comment'></div>意者，土训夹车道图诏事，其在斯时欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318227_comment'></div>考之传记，天下名山五千三百七十，名川三百，支川三千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318227_comment'></div>周国其在雍州，而立吴岳为西岳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1318227_comment'></div>三代居河洛，而四渎咸在山东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1318227_comment'></div>《公羊春秋》谓天子有方望之事，何休以为望祭凡三十六所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1318227_comment'></div>若义之修而礼之蒇，独于《般》诗见之，夙夜毖祀作周，恭先丕天之大律也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1318227_comment'></div>下逮穆王，大朝黄山，披图视典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1318227_comment'></div>《殷武》疏述郑玄之言，亦参周汉之域，验山川之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1318227_comment'></div>孔安国为汉博士，具见图籍，山川所在，学者尚有稽焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1318227_comment'></div>春官掌三辰之法，以犹鬼神示之居，注亦训犹为图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1318227_comment'></div>仰观俯察，两尽其势矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1318227_comment'></div>虽然，德懋而山川宁，道公而百川理，怀柔河岳，厥有本元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1318227_comment'></div>无设官为极之意，则经野之图不足以致治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1318227_comment'></div>无敬德祈天之忱，则卜洛之图不足以永年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1318227_comment'></div>是图之陈左右也，顾岐阳、丰水而念王业之孔艰，瞻洞庭、孟门而监地险之难恃，江汉思广及之德，南山思疆理之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1318227_comment'></div>清明在躬，与山川出云同一运化，然后能灵承于旅，惟典神天，嶪峨濛鸿，洋洋如在，玉帛云乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1318227_comment'></div>兹图外之眇指，敢正列其义，以昭万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1318227_comment'></div>谨记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1318227_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年2月13日</a>　以从事郎、扬州州学教授，试宏词科，第二场，题二首。作品：代皇子谢赐御书孝经十六句表；尧衢室铭。<div id='poem_1318135' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318135' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318135?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代皇子谢赐御书孝经十六句表<span class='inlineComment2'>（词科第二场，丙辰二月十三日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年2月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318135")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318135_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318135'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318135'>始于事亲，终于事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318135_comment'></div>满而不溢，高而不危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318135_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1318135'>口无择言，身无择行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318135_comment'></div>天之经也，地之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318135_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1318135'>德义可尊，作事可法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318135_comment'></div>居则致敬，养则致乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318135_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1318135'>通于神明，光于四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318135_comment'></div>进思尽忠，退思补过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318135_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1318135'>臣某言：伏蒙圣慈赐臣御书《孝经》十六句者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318135_comment'></div>睿谋垂裕，夙承父训之严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318135_comment'></div>神画疏恩，备举圣经之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318135_comment'></div>因心立教，拭目知荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318135_comment'></div>臣某惶惧惶惧、顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318135_comment'></div>惟夫子之发微言，为曾参而陈孝道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318135_comment'></div>首述君亲之事，谨始及终；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318135_comment'></div>复虞富贵之移，戒危与溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318135_comment'></div>身行口言之无失，天经地义之兼该。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318135_comment'></div>事可法，德可尊，表里俱正；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318135_comment'></div>居致敬，养致乐，造次弗违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318135_comment'></div>神明四海以交孚，进退一忱而非懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318135_comment'></div>有倬飞鸾之翰，于昭诒燕之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318135_comment'></div>二八句之特书，撮其枢要；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318135_comment'></div>千万人之咸悦，始于家邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318135_comment'></div>仰仿迩英之屏，俯殊制旨之注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318135_comment'></div>矧熙朝资善之学，肇祥符丙辰之春，诏儒臣而读是经，锡宸章而刊诸石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318135_comment'></div>荐观洪藻，宏贲前猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318135_comment'></div>某德愧温文，性惭岐嶷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318135_comment'></div>出有师，入有保，早齿虞庠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318135_comment'></div>亲则父，尊则君，恪趋周寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318135_comment'></div>曩者分封之涣号，诲之全孝以移忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318135_comment'></div>旨趣会于五经，未窥圣蕴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318135_comment'></div>德教加于百姓，徒仰皇明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318135_comment'></div>载观河洛图书之光，如亲洙泗问答之语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1318135_comment'></div>兹盖恭遇皇帝陛下学稽古典，笔寓天常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1318135_comment'></div>祚嗣万年，受祉而施于子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1318135_comment'></div>冠冕百行，得手而应于心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1318135_comment'></div>约漆简千有馀言，洒骊珠六十四字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1318135_comment'></div>淳化秘邱之刻，祖武可绳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1318135_comment'></div>绍兴方国之颁，人文增焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1318135_comment'></div>臣敢不聿严琰写，式广家藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1318135_comment'></div>仁孝制六章之诗，远迈唐宫之赐札；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1318135_comment'></div>夙夜事一人之训，缅思建邸之陈图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1318135_comment'></div>臣无任感天荷圣、激切屏营之至，谨奉表称谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1318135_comment'></div>臣某惶惧惶惧、顿首顿首，谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1318135_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318254' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318254' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318254?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尧衢室铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年2月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318254")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318254_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318254'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318254'>衢室，尧所以采民言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318254_comment'></div>惟尧舍己稽众，从谏弗咈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318254_comment'></div>粤昔黄帝，睿哲远览，合宫有听，明台有议，并谋兼知，诒燕后昆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318254_comment'></div>乃考室四达之衢，垂听而问焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318254_comment'></div>迩而百揆四岳，逖而九州四表，聪明光被，嘉言罔伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318254_comment'></div>猗与美哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318254_comment'></div>善旌谤木，昭其明也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318254_comment'></div>素题朴桷，昭其俭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318254_comment'></div>清问而鳏寡靡不达，畴咨而共吺不能蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318254_comment'></div>先惠之意寓于衢尊，尔极之谣闻于康衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318254_comment'></div>仁天知神，隆宽博问，广览兼听，八荒在闼，言布天下，诵圣至今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318254_comment'></div>厥后访以总章，观以总街，复以灵台，询以外朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318254_comment'></div>揆元探耑，帝实肇之，炳诸典谟，卓踪冠德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318254_comment'></div>铺观方策，下听于人，则管子纪其事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318254_comment'></div>议尽天下之心，则文中子申其说；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318254_comment'></div>垂衣襞幅，邃如神明之居，则子华子详其制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318254_comment'></div>《魏文帝纪》亦曰：「广询于下，丰规渊指，历历维见」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318254_comment'></div>或者有调元气、治阴阳之言，以为明堂异名，尧心未昭晰于亿万祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318254_comment'></div>禹之听治，犹铭簨簴，矧惟帝世，必有铭诗，而黍书轶焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318254_comment'></div>皇皇箴谏之路，贰室尊贤，太室考庸，未足匹休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318254_comment'></div>罔罗旧闻，补其辞曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1318254'>于穆放勋，道泰朝清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318254_comment'></div>光被四表，在予户庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318254_comment'></div>惟天为大，德宇恢闳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318254_comment'></div>储思法宫，群龙翼承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318254_comment'></div>从人稽众，圣而不矜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318254_comment'></div>五达之衢，谤木求箴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318254_comment'></div>康衢游童，洋洋颂声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318254_comment'></div>衢尊先惠，涵泳至仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318254_comment'></div>于焉筑室，广聪垂明，合宫之听，率祖攸行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318254_comment'></div>茅茨流化，頫数阶蓂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318254_comment'></div>幅舄入觐，若星共辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318254_comment'></div>彤车黄收，巍乎天临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318254_comment'></div>帝晖迩止，垂衣如神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1318254_comment'></div>上开言路，下达民情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1318254_comment'></div>何以来之，有鼓有旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1318254_comment'></div>清问鳏寡，尔隐毕申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1318254_comment'></div>畴咨四岳，朕愆悉陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1318254_comment'></div>侧陋在下，罔阏予闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1318254_comment'></div>象恭庸违，罔惑孔壬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1318254_comment'></div>相在尔室，咫尺八纮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1318254_comment'></div>谁谓民远，察其嚬呻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1318254_comment'></div>夏铎徇路，规谏于春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1318254_comment'></div>汤有总街，观诽于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1318254_comment'></div>爰周质隆，外朝是询。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1318254_comment'></div>维昔盛帝，轨迹易遵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1318254_comment'></div>君闻无壅，天衢以亨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1318254_comment'></div>孰曰道谋，不溃于成？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1318254_comment'></div>啧室之议，陋彼齐人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1318254_comment'></div>宣室之问，卑哉汉文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1318254_comment'></div>尧在万世，如见其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1318254_comment'></div>敢告后王，贻此休铭。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1318254_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年2月14日</a>　以从事郎、扬州州学教授，试宏词科，第三场，题二首。作品：天禧编御集序；汉华平颂。<div id='poem_1318188' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318188' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318188?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天禧编御集序<span class='inlineComment2'>（词科第三场题目）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年2月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318188")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318188_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318188'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318188'>宋受命于穆清，五纬集奎观，人文化天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318188_comment'></div>维三叶重光，真宗章圣皇帝浚哲钦明，体尧蹈舜，游意艺圃，积思书林，睿藻天葩，轇轕元化，庆云在上，万物五色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318188_comment'></div>宜刻玉版，藏金匮，垂训姚远，以三二典、七六经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318188_comment'></div>天禧之元，月旅黄钟，日躔庚子，臣虚己裒次御集百二十卷，爰即禁庭，俯示承弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318188_comment'></div>明年孟春，严储于继文殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318188_comment'></div>四年季夏甲午，列局崇文，分命注释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318188_comment'></div>仲冬庚申，出圣制七百二十二卷畀辅臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318188_comment'></div>五年季春庚子，钦奉御集，尊阁天章，定著为三百卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318188_comment'></div>仲秋庚午，藏之名山，以副墨朌焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318188_comment'></div>赫乎盛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318188_comment'></div>集有序篇，实出御制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318188_comment'></div>五年正月癸卯，偕圣政纪序，召迩列观之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318188_comment'></div>臣俟罪翰墨，衣被昭回之光，稽首书下方曰：帝王之文即天地自然之文，仰而观则七政三辰之炳耀，俯而察则山川卉木之彪列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318188_comment'></div>帝尧焕有文章，文王经纬天地，繇此其选，道心渊粹，发为英华，圣学精微，写为谟训，岂有意于文哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318188_comment'></div>昔者黄帝丹书及铭，传至周汉，圣文裒集，其昉此乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318188_comment'></div>高、文有传，著在《七略》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318188_comment'></div>武帝有集，始析二卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318188_comment'></div>贞观、开元，成集并垂，理愧于辞，驳亡以议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318188_comment'></div>惟我艺祖绍天觉民，赞述孔颜，道统复续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318188_comment'></div>太宗继序，缉熙光明，皇文掞天，箫勺宇宙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318188_comment'></div>臣文仲编为三十卷，臣彭年编为二百十四卷，燕谋诒翼，用敷遗于章圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318188_comment'></div>厥既北詟荤允，西縻灵夏，幅员清谧，威械戢藏，升中岱宗，展采汾阴，礼叶乐华，葳蕤葱茜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318188_comment'></div>帝益思持盈制治，启迪化原，乃增讲员，乃御延阁，左右图籍，镕经铸词，绿字琼章，璧明奎灿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318188_comment'></div>歌有《念农》、《阅兵》、《奉先》、《为政》《、丰年》、《观麦》、《喜雨》、《瑞雪》之属，斯元首薰风之雅咏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318188_comment'></div>论有《勤治》、《崇儒》、《祥瑞》、《解疑》《、思政》、《敧器》、《为君难》、《宽财利》之属，斯画卦重爻之邃学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318188_comment'></div>《龙阁》有赞，《圣文》有颂，《元龟》有序，《泰山》有铭，《庇民》有述，《修河》有碑，三记五箴之作，《清景》百篇之制，经史遍咏，明良载赓，肆笔而成，戛切韶濩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318188_comment'></div>帝心谦巩，未议汇辑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318188_comment'></div>祥符四祀九月丙子，臣敏中请录宸章，袭藏渠观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318188_comment'></div>而文颂歌诗十五卷上于五年四月癸卯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318188_comment'></div>号登天禧，遂金声玉振，而集大成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318188_comment'></div>臣窃从太史氏钦觌集目，凡颂、碑、铭、赞之卷二十六，诗歌、辞章、乐府之卷一百十四，论、述、序、箴、条记、文书其卷四十，《正说》、《承华要略》、《静居》、《玉宸》、《法音集》其卷四十有五，《春秋要言》五卷，胪分试题、表词卷别七十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318188_comment'></div>芸签钿轴，数盈三百，视滋福殿所观为益备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318188_comment'></div>云汉之章、风行水上之文，作者不可及已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1318188_comment'></div>鸿生钜学，属词摛藻，有三代风，非金玉追琢之功，鸢飞鱼跃之化欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1318188_comment'></div>抑臣管窥国史，祥符丙辰之春，开资善，训元良，箴记歌吟，日赉月锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1318188_comment'></div>天禧四祀仲冬甲戌，臣殊编摹赐东宫御制成五十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1318188_comment'></div>育蒙泉之德，培丰水之仁，《帝范》、《金镜》、《训戒》等书，方斯蔑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1318188_comment'></div>文子文孙监先宪，酌祖道，至于万年永保民，罔不自斯文始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1318188_comment'></div>臣谨表而出之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1318188_comment'></div>乾兴初元八月辛亥，以是集锡该辅，并识于篇，以铺扬我宋重规叠矩之盛美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1318188_comment'></div>臣谨序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1318188_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318269' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318269' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318269?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汉华平颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年2月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318269")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318269_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318269'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318269'>皇汉中兴三叶，缉熙康乂，燕及皇天，惠露德风，坯冶泰和，畅垓溯埏，炤景饮醴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318269_comment'></div>瑞命总集，嘉祥备致，仁及于木，效异吐奇，而华平生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318269_comment'></div>平之义大矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318269_comment'></div>在天为泰阶，在地为嘉木，世道夷陂，气感类从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318269_comment'></div>维木之祥，品汇匪一，宾连阔达，紫脱平露，《白虎》《礼纬》，彪列其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318269_comment'></div>而华平独著于《孝经援神契》，谓德至地则是物盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318269_comment'></div>张衡作赋，扬厉东京之美，春圃是植，爰纪神异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318269_comment'></div>薛综注释，指为瑞木，谓天下平则其华平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318269_comment'></div>《册府元龟》载元和二年至章和元年，华平见郡国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318269_comment'></div>《艺文类聚》述《东观记》，以为芝英华平，史官不可胜纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318269_comment'></div>沈约《宋志》亦曰其枝正平，王者有德则生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318269_comment'></div>汉元和中生郡国，其当章帝之世，与帝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318269_comment'></div>左右艺文，斟酌律礼，道无偏陂，如砥如衡，根于正心，发于平治，有泰之吉，无否之倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318269_comment'></div>煌虖休哉，植物之敧器也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318269_comment'></div>昔在孝武，奇木兆祥，胡粤冠带；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318269_comment'></div>亦越永平，木枝内附，朝堂奉觞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318269_comment'></div>矧时珍物，见象知治，应图合牒，儆戒默寓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318269_comment'></div>兰台诸彦，献歌踵闻，景况洪褫，铺藻犹𡙇，敢稽《选》注，以颂以规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318269_comment'></div>颂曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1318269'>颢穹槃物，木神则仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318269_comment'></div>汉以仁兴，木瑞爰轃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318269_comment'></div>赤符膺统，丕阐坤珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318269_comment'></div>德丰泽鬯，万象一春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318269_comment'></div>允文肃宗，岂弟宜民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318269_comment'></div>仁及于木，匹休周成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318269_comment'></div>支附叶著，函夏谧清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318269_comment'></div>言观于朝，贤庸俊登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318269_comment'></div>言观于边，𣟄靖燧沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318269_comment'></div>美发英华，治浃升平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318269_comment'></div>泰和融液，嘉卉挺生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318269_comment'></div>植之春圃，吐葩飏荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318269_comment'></div>祥参平露，光掩芝英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318269_comment'></div>五衢四照，未数山经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318269_comment'></div>含章自天，绚耀槐宸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1318269_comment'></div>启篇稽牒，咨尔儒臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1318269_comment'></div>德至于地，纬书昭陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1318269_comment'></div>乾元谦施，帝德之纯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1318269_comment'></div>烨烨其华，元气储精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1318269_comment'></div>维平不猗，式如玉衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1318269_comment'></div>太平有象，品物流形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1318269_comment'></div>其象维何，万国咸宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1318269_comment'></div>醴泉下滋，潏露上凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1318269_comment'></div>匪棣之偏，匪葵斯倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1318269_comment'></div>随方表应，敧器在庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1318269_comment'></div>考祥视履，毖于未萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1318269_comment'></div>用人必公，淑别慝明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1318269_comment'></div>敷政必和，直错枉信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1318269_comment'></div>天寿平格，葆命日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1318269_comment'></div>右我炎祚，木支蕃蓁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1318269_comment'></div>奇木旁出，对述终军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1318269_comment'></div>解编削衽，殊俗来宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1318269_comment'></div>木枝内附，永平昌辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1318269_comment'></div>寿觞敬举，驩溢簪绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1318269_comment'></div>于赫神物，夐轶前闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1318269_comment'></div>辩章化洽，肴覈仁林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1318269_comment'></div>咸曰我后，能莳尧蓂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1318269_comment'></div>俯陋后叶，并柯成文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1318269_comment'></div>瑞图逌纪，政令之均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1318269_comment'></div>维德弱刚，低卬以分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1318269_comment'></div>木匪于祥，戒在持盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1318269_comment'></div>无平不陂，保泰兢兢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1318269_comment'></div>顾名思义，有美有箴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1318269_comment'></div>文之雅诗，以继逵骃。</div><div id='poem_sentence_61_1318269_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年3月</a>　有旨听擢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年4月</a>　添差浙西安抚司干办公室。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年5月</a>　入朝任职，置文天祥为第一，评其“是卷古谊若龟鑑，忠肝如铁石，臣敢为得人贺！”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年5月</a>　入朝任职，弟应凤年二十七，廷对以第二甲第九人登第。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年</a>　掌管架格库文牍及库房修葺等。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年7月</a>　除国子録。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年10月</a>　改宣教郎，依旧职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年10月庚子</a>　诏皇子忠王赵祺授镇南遂安军节度使，皇女进封昇国公主，作表。作品：代贺皇子加两镇公主进封昇国表。<div id='poem_1318170' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318170' id='poem_title_1318170_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318170'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318170'>宝祚申休，昭格乾坤之贶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318170_comment'></div>浚源疏渥，式符震巽之亨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318170_comment'></div>庆辑宗祊，光增简册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318170_comment'></div>窃以汉封帝子，兼国十城；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318170_comment'></div>周重王姬，下后一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318170_comment'></div>未有跗鄂联辉之盛，诞膺丝纶并命之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318170_comment'></div>双节建旄，贻远谋于燕翼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318170_comment'></div>大邦彻土，协佳气于龙蟠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318170_comment'></div>彝章稽列圣之传，美号取陪京之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318170_comment'></div>非直亲亲而贤贤，用彰蛰蛰以绳绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318170_comment'></div>恭惟学粹察伦，德深垂裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318170_comment'></div>主器莫若长，早谕教以正名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318170_comment'></div>立爱始于家，成肃雍而流咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318170_comment'></div>克昌厥后，载锡之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318170_comment'></div>百世本支，衍绵瓞秾华之祉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318170_comment'></div>万年祚嗣，轶猗兰仙李之芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318170_comment'></div>臣幸玷观风，忻聆涣号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318170_comment'></div>宜民《假乐》，愿歌右命之章；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318170_comment'></div>占梦《斯干》，遂致中兴之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318170_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1318170_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年6月</a>　应麟上书具陈国是，建议当以德治国，君臣对答后，理宗问其父姓名，后赞曰：尔父以陈善为忠，可谓继美。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年正月</a>　替特命主掌贡举考试的知贡举谢皇上诏书。作品：代知举谢赐御札表。<div id='poem_1318171' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318171' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_1318171_comment'></div>天藻昭回，时髦兴起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318171_comment'></div>窃以熙朝稽古，进士设科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318171_comment'></div>无竞维人，有常立武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318171_comment'></div>萃强本折冲之彦，凝理内御外之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318171_comment'></div>大哉王言，监于先宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318171_comment'></div>训词深厚，焕有三代之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318171_comment'></div>俊良登崇，庶几二祖之烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318171_comment'></div>饬逌司而决择，广多士之蒐罗，祗聆丝纶，咸知标准。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318171_comment'></div>兹盖恭遇道行常久，德运乾元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318171_comment'></div>《菁莪》之泽既深，《采薇》之治尤重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318171_comment'></div>筹边体国，将因言而察能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318171_comment'></div>尊主庇民，俾由学而致用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318171_comment'></div>明谟所迪，美习维新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318171_comment'></div>臣敢不精以抡才，公而率属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318171_comment'></div>选士考实行，复观儒效之真；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318171_comment'></div>得贤立太平，益迓皇图之永。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1318171_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年2月</a>　因应麟博闻强识，积学多闻，除太常寺主簿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年3月</a>　出院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年5月</a>　轮对后殿，忤丁大全，是日即以台谏论罢。<br /><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年</a>　弟应凤中选博学宏词科，有“三洪”美称。<br /><a href="javascript: class='inlineComment2'>（集称洪兵书，未载其名。考《宋史》，是时有洪天锡、洪芹二人。《天锡传》不言居兵书，《洪芹传》云开庆元年权礼部（侍）郎、中书舍人，属兵兴，则此称兵书当为洪芹无疑。）</span>代洪兵书谢表。<span class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318175'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318175'>武部跻班，屡自天而有命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318175_comment'></div>文章率属，未满岁而为真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318175_comment'></div>揣分侥踰，承恩兢惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318175_comment'></div>窃以国有六职，司戎独省文书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318175_comment'></div>天生五材，明政必及閒暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318175_comment'></div>方《采薇》之治小愒，而彻桑之备有严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318175_comment'></div>元祐息兵，用苏轼词章之彦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318175_comment'></div>乾道复古，召黄中耆艾之儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318175_comment'></div>是以道德成乎安强，名实加于上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318175_comment'></div>如臣末学，敢跂前修！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318175_comment'></div>翰墨非长，叨世掌丝纶之美；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318175_comment'></div>弟昆迭进，愧才皆经纬之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318175_comment'></div>粗守朴忠，躐居华贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318175_comment'></div>俎豆之间未学军旅，承摄无虞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318175_comment'></div>甲兵之问不至庙堂，简稽何补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318175_comment'></div>久包羞于辰履，俄正秩于夏卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318175_comment'></div>帝有恩言，循墙靡获；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318175_comment'></div>官皆民誉，窃位是惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318175_comment'></div>钦哉训迪之明，凛若满盈之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318175_comment'></div>行周法度，敕舜时几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318175_comment'></div>假有庙以除戎，益谨不虞之戒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318175_comment'></div>尊上帝而吁俊，灼知常任之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318175_comment'></div>攘夷先政事之修，强本多隽英之进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318175_comment'></div>顾令迂懦，亦预褒升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318175_comment'></div>臣敢不精白承休，靖共好直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318175_comment'></div>既莫遂蔡谟之逊，再登纳言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318175_comment'></div>愿恪勤程伯之官，复歌《常武》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318175_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1318175_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a id='poem_content_1318138'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318138'>明堂孔阳，秩九筵之盛典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318138_comment'></div>圣人能飨，申亿载之宏休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318138_comment'></div>庆洽神人，欢腾宇宙<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318138_comment'></div>窃以接三才之奥，严将礼于季秋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318138_comment'></div>宣二祖之光，协初郊于先甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318138_comment'></div>物备口有成之告，民和皆至治之馨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318138_comment'></div>若昔燕诒，自今骏惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318138_comment'></div>恭唯刚健中正，悠久光明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318138_comment'></div>更化而福禄来，迓续肇基之运；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318138_comment'></div>修政而境土复，恢宏再造之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318138_comment'></div>观其会通，毖于上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318138_comment'></div>农扈奏屡丰之瑞，边陲凝耆定之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318138_comment'></div>精意以禋，裒时之对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318138_comment'></div>在宫在庙，观盥之荐有孚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318138_comment'></div>于帝于宗，泰元之策复始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318138_comment'></div>乂时旸若，德与气游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318138_comment'></div>前星重匕鬯之晖，华景粲璧珠之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318138_comment'></div>缉熙纯嘏，安乐太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318138_comment'></div>永命而丕历年，陈常于夏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318138_comment'></div>敷言而锡保极，有泽如春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318138_comment'></div>于赫汉仪，以笃周祜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318138_comment'></div>臣等幸叨显相，欣睹熙成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318138_comment'></div>式典靖四方，愿进夙夜畏威之戒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318138_comment'></div>奉觞上曼寿，聿观癸亥宗祀之祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318138_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1318138_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1263&endYear=1263')">1263年</a>　汤汉为少卿，与先生临墙居。朝夕讲道，赞应麟：“吾阅士良广，惟伯厚乃真儒也。使真文忠在，愿同在弟子列。”荐先生于似道。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年</a>　除行秘书郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年7月甲戌</a>　彗星见于柳，率同舍五人扣閤上书，极论执政、侍从、台谏之罪，积私财、行公田之害。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年8月</a>　轮对延和殿。有旨缴进。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年</a>　兼沂靖王府教授。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年9月</a>　赴讲堂讲《礼记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年</a>　迁行秘书著作佐郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年10月丁卯</a>　理宗崩，度宗即位。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年10月3日庚午</a>　兼摄礼部郎官，草百官表，撰请御正殿三表。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年11月壬申</a>　嗣君御殿，丞相四上表即允。似道令应麟增撰三表，应麟即临次具以进。作品：宰臣以下请度宗听政第一表、第二表、第三表、第四表、第五表、第六表、第七表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（表名据王应麟著张骁飞点校《四明文献集》中华书局2010年。）</span><div id='poem_1318139' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318139' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318139?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宰臣以下请度宗听政第一表</a><span class='authorDate'>（景定五年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318139")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318139_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318139'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318139'>四海遏音，遽□遗弓之慕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318139_comment'></div>百官承式，有严嗣服之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318139_comment'></div>跂望清光，肃循大卞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318139_comment'></div>恭唯聪明时敏，圣知日跻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318139_comment'></div>龙楼庶务之参闻，灼知政体；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318139_comment'></div>虎闱三善之兼得，允协人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318139_comment'></div>祇台德先，迪从子保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318139_comment'></div>问安视膳，冀文考之复初；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318139_comment'></div>遗大投艰，痛周家之降割。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318139_comment'></div>未堪多难，永言孝思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318139_comment'></div>然而色之戚、哭之哀，已孚舆望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318139_comment'></div>朝以听、夕以访，难旷繁机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318139_comment'></div>即位五始以体元，践阼三日而端冕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318139_comment'></div>惟哲作则，示民有尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318139_comment'></div>伏愿遹骏先猷，勉遵中制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318139_comment'></div>法宫亲事，乾首物而万国宁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318139_comment'></div>司士诏仪，德如辰而众星拱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318139_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1318139_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318143' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318143' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318143?labeling=true' target='_blank'>第五表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年11月壬申）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318143")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318143_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318143'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318143'>知临大君之宜，群心丕徯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318143_comment'></div>孝思下土之式，四诏如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318143_comment'></div>非敢咸谏于王，亦曰节情以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318143_comment'></div>窃惟伦制在乎兼尽，经权可以并行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318143_comment'></div>未有命戒而居庐，难遵滕国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318143_comment'></div>继犹判涣而谋庙，必监周诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318143_comment'></div>今敬通于神明，且哀发于言语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318143_comment'></div>是亦为政，颙若有孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318143_comment'></div>矧导训受瑁之初，俾听法服缞之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318143_comment'></div>考作室既底法，毖我成功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318143_comment'></div>朝至昃用和民，所其无逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318143_comment'></div>克绍先烈，惟怀永图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318143_comment'></div>慈良于丧，倘未正路朝之位；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318143_comment'></div>陟降厥士，亟当循便殿之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318143_comment'></div>伏愿寅念燕诒，于昭龙造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318143_comment'></div>即斋居而决事，新圣化以承休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318143_comment'></div>福威惟辟之尊，四方来贺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318143_comment'></div>公卿奉职以奏，庶绩其凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318143_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1318143_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318144' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318144' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318144?labeling=true' target='_blank'>第六表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年11月壬申）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318144")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318144_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318144'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318144'>视朝周典，聿观治化之新；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318144_comment'></div>易月汉仪，难执亮阴之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318144_comment'></div>五下明诏，一哉圣心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318144_comment'></div>仰思慕之无穷，由敷陈之未至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318144_comment'></div>窃以丧与易宁戚，虽致其哀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318144_comment'></div>礼因情为文，必知所节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318144_comment'></div>练冠而亲机务，素幄而见臣邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318144_comment'></div>古有行之，时则可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318144_comment'></div>放诸四海而准，孝已感于元□；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318144_comment'></div>至于万年惟王，本实关于初政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318144_comment'></div>体《访落》、《小毖》之意，躬《天保》、《采薇》之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318144_comment'></div>岂必端忧，乃为继志？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318144_comment'></div>伏愿卑于众戚，稽若邦彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318144_comment'></div>昭德以照百官，副玉几遗音之托；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318144_comment'></div>正统而法五始，衍宝龟申命之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318144_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1318144_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318145' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318145' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318145?labeling=true' target='_blank'>第七表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年11月壬申）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318145")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318145_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318145'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318145'>天作之君，飞龙利见；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318145_comment'></div>日致其孝，隙驷易流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318145_comment'></div>若三年惟不言，则万事惧有阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318145_comment'></div>谦冲已过，震越靡宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318145_comment'></div>窃以上圣每惜寸阴，治象皆观挟日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318145_comment'></div>嗣大历服，无毖恤成功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318145_comment'></div>受群臣朝，乃考图敷贲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318145_comment'></div>此作新民之美化，亦付有家之初心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318145_comment'></div>丕显孝皇，祗承高庙，执丧固踰旧体，涖政靡越旬时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318145_comment'></div>迪前人光，为后世法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318145_comment'></div>恭惟英姿绳武，粹学察伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318145_comment'></div>方裒集燕谋，敷言是彝是训；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318145_comment'></div>念绍膺骏命，无疆惟休惟艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318145_comment'></div>遽临旧贯之居，永怀罔极之感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318145_comment'></div>哀难为继，德何以加？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318145_comment'></div>伏望益广尧聪，少抑舜慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318145_comment'></div>人道自始，听宜务于五先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318145_comment'></div>生者常行，节愿参乎四制。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1318145_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年</a>　撰表。作品：贺冬至节表。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年</a>　推登极改元恩。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年12月甲辰</a>　以上生日为乾会节，撰四表。作品：请上乾会节名第一表、第二表、第三表、第四表。<div id='poem_1318149' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318149' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318149?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请上乾会圣节名第一表</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸淳元年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318149")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318149_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318149'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318149'>天生上圣，丕昭震夙之符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318149_comment'></div>月在正阳，允叶乾嘉之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318149_comment'></div>善治聿来于福禄，大德必得于寿名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318149_comment'></div>宜新凤纪之编，式表虹流之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318149_comment'></div>窃以仁皇御极，如岁之春；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318149_comment'></div>炎祚融辉，发祥维夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318149_comment'></div>若稽资始之义，用彰命哲之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318149_comment'></div>昔以元长人，于穆不已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318149_comment'></div>今以亨合礼，申锡无疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318149_comment'></div>恭惟刚健粹精，居行聚辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318149_comment'></div>储英潜跃，肇乘时于六龙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318149_comment'></div>膺运文明，期咸宁于万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318149_comment'></div>阐河图而毓瑞，承祖烈以重光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318149_comment'></div>臣工奉觞，忻千载之一遇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318149_comment'></div>侯卫执贽，浃四方之大和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318149_comment'></div>辑《诗》雅归美之忱，赞《易》象为君之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318149_comment'></div>既多受祉，于永保民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318149_comment'></div>臣等不胜大愿，谨以四月初九日为乾会节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318149_comment'></div>伏望俯鉴舆情，仰遵徽典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318149_comment'></div>南山献祝，薰风载咏于舜弦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318149_comment'></div>北阙胪欢，湛露普沾于周泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318149_comment'></div>著之令甲，副在有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318149_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1318149_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年</a>　草制诏书。作品：嗣荣王与芮赐诏书不名依前皇叔太师武康宁江节度使判大宗正嗣荣王加食邑一千户食实封四百户。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1265&endYear=1265')">1265年正月戊申</a>　乾会节，进疏。作品：功德疏。<div id='poem_1318163' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318163' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1318163'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318163'>尧封献祝，恪共臣职之常；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318163_comment'></div>汉阙疏荣，敷贲思言之奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318163_comment'></div>对扬焜耀，祗诵凌兢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318163_comment'></div>窃以亿载登太平，与天齐寿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318163_comment'></div>十行赐方国，细书成文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318163_comment'></div>藐如微臣，欣际嘉会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318163_comment'></div>伏念某久濡雨露，假守甸畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318163_comment'></div>宽诏屡颁，寅奉好生之训；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318163_comment'></div>颂声允洽，肃将归美之忱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318163_comment'></div>便蕃宸指之裒，舄奕侯邦之宠。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1265&endYear=1265')">1265年2月</a>　赵葵授少傅，草制。作品：赵葵特授少傅依前观文殿大学士充醴泉观使冀国公加食邑食实封仍令有司择日备礼册命制。<div id='poem_1318067' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318067' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318067?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赵葵特授少傅依前观文殿大学士充醴泉观使冀国公加食邑食实封仍令所司择日备礼册命制</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸淳元年二月三日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318067")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318067_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318067'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318067'>门下：朕祗遹燕谋，丕承鸿业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318067_comment'></div>祐民作君而相上帝，惟怀永图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318067_comment'></div>贰公弘化而弼一人，式序在位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318067_comment'></div>眷言硕望，首锡茂恩，晋左棘之穹班，涣大廷之显册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318067_comment'></div>少傅具官赵葵，宽闳而肃括，俊伟而光明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318067_comment'></div>文武宪于万邦，有应变折冲之略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318067_comment'></div>忱恂迪于九德，有庇民尊主之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318067_comment'></div>出则秉斧钺以董师，入则践枢衡而穆縡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318067_comment'></div>谦谦终吉，蹇蹇匪躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318067_comment'></div>愿从赤松，进退合于礼义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318067_comment'></div>非谓乔木，老成重于典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318067_comment'></div>肆予绍休，若古访落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318067_comment'></div>追先帝之遇，谅怀欲报之忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318067_comment'></div>贻哲命之初，靡忘用德之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318067_comment'></div>诞敷沛泽，可后耆英！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318067_comment'></div>昔宁皇之登至尊，命必大而升亚傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318067_comment'></div>有嘉雅操，允蹈前闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318067_comment'></div>夏篆通旃，峻跻特揖，祥源使组，仍冠延恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318067_comment'></div>增多邑于采封，衍真畬于圭食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318067_comment'></div>以笃股肱之旧，以昭体貌之隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318067_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318067_comment'></div>世服劳，纪于大常，夙懋屏毗之绩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318067_comment'></div>身虽外，心在王室，尚遵寅亮之谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318067_comment'></div>永肩远猷，益介纯嘏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318067_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1318067_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1265&endYear=1265')">1265年3月</a>　兼权礼部郎官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1265&endYear=1265')">1265年</a>　程元凤授少保，草制。作品：程元凤特授少保依前观文殿大学士充醴泉观使新安郡开国公加食邑食实封制。<div id='poem_1318068' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318068' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318068?labeling=true' target='_blank'>程元凤特授少保依前观文殿大学士充醴泉观使新安郡开国公加食邑食实封仍令所司择日备礼册命制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1265年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318068")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318068_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318068'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318068'>门下：朕仰惟前代训官，莫重贰公之任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318068_comment'></div>永言孝思嗣服，聿怀有佐之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318068_comment'></div>寅绍丕图，恪遵成宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318068_comment'></div>仁沾恩洽，用大赉于善人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318068_comment'></div>谟明弼谐，实劢相于烈考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318068_comment'></div>晋班孤棘，孚号明廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318068_comment'></div>特进具官程元凤，德厚而器闳，学醇而识邃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318068_comment'></div>浩然养以直，尽责难陈善之恭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318068_comment'></div>休焉如有容，得持美效君之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318068_comment'></div>辅赞而藏诸用，动静不失其宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318068_comment'></div>蔼闻藩翰之庸，自适丘园之佚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318068_comment'></div>访予落止，敷时绎思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318068_comment'></div>惟旧人知若勤，所以报先帝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318068_comment'></div>有嘉猷则入告，罔不祗师言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318068_comment'></div>繄我硕儒，可无异数！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318068_comment'></div>昔孝皇之盛际，重亚保之殊荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318068_comment'></div>臣浩以耆英而叙升，俊卿以宿望而延拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318068_comment'></div>兹率厥典，载锡之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318068_comment'></div>絺冕篆车，峻外朝之特揖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318068_comment'></div>珍台閒馆，仍秘殿之隆名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318068_comment'></div>申培采邑之封，益衍圭畬之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318068_comment'></div>非惟沾渥，式示褒章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318068_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318068_comment'></div>罔以宠居成功，久遂伊尹告归之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318068_comment'></div>在厥初贻哲命，无忘召公为保之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318068_comment'></div>克迈前修，永绥多祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318068_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1318068_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1265&endYear=1265')">1265年</a>　高斯得兼侍讲，草诰。作品：高斯得依前起居舍人特授侍讲诰。<div id='poem_1318092' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318092' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318092?labeling=true' target='_blank'>高斯得依前行起居舍人特授兼侍读诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1265年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318092")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318092_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318092'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318092'>敕具官某：朕闻学于古训乃有获，询兹黄发则罔愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318092_comment'></div>在天圣时，臣奭以《尚书》劝讲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318092_comment'></div>在元祐际，臣维因《宝训》进规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318092_comment'></div>诞登耆儒，聿骏先烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318092_comment'></div>尔履粹而养以直，学醇而资之深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318092_comment'></div>惟耇成人，肯来览德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318092_comment'></div>曰太史友，命尔纪言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318092_comment'></div>眷聚辨居行之勤，倚薰陶涵养之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318092_comment'></div>何相见之晚也，试垂听而问焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318092_comment'></div>百篇雅奥之文，中兴修攘之治，示我显行，率惟敉功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318092_comment'></div>清閒之燕尽精思，朕乐观于夙望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318092_comment'></div>温润之气可开道，尔念绍于前修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318092_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1318092_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a
