ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1266&endYear=1266')">1266年</a>　命举廉吏，草诏。作品：举廉吏诏。<div id='poem_1318037' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318037' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318037?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举廉吏诏<span class='inlineComment2'>（词科所业。下篇同。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1266年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318037")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318037_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318037'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318037'>敕门下：周听治以六计，廉善居先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318037_comment'></div>汉辟士以四科，清白为首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318037_comment'></div>朕灼知有俊，诞保受民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318037_comment'></div>惟前代迪厥官，不肩好货；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318037_comment'></div>凡正人羞其行，庶几成风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318037_comment'></div>尝赐札以律贪，复作铭而申训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318037_comment'></div>曾是在位，犹从匪彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318037_comment'></div>鞭挞不已而宠赂章，簠簋不饬而节行缺，退食鲜《羔羊》之操，虐民多《硕鼠》之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318037_comment'></div>念激浊在于扬清，而瘅恶莫如彰善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318037_comment'></div>神爵奖朱邑之洁，治盛循良；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318037_comment'></div>开元旌王邱之廉，风移苛娆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318037_comment'></div>一贤蒙擢，百辟向方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318037_comment'></div>肆公道之天开，闵颓波之澜倒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318037_comment'></div>克正罔敢弗正，既昭德以塞违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318037_comment'></div>进良以率不良，与厉精而更始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318037_comment'></div>咨尔承休之彦，体予美俗之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318037_comment'></div>廉欲得其真，公选洁修之士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318037_comment'></div>举皆贤于己，博询操履之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318037_comment'></div>内则如光禄之荐王嘉，外则如河东之察黄霸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318037_comment'></div>人之有猷有守，具以实言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318037_comment'></div>予其懋赏懋官，亦克用劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318037_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1318037_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1266&endYear=1266')">1266年</a>　升兼学士院权直。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1266&endYear=1266')">1266年3月</a>　援淳熙词臣倪思故事乞免兼礼部郎，有旨依所乞，免兼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1266&endYear=1266')">1266年9月</a>　转朝散郎，除将作监。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1266&endYear=1266')">1266年9月</a>　帝视朝，应麟轮对，帝嘉纳之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1266&endYear=1266')">1266年11月</a>　赐绯鱼袋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1266&endYear=1266')">1266年12月</a>　应麟叔父宗正少卿正甫公拯卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年正月己丑朔</a>　郊，为礼部郎官，奏解严，撰表。作品：拟贺郊祀礼成进诗表。<div id='poem_1318172' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318172' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318172?labeling=true' target='_blank'>拟贺郊祀礼成进诗表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1267年正月己丑朔）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318172")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318172_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318172'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318172'>万年敬休，方茂成王之德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318172_comment'></div>上日肆类，率循虞帝之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318172_comment'></div>乾端坤倪之燕娱，月御星驱之鴹吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318172_comment'></div>嘉气液洽，治象融明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318172_comment'></div>昔孝祖乾道之元，行郊礼孟春之朔，敛柴而美光烛，奠胙而慈颜愉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318172_comment'></div>维清文典，肇禋思皇多祜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318172_comment'></div>于赫汤孙，奏假申锡无疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318172_comment'></div>恭惟聪明宅中，仁俭自度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318172_comment'></div>恭默三祀，在宫在庙，不显亦临；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318172_comment'></div>兢业万几，治内治外，于神可告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318172_comment'></div>乃殷荐于豫顺，乃孝享于萃亨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318172_comment'></div>多士骏奔走而伻从，四方大和会而来祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318172_comment'></div>萧脂以兴嗣岁，黼绣以歌青阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318172_comment'></div>作龟祢宫，登奉徽册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318172_comment'></div>用骍太室，肆祼鬯圭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318172_comment'></div>芳扢泰畤之觚坛，肸饰甘泉之卤簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318172_comment'></div>毡栾皇邸，茧牲桂尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318172_comment'></div>爟火举而澹高斿，瑄玉奠而熙纯嘏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318172_comment'></div>翠凤回轸，金鸡舒恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318172_comment'></div>簇仗正太极之朝，簪花介长乐之寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318172_comment'></div>裒时之对，惟圣为能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318172_comment'></div>臣幸扈属车，肃展釐席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318172_comment'></div>正月见祖，奏元和亿载之诗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318172_comment'></div>千春献祥，续臣甫三礼之赋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1318172_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年正月己丑朔</a>　黎明肆赦，撰文。作品：郊祀大礼赦文首词、尾词。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年正月己丑朔丁酉</a>　奉皇太后宝上尊号称“寿和”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年正月己丑朔辛丑</a>　皇太后受册礼，以太常博士为前导寿和太和册宝官，草四诰。作品：谢堂改明堂恩曾祖深甫特赠太师进封鲁王。祖渠伯特赠太师追封魏王。父奕昌特赠太师追封魏王。母吴氏特赠齐魏国夫人。<div id='poem_1318128' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318128' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318128?labeling=true' target='_blank'>资政殿大学士两浙镇抚使谢堂该明堂恩曾祖深甫特赠太师进封鲁王诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1267年正月己丑朔辛丑）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318128")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318128_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318128'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318128'>敕：肆祀有来雍雍，裒对宗祊之嘏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318128_comment'></div>秉德其邻翼翼，肃将使范之恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318128_comment'></div>维贤相之流光，施曾孙之济美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318128_comment'></div>式敷馂泽，申贲蜜章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318128_comment'></div>具官某故曾祖某，德载鼎彝，功高廊庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318128_comment'></div>邓太傅佐中天之业，实钟长乐之祥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318128_comment'></div>郭汾阳著贯日之功，丕衍具庆之祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318128_comment'></div>衮绣焜煌于三叶，旌繁炳耀于六符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318128_comment'></div>助我明禋，锡以多祜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318128_comment'></div>师垣王社，人爵之贵可加；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318128_comment'></div>赠策纶言，祖烈之传无斁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318128_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1318128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1318128'><span class='label'>按：</span>深甫相宁宗。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1318128_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1318129' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318129' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318129?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢堂祖渠伯特赠太师追封魏王诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1267年正月己丑朔辛丑）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318129")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318129_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318129'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318129'>敕：多士对越在天，咨政途而相祀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318129_comment'></div>烈祖有秩斯祜，怀世德以敷恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318129_comment'></div>眷言棠笏之传，追贲松楹之享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318129_comment'></div>具官某祖父，裳华文献，乔木声猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318129_comment'></div>高密之仁，至训而报益大；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318129_comment'></div>汾阳之烈，在暧而庆弥长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318129_comment'></div>维《思齐》之功，有开必先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318129_comment'></div>维立政之辅，垂宪乃后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318129_comment'></div>约軝错衡之来假，和铃鞗革之有光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318129_comment'></div>告于文人，仍维师真王之秩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318129_comment'></div>介以繁祉，绵重圭累衮之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318129_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1318129_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318130' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318130' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318130?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢堂父奕昌特赠太师追封魏王诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1267年正月己丑朔辛丑）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318130")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318130_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318130'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318130'>敕：《我将》式文王之典，资时使领之贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318130_comment'></div>《崧高》褒申伯之功，溥予祭馂之惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318130_comment'></div>惟宗祀以教孝，用笃亲而兴仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318130_comment'></div>具官某故父某，大盈若冲，甚德而度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318130_comment'></div>裳华有章矣，尚长君退让之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318130_comment'></div>缁衣之宜兮，遵邓侯法度之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318130_comment'></div>象贤联辉于政路，骏奔陪祀于合宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318130_comment'></div>嘉乃义方，锡之悯册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318130_comment'></div>更康叔国，仍异姓王之荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318130_comment'></div>胙毕万封，衍后嗣人之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318130_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1318130_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318131' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318131' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318131?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢堂母吴氏特赠齐魏国夫人诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1267年正月己丑朔辛丑）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318131")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318131_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318131'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318131'>敕：《崧高》维翰之功，推本生贤之庆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318131_comment'></div>《召南》积行之美，端由正始之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318131_comment'></div>朕命贤戚而镇京师，秩禋祀而敷馂泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318131_comment'></div>异数密联于政路，徽章申贲于母仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318131_comment'></div>具官某故母某氏，文献名臣之家，柔嘉女士之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318131_comment'></div>礼共蘩沼，屏流水游龙之华；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318131_comment'></div>教属芝庭，衍袭紫传龟之祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318131_comment'></div>蝉嫣万石之赉，鸿渐两社之班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318131_comment'></div>绥辑王畿，凝皇皇奠枕之绩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318131_comment'></div>肃祗使领，俨峨峨奉璋之容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318131_comment'></div>眷义训以有原，谅孝思之追远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318131_comment'></div>锦囊象轴，大国兼齐魏之封；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318131_comment'></div>翟茀鱼轩，千载垂陶孟之范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318131_comment'></div>告之祢庙，铭之鼎彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318131_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1318131_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年正月戊申</a>　帝诣太学，行舍采礼，以曾参、孔伋升十哲之位，配食大成。应麟撰乐章二首。作品：酌献曾参郕国公。孔伋沂国公乐章。<span class='inlineComment2'>（应麟撰曾参孔伋配食大成乐章二首，即《酌献曾参郕国公》、《酌献孔伋沂国公》，第二篇非《孔伋沂国公二首》，当为点校者之误。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年2月乙丑</a>　因与帝阙相之论忤似道。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年2月</a>　草诏。作品：资政殿学士江万里上表辞免同知枢密院事不允仍断来章批答。<div id='poem_1318041' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318041' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318041?labeling=true' target='_blank'>资政殿学士江万里上表再辞免同知枢密院事不允断来章批答诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1267年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318041")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318041_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318041'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318041'>省表具知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318041_comment'></div>朕惟文事必有武备，圣人经纶之学，《易》为之原，于《萃》曰「戒不虞」，于《既济》曰「思患豫防」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318041_comment'></div>以几深之略，图久大之规，卿素学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318041_comment'></div>在我烈考，未究远猷，用敷遗于冲人，登贰宥密，庶几本强而精神折冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318041_comment'></div>厥有嘉言，以教告朕曰：戎情之往来叵测，边备之科琐当严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318041_comment'></div>乃言维服，尚式《萃》、《既济》之训，协谋筹幄，日申儆以讨军实，时閒暇以明政刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318041_comment'></div>率惟敉功，昭乃辟之有乂，亦有无穷之闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318041_comment'></div>懋哉，钬予时命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318041_comment'></div>所辞宜不允，仍断来章。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1318041_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年3月</a>　兼侍立修注官，权直学士院，以明堂恩数转官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年3月</a>　草制。作品：吕文德依前少保宁武保康军节度使荆湖安（抚）制置大使屯田大使兼四川策应大使兼荆鄂州军州事兼管内劝农营田使兼侍卫马军都指挥使霍邱郡开国公加食邑七百户食实封三百户制。<div id='poem_1318072' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318072' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318072?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吕文德依前少保宁武保康军节度使荆湖安抚制置大使屯田大使兼四川策应大使兼荆鄂州军州事兼管内劝农营田使兼侍卫马军都指挥使霍丘郡开国公加食邑七百户食实封三百户制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1267年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318072")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318072_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318072'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318072'>门下：朕祗承景命，懋敬肇禋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318072_comment'></div>定郊祀而允集坛，稽正月于汉典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318072_comment'></div>见宗祖而躬执礼，参元日于唐仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318072_comment'></div>乾度昭清，坤仪肃穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318072_comment'></div>闻金支羽林之乐，时则兴鼙鼓之思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318072_comment'></div>观玉路辰斿之容，时则念旂常之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318072_comment'></div>既辑敛柴之贶，趣申位棘之褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318072_comment'></div>扬于昕庭，敷我馂泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318072_comment'></div>具官某器资闳毅，志槩忠纯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318072_comment'></div>来旬来宣而告成，协济攘夷之略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318072_comment'></div>有严有翼而共武，屡书敌忾之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318072_comment'></div>乃兼双节之荣，乃践贰公之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318072_comment'></div>讨军实而申儆，克壮其猷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318072_comment'></div>未阴雨而绸缪，以固吾圉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318072_comment'></div>朕惟除戎斯致孝享，治外可告神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318072_comment'></div>幸甘泉弭夕烽之虞，而参旗驰月捷之奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318072_comment'></div>盖以本强于荆土，用能表拓于蜀疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318072_comment'></div>于敉图功，其绥多福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318072_comment'></div>兹庸加劳而赐胙，亦如相祀之执膰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318072_comment'></div>爰赋增封，真畬衍食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318072_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318072_comment'></div>觐群牧而班瑞，朕率循肆类之初；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318072_comment'></div>敏戎公而锡田，尔尚迪对扬之祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318072_comment'></div>益恢茂烈，永乂嘉师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318072_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1318072_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年4月</a>　次子昌世生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年6月癸酉</a>　美人杨进封淑妃，草制。作品：杨淑妃制。<div id='poem_1318073' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318073' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318073?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨淑妃制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1267年6月癸酉）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318073")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318073_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318073'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318073'>门下：朕祗率邦彝，遹修内治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318073_comment'></div>《周南》之得淑女，正王化而厚人伦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318073_comment'></div>唐典之建列妃，赞后职而论妇礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318073_comment'></div>寅奉慈宸之训，爰登世阀之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318073_comment'></div>飏于昕朝，示我德选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318073_comment'></div>美人杨氏凝姿敏惠，迪性柔嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318073_comment'></div>图史有闻，钟袭紫传龟之庆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318073_comment'></div>言容可度，蹈佩环鸣玉之和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318073_comment'></div>展如法相之良，温其内则之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318073_comment'></div>惟朕饬己以敬，齐家在初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318073_comment'></div>眷《葛覃》《樛木》之诗，本原既正；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318073_comment'></div>凡茝若兰林之列，位号靡充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318073_comment'></div>妙简壸仪，晋联宫秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318073_comment'></div>恪助《思齐》之至养，式孚长乐之徽音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318073_comment'></div>谓象著四星，盍仰模于乾纬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318073_comment'></div>而教行九御，畴协辅于坤闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318073_comment'></div>载锡茂恩，用光懿范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318073_comment'></div>名超贤德，荣参揄翟之衣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318073_comment'></div>品视公台，绚采金章之绶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318073_comment'></div>惟时异数，若昔令猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318073_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318073_comment'></div>王假有家，天被尔禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318073_comment'></div>朕怡愉而后佐馂，尔其承视膳之恭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318073_comment'></div>朕节约而后亲蚕，尔其戒曳衣之侈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318073_comment'></div>朝夕有无私之志，夙夜有相戒之心，益衍祉于紫庭，永流芳于彤管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318073_comment'></div>可特进封淑妃。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1318073_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年8月</a>　轮对。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年8月乙丑</a>　草制。作品：嗣荣王进封福王主荣王祀事加食邑一千户食实封四百户仍令所司择日备礼册命制。<div id='poem_1318071' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318071' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318071?labeling=true' target='_blank'>嗣荣王进封福王主荣王祀事加食邑一千户食实封四百户仍令所司择日备礼册命制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1267年8月乙丑）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318071")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318071_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318071'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318071'>门下：朕绍天骏命，若昔鸿猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318071_comment'></div>建令德以屏周，昭备物之典册；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318071_comment'></div>封近亲而辅汉，开大国之土疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318071_comment'></div>惟时叔父之尊，峻极帝师之贵，名位宜加于异数，山川犹袭于旧邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318071_comment'></div>长乐慈谦，谓褒崇之未称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318071_comment'></div>先王笃爱，岂冲眇之敢忘？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318071_comment'></div>进爵分圭，涓辰涣綍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318071_comment'></div>皇叔太师与芮，秉心宽裕，迪性高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318071_comment'></div>赤舄之德硕肤，乐善不倦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318071_comment'></div>绿竹之文瑟僩，大盈若冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318071_comment'></div>阅理义以既多，服俭恭而惟一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318071_comment'></div>羽翼圣考，表仪天支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318071_comment'></div>韡韡《棠棣》之和，振振《麟趾》之厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318071_comment'></div>肆予承序，立敬在初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318071_comment'></div>康叔之属独尊，助兹宅命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318071_comment'></div>东平之恩莫比，诏以弗名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318071_comment'></div>载锡宠光，未隆体貌，何以遹追于先志，盖尝参绎于前规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318071_comment'></div>仁祖爱定邸之贤，更封于镇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318071_comment'></div>哲庙殊曹国之眷，赐履于荆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318071_comment'></div>皆由《下武》之孝思，推为《行苇》之内睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318071_comment'></div>率循彝宪，可后徽章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318071_comment'></div>是用瑑金玺而胙真王，焘赤社以介景福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318071_comment'></div>三山寰宇，徽号肇新；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318071_comment'></div>双节斋坛，多仪惟旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318071_comment'></div>寅念寝园之奉，具严烝祫之修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318071_comment'></div>盛德百世祀，虞丕衍统承之庆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318071_comment'></div>眉寿千岁保，鲁茂迎昌炽之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318071_comment'></div>仍董正于宗盟，并丰陪于采邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318071_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318071_comment'></div>九经尊位以重禄，必先诸父之亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318071_comment'></div>万年惟王永保民，尚式庶邦之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318071_comment'></div>与宋无极，纯嘏是常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318071_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1318071_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年10月庚申</a>　复开州，草诏。作品：赐吕文德收复开州江面肃清奖谕诏。<div id='poem_1318044' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318044' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318044?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐吕文德收复开州江面肃清奖谕诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸淳三年十一月十一日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318044")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318044_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318044'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318044'>敕文德：朕懋《采薇》治外之勤，谨彻桑未雨之备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318044_comment'></div>日申儆军实，无竞维人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318044_comment'></div>天毖我成功，所助者顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318044_comment'></div>狡焉鞑寇，窃据开城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318044_comment'></div>裒凶鞠顽，弗顾佛狸之谶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318044_comment'></div>折冲厌难，靡忘钜鹿之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318044_comment'></div>卿策虑通于神明，忠忱卫于社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318044_comment'></div>奋鹰扬之勇，卯诏辰行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318044_comment'></div>率虎阚之师，风驱霆击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318044_comment'></div>我环攻而气倍，彼株困而技穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318044_comment'></div>旃裘之援莫前，金汤之险旋复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318044_comment'></div>肤公甚隽，胜势用张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318044_comment'></div>巴夔西土之喉衿，既克敉定；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318044_comment'></div>襄峡上流之唇齿，犹肆窥觎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318044_comment'></div>恃吾有以待之，惟卿独能平尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318044_comment'></div>以身督战，先事候情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318044_comment'></div>百将一心，凡履屐间当任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318044_comment'></div>四牡三捷，从枕席上过师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318044_comment'></div>运奇伐谋，并力逐北，俾投鞭之丑远遁，而阻隘之群一空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318044_comment'></div>汔奏肃清之勋，深嘉捍御之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318044_comment'></div>荆州通蜀而用武，朕方观葛亮之规模；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318044_comment'></div>江浒出军而告成，卿尚图召虎之事业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318044_comment'></div>益恢疆宇，丕耀旂常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318044_comment'></div>故兹奖谕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1318044_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年10月甲戌</a>　大雷电。应麟奏言忤似道，似道斥逐之意遂决。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年10月</a>　除秘书少监。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年10月</a>　升兼侍讲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年10月</a>　上疏论市舶，不报。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年11月</a>　进讲《毛诗》、《礼记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年11月</a>　除起居舍人，兼权中书舍人，书行吏右礼工房。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年11月</a>　经筵进读《孝宗宝训》终篇，转朝请郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年12月</a>　以柱史故事在牒閤门直前奏对，二史直前之制遂废。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年</a>　与右相叶梦鼎以文章政事荐孙枝子璹于朝，命知临海县事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年</a>　谢枋得自兴国军贬所放还，除史馆。草诰。作品：谢枋得特授秘书省著作郎兼权司封郎诰。<div id='poem_1318095' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318095' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318095?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢枋得特授秘书省著作郎兼权司封郎诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1267年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318095")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318095_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318095'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318095'>敕具官某：《春秋》成而乱贼惧，作执秩以正官，用能一战策勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318095_comment'></div>朕崇奖气节之士，兼史职郎选而命之，庶有厌难折冲之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318095_comment'></div>尔以鲠直忤大奸，义形于色，为一乡之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318095_comment'></div>广信控风寒要冲，惟季梁在随，楚不敢谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318095_comment'></div>忠信行乎州里，隐然金汤之固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318095_comment'></div>是用进长承明，兼组主爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318095_comment'></div>凡抟力之法，捍城之备，暨守臣共图之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318095_comment'></div>既克有定，谓尔来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318095_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1318095_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1268&endYear=1268')">1268年闰正月</a>　草诏。作品：科举诏。<div id='poem_1318039' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318039' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318039?labeling=true' target='_blank'>科举诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1268年闰正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318039")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318039_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318039'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318039'>敕门下：国家用儒之效，与三代比隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318039_comment'></div>朕绍休圣绪，于今四年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318039_comment'></div>粤若恭默之时，亦既选士，未遑亲策，兹将进于庭而问焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318039_comment'></div>仰惟仁祖临轩之初，太史奏云瑞，名臣辈出，施之事业，硕大光明，朕甚慕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318039_comment'></div>先帝道久仁洽，凡今宗工献臣，莫非丰芑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318039_comment'></div>涵濡之泽，燕诒我后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318039_comment'></div>顾惟天下之才无穷，而对□之亦有无穷之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318039_comment'></div>思昔敷纳以言，明试以功，兴贤兴能，出长入治，所取皆有用之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318039_comment'></div>爰自以文设科，视古寖异，然经术词章所以觇济时之蕴，徒文乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318039_comment'></div>学问粹而器识宏，其文浑厚雅正，实用于是乎见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318039_comment'></div>朕既临雍，表章儒先，首善崇化，以风四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318039_comment'></div>矧景运维新，协乎五纬聚奎之岁，尔多士其必跃然兴起矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318039_comment'></div>盖饬操履以培其本，明理义以浚其原，勿事穿凿，勿尚浮靡，以称作人之实意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318039_comment'></div>群有司尚亦公尔考择，明尔鉴裁，俾抱负器能之士，惟朕时举，庶得贤立太平之业，式克迪前人光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318039_comment'></div>其率朕志无斁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1318039_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1268&endYear=1268')">1268年</a>　除秘阁修撰，主管建康府崇禧观。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1268&endYear=1268')">1268年夏</a>　梦游真逸阁，撰记。作品：真逸阁记。<div id='poem_1318241' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318241' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318241?labeling=true' target='_blank'>真逸阁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1268年夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318241")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318241_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318241'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318241'>子王子自柱下史免归，为句曲山祠官，夏日憩北窗，梦游其处，一道士延入精舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318241_comment'></div>凝尘满席，惟有《道德经》一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318241_comment'></div>翻首章问焉，道士曰：「无者感而寂，未尝无也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318241_comment'></div>有者寂而感，未尝有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318241_comment'></div>頠也晏也，以有无言道，而道隐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318241_comment'></div>且子不闻华阳隐居之诗乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318241_comment'></div>架上取《梁书》传读之，至夷甫散诞、平叔谈空之语，洒然悟曰列仙之儒，知道若隐居鲜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318241_comment'></div>古之博大真人，尹、聃是也，而诞者非真；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318241_comment'></div>言中伦，行中虑，是曰逸民，而空者非逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318241_comment'></div>为诞且空者谓万有皆无，独以埶利为真有而身殉之，邪说波流，变华而夷，极于梁而后止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318241_comment'></div>《易》曰『知几其神乎』，隐居有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318241_comment'></div>世以隐居比子房，盖有经世之学者为能遗世而立于独，蝉脱滓浊，不以富贵撄其心，宁学曳尾之龟而不嗅骄饵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318241_comment'></div>彼谓山中宰相者，陋哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318241_comment'></div>言未既，蘧然觉，起至户外，有黄冠来谒，视其刺，寿圣观石宗玉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318241_comment'></div>进而言曰：「观在宝龟寺山，隐居传云尝诣鄮县育王塔，自誓受五大戒，是山盖尝游息焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318241_comment'></div>今新三层楼，放𢘍永元旧筑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318241_comment'></div>上曰真逸，以奉肖像，傲松在其中，伴云在其下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318241_comment'></div>储清联邃，轶埃风而凌倒景，恍如金陵、华阳之天，与三茅君拱揖，不知犹吾鄞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318241_comment'></div>尝闻故老言，吾邦山远水秀，神仙攸宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318241_comment'></div>鄞大里黄公茹芝肥遁者也，鄞之东有梅山，子真避世之地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318241_comment'></div>浮海至翁洲，安期生之遗迹可寻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318241_comment'></div>楼上松风谡谡，如闻吹笙声，意者隐居乘飙车羽轮，从二三子期汗漫于九垓之外，其亦乐于斯乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318241_comment'></div>愿纪其事，与山石无极」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318241_comment'></div>子王子谢不能，因语其梦，遂笔而为记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1318241_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1269&endYear=1269')">1269年12月</a>　依旧职差知徽州。以父讳近州名辞免，不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年7月</a>　除秘书监，兼权中书舍人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年7月</a>　刘克庄、汤汉卒，陈合、冯梦得适以故去，似道始曰非伯厚不可，因是有诏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年10月</a>　转朝散大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年10月</a>　解郡组造朝供职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年10月</a>　书行吏右礼刑房，兼国史院编修、实录院检讨官、兼侍讲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年10月</a>　进讲《礼记》、《大学》，读《九朝通略》、《通鉴纲目》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年11月</a>　除起居郎，仍权中书舍人，兼权礼部侍郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年12月己亥</a>　谢方叔特叙复元官职惠国功致仕，作制。作品：谢方叔特授特进依前观文殿大学士惠国功致仕加食邑食实封制。<div id='poem_1318069' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318069' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318069?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢方叔特授特进依前观文殿大学士惠国公致仕加食邑食实封制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1271年12月己亥）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318069")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318069_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318069'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318069'>门下：嗣德罔不在初，惟忠厚为家法；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318069_comment'></div>旧人丕克远省，惟爵齿为达尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318069_comment'></div>顾予缵图，受命施惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318069_comment'></div>敬休亿万载，燕及皇天；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318069_comment'></div>咨尔二三臣，既右烈考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318069_comment'></div>乃眷垂车之佚，诞朌锡位之荣，绎于师虞，扬以涣号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318069_comment'></div>金紫光禄大夫具官谢方叔，闳深而耆艾，忱裕而粹夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318069_comment'></div>经德不回，凛松柏后凋之操；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318069_comment'></div>秉心无竞，参圭璋特达之纯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318069_comment'></div>曩宅揆以奋庸，善守文而持正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318069_comment'></div>仲山之明且哲，以保其身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318069_comment'></div>孟轲之致为臣，皆有所式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318069_comment'></div>行愿素履之吉，受祉黄发之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318069_comment'></div>法空谷之自持，藐浮云之何慕？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318069_comment'></div>惟今立政，稽古尚贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318069_comment'></div>未遑设几以须，若仁祖遇衍之礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318069_comment'></div>必有进官之宠，若哲庙待绛之彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318069_comment'></div>联华一品之阶，冠序群公之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318069_comment'></div>遹观故事，实非上宰以不除；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318069_comment'></div>用奖耆儒，庶乎清风之咸耸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318069_comment'></div>仍延恩之遝职，增奉邑之新畬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318069_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318069_comment'></div>践阼而问丹书，朕既迪周王之训；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318069_comment'></div>箴国而作懿戒，尔益逾卫武之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318069_comment'></div>俾寿而臧，有猷则告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318069_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1318069_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年</a>　草诰。作品：昝万寿特授复州团练使知嘉定府兼成都路安抚副使诰。<div id='poem_1318104' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318104' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318104?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昝万寿特授复州团练使知嘉定府兼成都府路安抚副使诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸淳七年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318104")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318104_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318104'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318104'>敕具官某：率宁人，有指疆土，尤重嘉师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318104_comment'></div>谨侯度，修尔戎兵，其惟良将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318104_comment'></div>懋简折冲之绩，诞敷进律之褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318104_comment'></div>尔挺志忠纯，受才沈毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318104_comment'></div>壮谋定金城之略，雄棱憺玉门之关，统戎沔阳而威信孚，宅牧泸水而保障固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318104_comment'></div>肆畴咨于虓虎，俾易镇于犍为，正秩戎团，仍贰帅阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318104_comment'></div>惟严于备御则江流靖，惟勤于抚绥则民心安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318104_comment'></div>往奏肤公，祗若明训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318104_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1318104_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年2月癸巳</a>　谢方叔卒，赠少师。草诰。作品：谢方叔特赠少师诰。<div id='poem_1318117' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318117' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318117?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢方叔特赠少师诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（咸淳八年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318117")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318117_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318117'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318117'>敕：旧人丕远省，甫攽休复之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318117_comment'></div>一老不慭遗，亟揽馀忠之奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318117_comment'></div>聿怀耆彦，载锡悯章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318117_comment'></div>具官某秉心纯明，制行果毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318117_comment'></div>振直声于言路，迪简先帝之知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318117_comment'></div>耸雅望于政途，遂登上相之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318117_comment'></div>裕于进退，介以寿臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318117_comment'></div>致为臣而归，从容知止；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318117_comment'></div>虽尔身在外，注想询猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318117_comment'></div>念未踰卫武之年，曷弗瘉平津之疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318117_comment'></div>惟德爵齿昔所难兼，若耇成人今其馀几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318117_comment'></div>九京不可作已，亚师于以赠之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318117_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318117_comment'></div>就珍从以乞言，嗟清规之已远；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318117_comment'></div>及生存而加綍，慨荣命之不先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318117_comment'></div>礼貌其隆，始终无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318117_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1318117_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年</a>　转朝散大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年6月丁酉</a>　草诰。作品：章鑑特授端明殿学士同签枢密院事诰。<div id='poem_1318084' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318084' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318084?labeling=true' target='_blank'>章鉴特授端明殿学士同签书枢密院事诰<span class='inlineComment2'>（外制掖垣藁，以下同。　咸淳八年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1272年6月丁酉）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318084")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318084_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318084'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318084'>敕：祗勤外治，劼毖中枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318084_comment'></div>以敉宁武功，倚群贤之强本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318084_comment'></div>惟几康弼直，咨同德之合谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318084_comment'></div>迪简荩臣，诞扬明命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318084_comment'></div>具官某器裕而守正，识融而履纯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318084_comment'></div>中外不倚不流，得诸涵养之厚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318084_comment'></div>学问如磨如琢，从我新益之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318084_comment'></div>俊心灼知，贤业可大，乃践争臣之列，乃仪常伯之联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318084_comment'></div>绳愆格其非，出纳惟允；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318084_comment'></div>陈善谓之敬，就将有光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318084_comment'></div>察其忠嘉，宜在宥密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318084_comment'></div>念《采薇》守卫之策，正彻桑绸缪之时，风寒严护于江淮，月捷冀清于襄岘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318084_comment'></div>有常立武，无竞维人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318084_comment'></div>若颐浩由天官而升，若晏殊以宫寀之旧，俾陪借箸之画，式协推车之忱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318084_comment'></div>班书殿而总要经，爵躬圭而增多邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318084_comment'></div>其赞帷幄筹之运，以成道德威之强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318084_comment'></div>噫，在元祐则岩叟谠言，用君子而保国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318084_comment'></div>在中兴则臣鼎远虑，申军律而治兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318084_comment'></div>共济民谟，克迈前哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318084_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1318084_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年7月</a>　书行吏左户房。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年</a>　元兵久围襄樊，应麟上疏极言边事，忤似道，似道复谋斥逐之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年9月</a>　祀明堂，摄左相，进玉幣爵。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='7166eafde155472eb06c9ac8885d444f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7166eafde155472eb06c9ac8885d444f");'><span id='7166eafde155472eb06c9ac8885d444f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1275')">1274-1275年</a>，52-53岁</div><div id='7166eafde155472eb06c9ac8885d444f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年12月</a>　服阕，诣临安造朝。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年正月</a>　叶梦鼎上封事，特授醴泉观使，兼侍读，不拜，草制。作品：叶梦鼎特授醴泉观使兼侍读依前少傅观文殿大学士信国公加食邑食实封制。<div id='poem_1318077' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318077' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318077?labeling=true' target='_blank'>叶梦鼎特授充醴泉观使兼侍读依前少傅观文殿大学士信国公加食邑食实封如故制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318077")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318077_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318077'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318077'>门下：朕更张初政，率吁宿儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318077_comment'></div>询黄发则罔愆，闵劳宅牧之事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318077_comment'></div>学古训乃有获，延登劝诵之联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318077_comment'></div>惟尊德乐道以有为，庶遗大投艰其求济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318077_comment'></div>勉从巽牍，诞有涣纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318077_comment'></div>具官某刚大而粹明，忱恂而闳裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318077_comment'></div>海滨大老，凛廉顽立懦之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318077_comment'></div>天下达尊，懋辅世长民之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318077_comment'></div>硕果表于群彦，灵光岿乎三朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318077_comment'></div>责难谓恭，陈尧舜之正道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318077_comment'></div>不可则止，耻由求之具臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318077_comment'></div>肆予改弦，申命赐履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318077_comment'></div>望公如望岁，允有甘棠之思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318077_comment'></div>治民如治家，丕徯黍苗之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318077_comment'></div>以楚邱之谋始壮，而东山之志不渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318077_comment'></div>股肱力汝为，不欲烦于方面；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318077_comment'></div>耆寿俊在服，其进疆于本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318077_comment'></div>念冲人道问学之初，维大臣傅德义之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318077_comment'></div>绍兴旧弼，冠延恩之职而敷经；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318077_comment'></div>淳熙耆英，领祥源之使而诏读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318077_comment'></div>若稽茂典，载锡优章，肯从我游，克迈乃训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318077_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318077_comment'></div>问丹书之敬义，毋勤师尚父表海之行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318077_comment'></div>瞻绿竹之琢磨，尚迪卫武公箴国之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318077_comment'></div>有谋则就，盍归乎来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318077_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1318077_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年正月</a>　黄万石为江西制置使，草诰。作品：黄万(百)[石]依前资政殿学士特升江西制置大使兼江西转运使诰。<div id='poem_1318097' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318097' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318097?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黄万石依前资政殿学士特升江西制置大使兼江西转运使诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（德祐元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318097")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318097_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318097'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318097'>敕：宣力四方汝为，既视恩于政路；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318097_comment'></div>在师三锡承宠，盍增重于阃权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318097_comment'></div>昔高庙之耆武功，命臣纲而镇江右，宏开制阃，特畀大名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318097_comment'></div>祗率旧章，诞敷褒律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318097_comment'></div>具官某经纶实学，开济远猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318097_comment'></div>吉甫文武宪邦，才周应变；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318097_comment'></div>孔明危难受任，志切救时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318097_comment'></div>缨冠往以扶王事之艰，投袂起以赴乡邻之急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318097_comment'></div>四郊若防制水，恃乃捍城；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318097_comment'></div>六师以修我戎，徯其卫社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318097_comment'></div>慨天堑波涛之沸，凛风寒根本之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318097_comment'></div>率四方诸侯，贲机衡之异渥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318097_comment'></div>谋中军元帅，峻弓钺之专征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318097_comment'></div>分陕之任益隆，殄虏之勋可冀，兼华漕节，植屏洪都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318097_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318097_comment'></div>元戎先十乘之行，朕欲壮中流之襟带；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318097_comment'></div>一贤制千里之难，卿其恢外御之规模。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318097_comment'></div>精神折冲则气势强，指授当任则将士励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318097_comment'></div>既克有定，聿图尔庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318097_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1318097_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年正月</a>　李庭芝筑城，草诰。作品：显谟阁直学士两淮制置使知扬州李庭芝筑城奖谕诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（按《本纪》：李庭芝筑清河城，以图来上，诏庭芝进一秩，在咸淳十年八月。惟是先生服未及禫，安有当制草诰之事？而庭之别筑他城，则《本纪》及《传》无考，岂下诏在隔年欤？姑附正月末，俟考。）</span><div id='poem_1318043' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318043' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318043?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐显谟阁直学士两淮安抚制置使知扬州李庭芝筑城奖谕诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1318043_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318043'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318043'>敕庭芝：朕遹骏先猷，仪图外治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318043_comment'></div>程伯之率淮浦，既立武以修戎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318043_comment'></div>山甫之城东方，爰任贤而赋政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318043_comment'></div>眷言扬土之屏翰，粤若相臣之旬宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318043_comment'></div>无竞维人，屹金汤而鼎立；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318043_comment'></div>有截其所，萃壁垒以星联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318043_comment'></div>相攸西北之隅，裒时形势之要，允怀胜算，孰赞肤功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318043_comment'></div>卿儒雅折冲，谋谟经远，增二万列屯之备，懋七年善政之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318043_comment'></div>未雨而绸缪，无日不申儆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318043_comment'></div>谓分营于箕翼，必设险于带襟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318043_comment'></div>如山之苞，控仁愿三城之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318043_comment'></div>因地之利，仿仲淹大顺之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318043_comment'></div>实墉实壑而干方，乃疆乃理而筑室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318043_comment'></div>不愆于素，伻来以图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318043_comment'></div>召伯有成，王心则宁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318043_comment'></div>载嘉尔绩，鲁侯之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318043_comment'></div>海邦是若，永乂我民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318043_comment'></div>故兹奖谕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1318043_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年正月</a>　李庭芝制置淮东，擢陆秀夫为参议官，草诰。作品：陆秀夫特授淮东提刑兼淮东制置使参议官诰。<span class='inlineComment2'>（按《陆秀夫传》云咸淳十年擢参议官，或赐诰在隔年欤？姑附正月末，俟考。）</span><div id='poem_1318103' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318103' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318103?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陆秀夫特授淮东提刑兼淮东制置使参议官诰</a><span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318103'>敕具官某：古者兵刑一致，猾夏奸宄皆士官所惩，献馘献囚皆鲁泮之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318103_comment'></div>尔以通材敏议，久参阃画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318103_comment'></div>淮东祥刑使者缺，命尔受我嘉师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318103_comment'></div>察狱以情，斯可一战；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318103_comment'></div>乘轺飞檄，尔实兼之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318103_comment'></div>审谳洗冤，筹边决胜，所以拯黎元之命者在此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318103_comment'></div>往钦哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318103_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1318103_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年2月甲辰</a>　高达检校少保，草制。作品：高达检校少保依前宁江节度左金吾卫上将军荆湖北路制置副使兼安抚使马步军都总管府兼知江陵军府事兼管内劝农营田使节制知本府屯戍军马固始郡开国公加食邑食实封制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年2月</a>　草制。作品：孙虎臣授清远军节度使加食邑食实封制。<div id='poem_1318079' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318079' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318079?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙虎臣特授清远军节度使加食邑食实封制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318079")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318079_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318079'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318079'>门下：朕注意戎昭，疚怀边琐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318079_comment'></div>赐诸侯弓钺，用进律于有功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318079_comment'></div>建大将鼓旗，爰设坛而具礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318079_comment'></div>告尔多士，扬于明廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318079_comment'></div>具官某志概忠纯，器资宏毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318079_comment'></div>有御侮折冲之略，援桴鼓则忘身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318079_comment'></div>有牧人御众之才，执干戈而卫社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318079_comment'></div>式固吾圉，屡奏肤公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318079_comment'></div>击楫誓中原之清，矫矫冠军之勇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318079_comment'></div>鸣剑驰伊吾之志，洸洸敌忾之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318079_comment'></div>愤犬羊之跳梁，率熊罴而攘却。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318079_comment'></div>表撑里拓，严保障于海陵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318079_comment'></div>左弭右鞬，瞻威棱于江浒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318079_comment'></div>庶几报彭衙之役，岂止复雁门之踦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318079_comment'></div>淮浦修我戎，倚招携而讨叛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318079_comment'></div>师中承天宠，盍懋赏以陟明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318079_comment'></div>膺将军跽毂之荣，锡融水齐旄之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318079_comment'></div>增封多衍，食邑真畬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318079_comment'></div>以旌细柳坚壁之勤，以恢《采薇》治外之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318079_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318079_comment'></div>边境功名在良将，朕惟奖励于忠忱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318079_comment'></div>兵事节度皆付公，尔亟肃清于氛祲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318079_comment'></div>祗若兹训，捍我于艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318079_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1318079_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年2月庚申</a>　贾似道溃师江上，畿甸震动。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年2月丙寅</a>　趣文天祥入卫，草诏。作品：赐文天祥诏。<div id='poem_1318061' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318061' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318061?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐文天祥诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年2月丙寅）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1318061'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318061'>卿倡义旅以卫王室，秉忠忱以济时艰，爰咨常伯之英，趣膺制阃之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318061_comment'></div>将士用命，遂汛扫于虏氛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318061_comment'></div>精神折冲，益振扬于胜气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318061_comment'></div>孔嘉体国之志，亟奏攘夷之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318061_comment'></div>元戎先行，周邦咸喜，载加锡赉，式示眷怀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1318061_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年2月庚午</a>　令夏贵以所部兵入卫，草诏。作品：赐夏贵诏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年2月</a>　令昝万寿将兵入卫。作品：赐昝万寿诏。<div id='poem_1318053' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318053' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318053?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐昝万寿诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318053")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318053_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318053'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318053'>敕万寿：自丑虏饮江，荐食近畿，国势岌岌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318053_comment'></div>秋风已动，后忧方大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318053_comment'></div>卿忠义谋略，名冠西川，虏所畏者惟卿耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318053_comment'></div>缨冠投袂，以救国家之急，此卿之志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318053_comment'></div>吾与嗣君简注已久，屡颁手札，又谕丞相驰书，仍遣专使衔命趣召，未知使者已达吾意否乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318053_comment'></div>诸将虽已进师，未有统帅，天其或者待卿以成肃清恢复之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318053_comment'></div>今再遣某官趣卿来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318053_comment'></div>卿忠忱体国，必能提精兵，率良将，取间道鼓行而前，星驰入卫，以殄灭此虏为期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318053_comment'></div>将士闻卿来朝，壮气百倍，虏不足平也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1318053_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年2月</a>　侍从班惟杨文仲，命知漳州，草诏，文仲三上章乞休致，改知泉州。作品：杨文仲特授集英殿修撰知漳州诰。<div id='poem_1318100' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318100' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318100?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨文仲特授集英殿修撰知漳州诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318100")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318100_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318100'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318100'>敕：朕选渤海贤良之守，用乂嘉师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318100_comment'></div>厌承明侍从之劳，难违雅意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318100_comment'></div>眷漳浦价藩之重，有臣熹善政之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318100_comment'></div>今得其人，乃试以政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318100_comment'></div>具官某鲁诸儒之学，周吉士之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318100_comment'></div>择乎中庸，玉瓒黄流之器；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318100_comment'></div>好是正直，朱弦清庙之音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318100_comment'></div>出奏民庸，入议禁路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318100_comment'></div>命时贰于起部，职简而清；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318100_comment'></div>咨绾长于国庠，士有所式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318100_comment'></div>方群彦聚朝而共济，慨一贤补郡之独先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318100_comment'></div>惟朕勉从，俾尔谨牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318100_comment'></div>越在外服，曷思自叶以流根；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318100_comment'></div>式是南邦，必图厚下而立本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318100_comment'></div>勿谓闽土之远，亦若周畿之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318100_comment'></div>伫闻政声，毋替猷告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318100_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1318100_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年2月</a>　吕大圭知漳州，草诰。作品：吕大圭特授祕阁修撰知漳州诰。<div id='poem_1318101' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318101' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318101?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吕大圭特授秘阁修撰知漳州诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318101")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318101_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318101'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318101'>敕具官某：朕择选良吏而宅乃牧，嘉耇成人而遂其志，体臣子民之仁一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318101_comment'></div>尔学醇行粹，为时宿儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318101_comment'></div>访予落止，入说迩英，有涵养薰陶之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318101_comment'></div>司宗惟亚，典制典选，意新才壮，何求退之果也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318101_comment'></div>漳浦价藩，尔居相迩，命尔怀二千石绶，以蓬阁论撰荣其归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318101_comment'></div>身处江湖之远，名在奎壁之躔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318101_comment'></div>《诗》云：「毋金玉尔音，而有遐心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318101_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1318101_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年3月</a>　除中书舍人，兼直学士院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年3月庚辰</a>　草诰。作品：唐震特赠华文阁待制印应雷特赠端明殿学士诰。<div id='poem_1318121' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318121' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318121?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐震特赠华文阁待制诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年3月庚辰）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318121")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318121_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318121'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318121'>敕：事君能致身，封疆之寄为重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318121_comment'></div>自古皆有死，忠义之名长存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318121_comment'></div>慨国步之斯频，嗟臣节之未厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318121_comment'></div>载嘉砥柱之操，三叹磬声之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318121_comment'></div>具官某刚毅近仁，质直好义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318121_comment'></div>河北诸郡，独有真卿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318121_comment'></div>睢阳一城，莫救许远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318121_comment'></div>孤垒危于朝露，劲气贯乎秋霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318121_comment'></div>壮矣结缨，白刃可蹈也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318121_comment'></div>哀哉握节，犀轩三襚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318121_comment'></div>乃次对于松阶，俾庙食于栾社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318121_comment'></div>锡以令谥，录其遗孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318121_comment'></div>□□□□，若中兴之褒唐重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318121_comment'></div>九京可作，尚百世以祀番君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318121_comment'></div>谅尔英魂，歆我悯典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318121_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1318121_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年3月乙酉</a>　加张世杰保康军节度使，草制。作品：张世杰特授保康军节度使左金吾卫上将军浙西制置副使兼知平江府仍旧带行枢密都承旨扬州驻劄御前诸军都统行枢督府总统一应军马加食邑食实封制。<div id='poem_1318080' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318080' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318080?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张世杰特授保康军节度使左金吾卫上将军浙西制置副使兼知平江府仍旧带行枢密都承旨扬州驻劄御前诸军都统行枢督府总统一应军马加食邑食实封制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年3月乙酉）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318080")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318080_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318080'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318080'>门下：千里之内曰畿，莫首重乎根本之地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318080_comment'></div>十国为连有帅，莫兼严平弓钺之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318080_comment'></div>惟予一人，未堪多难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318080_comment'></div>出车王事棘矣，孰式遏于要冲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318080_comment'></div>跽毂将军制之，爰畴咨于宿望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318080_comment'></div>建淑旂而分阃，敷明綍以扬廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318080_comment'></div>某官雄毅而沈潜，忠良而笃实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318080_comment'></div>帷幄决子房之胜，方略运于韬钤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318080_comment'></div>草木知万福之名，威棱憺于边境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318080_comment'></div>矫矫冠军之勇，惓惓卫上之忱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318080_comment'></div>修戈矛与同仇，志殄歼于逆虏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318080_comment'></div>儆师徒讨乱略，躬奖率于颜行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318080_comment'></div>忾缀斿之阽危，首投袂而入援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318080_comment'></div>执讯获丑，《采薇》之捷屡书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318080_comment'></div>披雾清氛，前茅之气大振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318080_comment'></div>再念吴门之危急，尝劳师律之菑攘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318080_comment'></div>却敌贤于长城，微卿民其左衽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318080_comment'></div>今堂奥之寇寖迫，而藩篱之重当严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318080_comment'></div>稽中兴名将之成规，膺右浙制垣之重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318080_comment'></div>谨固保障则常润可复，汛扫妖祲则京师以宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318080_comment'></div>克壮其猷，用锡尔祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318080_comment'></div>斋坛授钺，领巨镇于房陵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318080_comment'></div>吾臣司金，盛戎容于缇骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318080_comment'></div>以危难之间受任，以节度之事付公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318080_comment'></div>兼升牧守之荣，益强屏翰之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318080_comment'></div>衍其采邑，明我茂恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318080_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318080_comment'></div>地利不如人和，朕遹求于多助；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318080_comment'></div>武服以定王国，尔趣奏于肤公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318080_comment'></div>三军同力，以收复宇之勋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318080_comment'></div>众志成城，以集安民之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318080_comment'></div>俾金汤之不耸，永带砺之有光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318080_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1318080_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年3月</a>　赠江万里太傅、益国公，草诰。作品：江万里特赠太傅诰。<div id='poem_1318118' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318118' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318118?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江万里特赠太傅诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（德祐元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318118")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318118_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318118'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318118'>敕：多难维其棘，方加璧以趣来；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318118_comment'></div>一老不慭遗，怆《怀沙》而永逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318118_comment'></div>哀哉殄瘁，闻者䀌伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318118_comment'></div>慨念精忠，时飏悯册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318118_comment'></div>具官某文起八代之陋，学贯六经之传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318118_comment'></div>休休其心有容，得宰相体；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318118_comment'></div>蹇蹇匪躬之故，先天下忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318118_comment'></div>九龄罹偃月之谋，诸梁深如岁之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318118_comment'></div>若涉渊冰求济，尚明保予；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318118_comment'></div>猷询黄发罔愆，惟克迈训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318118_comment'></div>聿怀劝讲之助，骇闻遗札之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318118_comment'></div>寇至盍去诸，弗易子思之守；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318118_comment'></div>人莫我知已，宁从彭咸之居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318118_comment'></div>凛一节之不渝，虽百身其莫赎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318118_comment'></div>贲以苏轼之谥，襚以谢安之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318118_comment'></div>将兴百世而立懦夫，用张四维而厉臣节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318118_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318118_comment'></div>仁必有勇，嗟予失纳诲辅德之贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318118_comment'></div>义重于生，可以愧临难茍免之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318118_comment'></div>英魂未昧，茂渥其歆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318118_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1318118_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年3月</a>　陈宜中起复刘黻，草诰。作品：刘黻起复授端明殿学士知庆元府沿海制置使诰。<div id='poem_1318088' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318088' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318088?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刘黻特起复授端明殿学士知庆元府沿海制置使诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318088")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318088_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318088'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318088'>敕：朕慨思时艰，申饬外治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318088_comment'></div>陟禹迹至海表，其克诘于戎兵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318088_comment'></div>命毕公釐东郊，以谨固于封守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318088_comment'></div>眷论思之峻望，懋牧御之殊庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318088_comment'></div>赐齐履以重临，墨晋绖而强起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318088_comment'></div>某官学茂而识裕，志刚而气和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318088_comment'></div>议论通古今，动众心，介然蹇谔之操；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318088_comment'></div>文武有威风，知大体，展也经纶之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318088_comment'></div>以常伯简知于先朝，惟连率著勋于鄞水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318088_comment'></div>黍苗之泽允洽，甘棠之爱不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318088_comment'></div>虽孝思切舆骞之永怀，而民望期霸伋之再至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318088_comment'></div>矧狼心之匪茹，严鲸沫之预防，牖户阴雨之备未修，戈船下濑之师多缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318088_comment'></div>人惟求旧，戎有良翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318088_comment'></div>弓钺之锡专征，趣为朕往；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318088_comment'></div>金革之事无避，难以家辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318088_comment'></div>仁庙咨臣靖镇桂林，孝祖诏臣介帅荆岘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318088_comment'></div>事维孔棘，礼有从权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318088_comment'></div>是用隮峻职于承明，耸雄棱于制阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318088_comment'></div>即里门而视印，冀溟渤之澄波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318088_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318088_comment'></div>精神强本折冲，既念移忠之义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318088_comment'></div>喉舌赋政于外，益图敉武之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318088_comment'></div>勿迟其行，式克用乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318088_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1318088_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年3月</a>　草诰。作品：文天祥特授集英殿修撰都承旨依旧江西安抚副使诰。<div id='poem_1318093' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318093' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318093?labeling=true' target='_blank'>文天祥特授集英殿修撰枢密都承旨依旧江西安抚副使诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318093")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318093_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318093'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318093'>敕具官某：多难维其棘矣，有嘉卫上之忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318093_comment'></div>来朝又何予之，载锡在师之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318093_comment'></div>脂车趣驾，进律敷恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318093_comment'></div>尔才裕经纶，器兼文武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318093_comment'></div>以皋伊冠伦之望，有管乐济时之猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318093_comment'></div>纠合义师，欲以身任国家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318093_comment'></div>感愤外患，不以贼遗君父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318093_comment'></div>忧分阃，畀重弓，导旨预前，筹之画□。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318093_comment'></div>朕方旰食而虑，尔盍夜衣而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318093_comment'></div>知当缨冠投袂之时，正如奉瓮沃釜之急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318093_comment'></div>用隮华于书殿，俾视渥于从涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318093_comment'></div>修戈矛与同仇，亟其入觐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318093_comment'></div>运帷幄而决胜，尚赖协谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318093_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1318093_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年4月</a>　内殿奏对，暂权给事中、吏部尚书，兼掌外制，书行吏左户兵刑房。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年4月</a>　正谢，赐紫金鱼袋，兼同修国史、实录院同修撰，兼侍读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年4月</a>　上疏陈十事，曰急征讨，曰明政刑，曰万廉耻，曰通下情，曰求将才，曰练军实，曰备粮饷，曰举实才，曰择牧守，曰防海道。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年4月甲辰</a>　以高斯得言加赠江万里太师，谥文忠。草诰。作品：江万里特赠太师诰。<div id='poem_1318119' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318119' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318119?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江万里特赠太师诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年4月甲辰）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318119")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318119_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318119'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318119'>敕：君子式黄发，莫重乎德齿之尊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318119_comment'></div>圣人有金城，莫难乎节义之守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318119_comment'></div>嗟予大老，逢此鞠凶，用震悼于朕心，肆表章其芳烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318119_comment'></div>具官某浩气刚直，德性高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318119_comment'></div>孤忠自持，屡堕林甫偃月之计；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318119_comment'></div>特立不倚，靡附贾充夕阳之奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318119_comment'></div>盍归乎来，克迈乃训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318119_comment'></div>若金用砺，方咨汝说之贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318119_comment'></div>怀瑾握瑜，永慨灵均之恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318119_comment'></div>御事罔或耆寿，其天不吊慭遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318119_comment'></div>哀哉歼良，潸焉出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318119_comment'></div>彼误国不死，适以遗臭万年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318119_comment'></div>维杀身成仁，凛乎生气千载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318119_comment'></div>襚师垣之极品，贲哀敛之殊荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318119_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318119_comment'></div>三公唯其人，怅失扶颠持危之助；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318119_comment'></div>九原如可作，尚兴廉顽立懦之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318119_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1318119_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年4月乙卯</a>　刘师勇复常州，以姚訔知常州，草诰。作品：姚訔特授带行太府寺丞依旧知常州诰。<div id='poem_1318096' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318096' class='poemTitle </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318096")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318096_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318096'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318096'>敕具官某：毗陵控风寒之冲，浙河以西，若防之制水，恃为屏翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318096_comment'></div>狡虏侵轶亡谋，壹大治之，则可以固吾圉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318096_comment'></div>厌难折冲，惟良二千石是赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318096_comment'></div>尔以世臣居是邦，即家剖符，义概奋发，且战且守，服劳维多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318096_comment'></div>外府转丞，示我陟明之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318096_comment'></div>益坚捍御，亟奏肤公，朕将有懋赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318096_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1318096_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年4月己酉</a>　命刘师勇守平江，草诰。作品：刘师勇特授左武大夫依前濠州团练使带御器械平江府驻劄诸军都统制诰。<div id='poem_1318116' class='_poem'><div class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318116")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div
