class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318116_comment'></div>具官某俶傥扶义，雄烈逸群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318116_comment'></div>统率戈船，既振威于海道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318116_comment'></div>训齐武旅，爰养锐于毗陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318116_comment'></div>趋潜师而进吕城，欲乘势而复京口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318116_comment'></div>中权后劲，冒矢石以身先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318116_comment'></div>彼竭我盈，詟旃裘而胆落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318116_comment'></div>执讯获丑，敌忾献功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318116_comment'></div>载嘉后亭桥之奇勋，峻隮东山阁之华秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318116_comment'></div>伫奏肃清之捷，嗣膺褒擢之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318116_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1318116_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年4月丙辰</a>　诏夏贵入卫。草二诏。作品：赐淮西制置大使夏贵奖谕诏。<div id='poem_1318045' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318045' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318045?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐淮西制置大使夏贵奖谕诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年4月丙辰）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318045")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318045_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318045'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318045'>敕夏贵：朕惟盛夏逾半，分阴易流，诸路勤王兵已集，望卿奖三军以清江面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318045_comment'></div>惟长淮以西，倚卿为金城，守庐复巢，通北江之咽喉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318045_comment'></div>屡战屡捷，丑虏胆寒，进师濡和，则建业、当涂有克复之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318045_comment'></div>奏六月之肤公，报先帝之殊遇，在此行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318045_comment'></div>卿谓水陆并进，随机用事，知勇明决，允契朕心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318045_comment'></div>亟其合熊罴之士，扫蛇豕之穴，献俘清庙，饮至京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318045_comment'></div>宗社生民之福，岂惟予一人以宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318045_comment'></div>故兹奖谕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1318045_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年4月丙辰</a>　诏夏贵入卫。草二诰。作品：夏松特赠保康军节度使诰。<div id='poem_1318126' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318126' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318126?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夏松特赠保康军节度使诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年4月丙辰）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318126")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318126_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318126'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318126'>敕：事君能致身，封疆之臣尤重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318126_comment'></div>自古皆有死，忠义之誉长存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318126_comment'></div>聿怀磬声之思，载锡轩襚之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318126_comment'></div>具官某威名济于世美，兵略得于家传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318126_comment'></div>裕父功惟我有臣，如李愬之在唐室；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318126_comment'></div>若内举皆堪为将，如曹玮之在本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318126_comment'></div>慨丑虏之窥江，统师干而捍寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318126_comment'></div>搴旂者数矣，勇不顾身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318126_comment'></div>缨冠而救之，志于殉国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318126_comment'></div>嗟将星之遽殒，凛义气之如生，授齐钺以饰尔终，赐令谥以褒尔节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318126_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318126_comment'></div>加等而葬许穆，重恻我心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318126_comment'></div>登坛而拜淮阴，莫追既往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318126_comment'></div>英魂未昧，茂渥其歆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318126_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1318126_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年4月丁卯</a>　李庭芝率所部郡县扼守日，调苗再成战其南，许文德战其北，姜才战其中，将士用命。丁卯，加李庭芝参加政事。草五诏。作品：赐李庭芝奖谕诏。李庭芝特授参知政事依旧淮东安抚制置大使兼知扬州淮西策应大使诰。姜才依前右武大夫特授扬州防御使依旧建康府驻劄御前诸军都统制诰。许文德特授扬州观察使依旧知淮安州淮东安抚使兼淮东策应使诰。苗再成特授拱卫大夫依前知□州防禦除带行御器械知真州诰。<div id='poem_1318048' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318048' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318048?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐李庭芝奖谕诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年4月丁卯）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318048")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318048_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318048'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318048'>敕庭芝：朕未堪多难，丑虏率我蟊贼以来，荡摇我边疆，狡焉窥淮之谋，将塞馈饷之途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318048_comment'></div>卿以股肱之良，任方面之重，激昂将士，指授方略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318048_comment'></div>维时熊罴不二心之臣，合谋同力，人百其勇，誓必剪灭虏而朝食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318048_comment'></div>师直为壮，天助者顺，大捷于湾头，再捷于淮安，三捷于宝应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318048_comment'></div>执讯获丑，来奏肤公，威棱赫张，可以舒华夏之气，詟旃裘之胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318048_comment'></div>卿为东陲金城，修捍于艰，以集隽功，朕维宠嘉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318048_comment'></div>乘战胜之威，扫妖垒而空之，则卿之勋业暨诸将功名，昭垂竹帛，于《常武》淮浦之诗有光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318048_comment'></div>其益励忠臣义士，坚守于内，力战于外，纠合精锐，霆击风驱，壹大治之，使匹马只轮无返者，用成攘夷复境之丕绩，朕所望于诗书之帅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318048_comment'></div>战多之赏，已视功行之，指期肃清，高爵厚秩无所吝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318048_comment'></div>比尔将士，咸体朕意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318048_comment'></div>故兹奖谕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1318048_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318085' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318085' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318085?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李庭芝特授参知政事依旧淮东安抚制置大使兼知扬州兼淮西策应大使诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（德祐元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318085")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318085_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318085'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318085'>敕：祗遹先猷，仪图哲辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318085_comment'></div>庆历彦博之参国，秉肃将河北之征师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318085_comment'></div>绍兴臣鼎之预政，除擢繇江右之大阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318085_comment'></div>乃眷干方之绩，延登鬷假之联，载锡褒纶，率循茂典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318085_comment'></div>具官某洪深而肃括，硕大而光明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318085_comment'></div>曰阃外制之，蕴知国知兵之略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318085_comment'></div>言长城远矣，兼允文允武之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318085_comment'></div>属边琐之孔艰，严风寒之谨护。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318085_comment'></div>淮浦戒我师旅，率励勤王之忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318085_comment'></div>执政犹吾股肱，灼知体国之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318085_comment'></div>朕慨《采薇》治外之急，思集蓼毖患之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318085_comment'></div>敕命惟时惟几，盍惜阴而攘却；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318085_comment'></div>继今立政立事，其揆策以赞襄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318085_comment'></div>是用擢贰台衡，仍分阃钺，以协济日万几之务，以耆定月三捷之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318085_comment'></div>旂垒如光弼之增明，廊庙有德裕而益重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318085_comment'></div>衍其采邑，壮乃威声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318085_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318085_comment'></div>东方毕公率之，虽身外而心王室；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318085_comment'></div>北伐张仲在矣，其武服以奏肤公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318085_comment'></div>无竞维人，往敬用治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318085_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1318085_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318112' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318112' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318112?labeling=true' target='_blank'>姜才依前右武大夫特授□州防御使依旧建康府驻劄御前诸军都统制诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年4月丁卯）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318112")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318112_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318112'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318112'>敕：安边境在良将，久宣敌忾之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318112_comment'></div>共武服奏肤公，式厚策勋之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318112_comment'></div>有嘉壮概，载锡褒章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318112_comment'></div>具官某果锐而好谋，忱恂而尚义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318112_comment'></div>隐若敌国，差强人意，洸洸卫上之忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318112_comment'></div>率彼淮浦，以修我戎，暨暨冠军之勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318112_comment'></div>狡焉丑类，梗我要冲，逞蛇豕以薄城，驱犬羊而犯顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318112_comment'></div>郊多垒辱也，独被发以缨冠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318112_comment'></div>鼓三军进之，乃雄心而鸣剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318112_comment'></div>先锋鏖战，入阵剿除，亟收破竹之勋，来献《采薇》之捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318112_comment'></div>威棱大振，赏典趣攽，陟使领于捍防，表戎昭之果毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318112_comment'></div>有功见知则说，用劝熊罴之臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318112_comment'></div>击虏以灭为期，尽清狐兔之穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318112_comment'></div>勉建殊绩，嗣有茂恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318112_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1318112_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318109' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318109' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318109?labeling=true' target='_blank'>许文德特授□州观察使依旧知淮安州淮东安抚副使兼淮东策应副使诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年4月丁卯）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318109")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318109_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318109'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318109'>敕：戒戎旅率淮浦，遹成却敌之隽功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318109_comment'></div>承天宠在师中，载锡策勋之懋赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318109_comment'></div>有嘉敌忾，用劝戎昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318109_comment'></div>具官某识明而志忠，谋老而气壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318109_comment'></div>憺雄棱于阃外，如虎在山；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318109_comment'></div>殿重镇于淮阴，若罴当道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318109_comment'></div>贤于长城矣，岂忧匈奴哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318109_comment'></div>慨狡虏之乱常，挟叛臣而犯顺，犬羊驱十万之众，蜩螗交四面之锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318109_comment'></div>维我屏翰之良，悉心战守之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318109_comment'></div>昼御宵击，保固金汤之疆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318109_comment'></div>电扫风除，攘殄旃裘之丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318109_comment'></div>大奏《采薇》之捷，优奖前茅之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318109_comment'></div>正使领于廉车，耸军容于方面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318109_comment'></div>既酹茂绩，益励英猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318109_comment'></div>念多垒之未清，凛东陲之孔棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318109_comment'></div>用师观衅而动，乘胜气以荡平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318109_comment'></div>击虏以灭为期，趣劲兵而应援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318109_comment'></div>式克耆定，尚有殊褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318109_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1318109_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318114' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318114' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318114?labeling=true' target='_blank'>苗再成特授拱卫大夫依前和州防御使除带行御器械知真州诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（德祐元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318114")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318114_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318114'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318114'>敕：王事多难维其棘，师克在和；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318114_comment'></div>我武维扬伐有辞，功有厚赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318114_comment'></div>某鸣剑伊吾之壮志，坚壁细柳之英标。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318114_comment'></div>自守圉于仪真，克执丑于江浒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318114_comment'></div>率劲兵而勇往，径捣妖巢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318114_comment'></div>燬列栅以无馀，连收隽捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318114_comment'></div>忠忱足以振士气，义概足以慑戎心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318114_comment'></div>贲褒律之殊荣，晋横班之峻秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318114_comment'></div>用锡尔祉，益殚拱扈之勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318114_comment'></div>立定厥功，嗣有宠褒之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318114_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1318114_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年5月甲戌</a>　命李庭芝津遣贾似道归身终丧。作品：责谕贾似道终丧诏。<div id='poem_1318049' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318049' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318049?labeling=true' target='_blank'>责谕贾似道归里终丧诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（德祐元年五月四日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318049")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318049_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318049'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318049'>敕似道：吾闻忠孝臣子之大节，命义天下之大戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318049_comment'></div>卿受国家之殊遇，居将相之重任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318049_comment'></div>迩者督师弗绩，蹙国偾军，人言沸腾，欲正其罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318049_comment'></div>吾与嗣君念卿服劳王朝，务存体貌，俾归里终丧，用彰孝治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318049_comment'></div>吾于待大臣之礼至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318049_comment'></div>闻卿安处维扬，未即就道，公议坌涌，皆谓臧孙纥如防，《春秋》大义凛如霜日，君令臣从，焉可违也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318049_comment'></div>吾维卿素以忠孝自负，必不固违吾命，以亏事君事亲之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318049_comment'></div>凡群臣所奏，姑惟置之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318049_comment'></div>今归途未阻，可以退修初服，尽礼倚庐，而犹复翱翔淮壖，忠孝胥失，进退无据，大臣出处当如是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318049_comment'></div>兹命李庭芝宣吾与嗣君忠厚之至意，卿其亟归丧次，以尽臣子之道，以弭公议之责，固当曲示保全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318049_comment'></div>否则众论益甚，名教靡容，吾虽欲屈法伸恩，而不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318049_comment'></div>卿尚明听吾言，善始以终，亦有辞于永世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318049_comment'></div>故兹诏示。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1318049_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年5月己卯</a>　草诰。作品：王柏特赠承事郎诰。<div id='poem_1318124' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318124' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318124?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王柏特赠承事郎诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年5月己卯）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318124")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318124_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318124'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318124'>敕某：朕惟正学不明，士习颓靡，人心陷溺，稔成艰危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318124_comment'></div>是用崇奖宿儒，使闻风兴起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318124_comment'></div>尔祖为淳熙名流，尔远世其家，文献渊源，博以诸老之琢磨，养粹得深，卷道不试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318124_comment'></div>从臣有请，追贲京秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318124_comment'></div>当孔棘之时，所以张四维、扶世教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318124_comment'></div>诏于幽扃，服享殊渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318124_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1318124_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年5月</a>　加张珏检[校]少保、知重庆府。草诏。作品：赐四川制置使兼知重庆府诏。<div id='poem_1318052' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318052' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318052?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐四川制置副使兼知重庆府张珏诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318052")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318052_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318052'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318052'>敕张珏：吾拥佑嗣君，未堪多难，似道误国溃师，虏祸极矣，国事急矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318052_comment'></div>以卿忠忱壮概，著勋西蜀，用授节钺，联亚保，分蜀阃之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318052_comment'></div>今戎氛逼近，其忧有重于蜀者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318052_comment'></div>已出六月之师，趣诸将进讨，犹虑气势未合，如卿义勇奋发，吾望卿来，如望岁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318052_comment'></div>同室有斗，缨冠往救；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318052_comment'></div>邻国有难，顿首出师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318052_comment'></div>卿忠义质神明，其忍坐视国家之急乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318052_comment'></div>其亟奖率三军，星驰电迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318052_comment'></div>或湖北路梗，即从间道入援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318052_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「王于兴师，修我戈矛，与子同仇」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318052_comment'></div>吾所望于熊罴不二心之臣也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1318052_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年5月庚寅</a>　勉谕王爚陈宜中诏。<div id='poem_1318056' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318056' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318056?labeling=true' target='_blank'>勉谕王爚陈宜中诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（德祐元年五月二十日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318056")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318056_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318056'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318056'>遭家不造，狄难孔棘，民自择相，我兴授之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318056_comment'></div>如光、公著皆中外之人望所冀，吁谟远猷，共济艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318056_comment'></div>今人心寖回，援兵渐集，此二相协力经纶之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318056_comment'></div>夏已逾半，正当惜分阴以图攘却，时几易失，虏谋难测，吾朝夕凛凛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318056_comment'></div>外议谓二相颇有不和之迹，览辅臣奏疏，忧爱恳切，谓定大计于危疑，诛大奸于仓卒，勋在王室，初无轻重，何嫌何疑而至是？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318056_comment'></div>吾惟丙、魏同心，房、杜济谋，在平时犹然，况危急存亡之秋乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318056_comment'></div>盍念国事之艰，协心同德，日入都堂，共议扶持宗社、拯救民生之策，勿以细故妨大计。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1318056_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年5月丙申</a>　遣使以元兵至，告天地宗庙社稷。撰文。作品：遣守臣走告南狱奏告滁州端命殿太祖皇帝神御文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：《四明文献集》分作两篇：《遣守臣奏告南狱》、《奏告滁州端命殿太祖皇帝神御》，且前篇改“走”为“奏”。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年5月己亥</a>　草诰。作品：赵與禟特赠朝请郎直华文阁诰。<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：赵與禟之“禟”，原书作“禾+唐”，据《四明文献集》改。）</span><div id='poem_1318123' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318123' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318123?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赵与禟特赠朝请郎直华文阁诰<span class='inlineComment2'>（知宁国县）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年5月己亥）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318123")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318123_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318123'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318123'>敕具官某：王事多难，孰非全躯避祸患之臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318123_comment'></div>宗子维城，独效捍敌死封疆之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318123_comment'></div>听磬声而嘅叹，锡纶命以宠褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318123_comment'></div>尔振振周公族之英，蹇蹇楚同姓之操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318123_comment'></div>志坚即墨之守，躬蹈井督之危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318123_comment'></div>方免胄以卫民，竟结缨而徇义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318123_comment'></div>伤哉贤令，罹此鞠凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318123_comment'></div>增十秩以追崇，嗟百身以莫赎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318123_comment'></div>仍跻延阁，并录孤儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318123_comment'></div>俾庙食以旌忠，尚毅魂之殄虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318123_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1318123_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年6月庚子朔</a>　日食，白昼如夜，星见，鸡鹜皆归。草诏。作品：日食求言诏。<div id='poem_1318040' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318040' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318040?labeling=true' target='_blank'>日食求言诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年6月庚子朔）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318040")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318040_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318040'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318040'>敕门下：惟天降割我家，嗣君幼冲，未堪多难，吾以衰耄，勉同听政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318040_comment'></div>明不能察奸臣之误国，仁不能救丑虏之殄民，德泽弗流，政令多失，乖气致异，适见于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318040_comment'></div>乃季夏月朔，日有食之既，阳微昼晦，变莫大焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318040_comment'></div>吾惟艰危之会，忧心如薰，重以灾异谴告，于何不臧，厥咎在吾，痛自刻责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318040_comment'></div>贬损尊号，犹恐未尽应天之实，方与嗣君夙夜祗惧，省躬悔过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318040_comment'></div>慨念奸臣专政之久，杜塞言路，蒙蔽天变，下情壅于上闻，祸至此极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318040_comment'></div>今吾大警悟、大惩艾，虚心以改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318040_comment'></div>惟人言所以达天意，咨尔百僚士庶，尽忠极言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318040_comment'></div>凡凉菲之愆，政事之疵，黎元之疾苦，爰暨攘夷固圉之长策，可以销恶运、导和气者，毋有隐讳，将采择施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318040_comment'></div>人心悦而天怒解，庶其在此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318040_comment'></div>布告中外，体吾至意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1318040_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年6月</a>　应诏言答天戒五事，陈备御十策。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年6月</a>　进读《三朝宝训》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年6月丙午</a>　言开庆之祸始于丁大全，凡大全之党在谪籍者皆勿宥。从之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年6月己酉</a>　缴还章鑑、曾渊子録黄，言韩震为逆，二人实芘之，且渊子芘翁应龙，致有逸罚，又尝窃府库金以遁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年6月庚戌</a>　削鑑一官，放归田里；渊子再削一官，徙吉州；诛翁应龙，籍其家。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年6月甲寅</a>　王爚请相留梦炎，乞以经筵备顾问，陈宜中请相梦炎，乞祠。草三制。作品：王爚依前少保特授平章军国重事一月两赴经筵五日一朝仍赴都唐议加食邑食实封制。陈宜中特授左丞相依前兼枢密使都督诸路军马加食邑食实封制。留梦炎特授宣奉大夫右丞相兼枢密使都督诸路军马加食邑食实封制。<div id='poem_1318074' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318074' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318074?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王爚依前少保特授平章军国重事一月两赴经筵五日一朝仍赴都堂议事加食邑食实封制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年6月甲寅）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318074")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318074_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318074'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318074'>门下：尊贤敬大臣，莫重乎老成典型之望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318074_comment'></div>治国平天下，莫先乎内外修攘之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318074_comment'></div>眷予宅揆之英，允有经邦之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318074_comment'></div>二人同心之助，方共济于多艰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318074_comment'></div>一日万几之繁，不欲劳以细务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318074_comment'></div>优加异数，孚告明庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318074_comment'></div>少保具官王爚，清任而和，刚大以直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318074_comment'></div>守文持正，至公以天下为心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318074_comment'></div>尊主庇民，可久则贤人之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318074_comment'></div>行藏系善类之消长，出处关时运之盛衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318074_comment'></div>惟上帝赉予，爰立作相；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318074_comment'></div>维旧人远省，惠然肯来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318074_comment'></div>定大计如砥柱之不移，折奸萌若元龟之先见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318074_comment'></div>改纪其政，遹求厥宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318074_comment'></div>道德成乎安疆，国势复振；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318074_comment'></div>将相和则豫附，人心寖回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318074_comment'></div>以敉图功，丕应徯志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318074_comment'></div>蹇蹇匪躬之故，允惟房、杜之济谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318074_comment'></div>休休其心有容，乃效皋，夔之相逊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318074_comment'></div>朕若稽元祐，图任宿儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318074_comment'></div>一老时游庙堂，咨以大政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318074_comment'></div>二相并秉钧轴，协于同寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318074_comment'></div>祗率彝章，参建硕辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318074_comment'></div>特崇耆艾之礼，俾居劳佚之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318074_comment'></div>举其宏纲，维《天保》、《采薇》之治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318074_comment'></div>询兹黄发，有《访落》、《小毖》之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318074_comment'></div>入开导于经帷，间从容于朝宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318074_comment'></div>圭腴申锡，体貌益隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318074_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318074_comment'></div>方叔克壮其猷，朕庶几复古之绩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318074_comment'></div>伊尹自任以重，卿勿替格天之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318074_comment'></div>寿俊在位则外患消，吁谟定命则治本立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318074_comment'></div>懋乃一德，登于丕平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1318074_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1318074_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318075' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318075' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318075?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈宜中特授右丞相依前兼枢密使都督诸路军马加食邑食实封制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年6月甲寅）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318075")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318075_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318075'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318075'>门下：朕思济多艰，畴咨硕望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318075_comment'></div>惟尹躬有一德，右厥辟而宅师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318075_comment'></div>惟说命总百官，置诸左而纳诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318075_comment'></div>嘉乃经纶之学，弼予宁敉之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318075_comment'></div>无竞维人，倚同心之辅政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318075_comment'></div>式序在位，协鼎足之承君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318075_comment'></div>延拜元台，诞敷垣制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318075_comment'></div>具官某德秉乎弘毅，识造乎高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318075_comment'></div>知仁勇之资，治国家而有裕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318075_comment'></div>刚大直之气，塞天地以无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318075_comment'></div>简在先皇，俾辅后嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318075_comment'></div>赞雷厉风飞之决，宗庙再安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318075_comment'></div>开否消泰长之机，纪纲一正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318075_comment'></div>定众志于缀斿之际，回治象于惊涛之冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318075_comment'></div>精神强而英隽聚朝，指授当而将士用命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318075_comment'></div>忠贯皦日，未尝言房、杜之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318075_comment'></div>计安生民，将欲复文、武之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318075_comment'></div>乃若休休有容之度，蔼然济济相逊之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318075_comment'></div>盖开忱布公之心，犹恐无助；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318075_comment'></div>而应变守文之美，其惟协恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318075_comment'></div>若昔元祐之隆，登庸成德之彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318075_comment'></div>闵劳大事，咨重事之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318075_comment'></div>仪图真儒，冠上相之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318075_comment'></div>祗遹先宪，增光前闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318075_comment'></div>六月薄伐而饬戎车，仍令督军之寄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318075_comment'></div>千里决胜而运筹幄，聿严基命之谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318075_comment'></div>以尊冢宰掌邦治之权，以懋百揆熙帝载之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318075_comment'></div>申陪邑采，丕耸岩瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318075_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318075_comment'></div>四海既平，时靡有争，朕正倚修攘之略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318075_comment'></div>三后协心，同底于道，卿益恢康济之猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318075_comment'></div>惟时惟几，以迓天休；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318075_comment'></div>惟和惟一，以凝国是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1318075_comment'></div>保大定功而干戈戢，更化善治而福禄来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1318075_comment'></div>乂我受民，钦若成烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1318075_comment'></div>可<span class='inlineComment2'>（《四明文献集》卷四。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1318075_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1318075'>事：原缺，据四库本、清抄本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1318075_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318076' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318076' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318076?labeling=true' target='_blank'>留梦炎特授宣奉大夫右丞相兼枢密使都督诸路军马加食邑食实封制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年6月甲寅）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318076")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318076_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318076'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318076'>门下：选众而举皋陶，有虞所以凝庶绩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318076_comment'></div>相右而命召奭，成周所以保受民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318076_comment'></div>迪思先皇，敷遗哲辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318076_comment'></div>运筹决胜，惟简在上帝心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318076_comment'></div>宅揆奋庸，其毖我成功所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318076_comment'></div>告尔多士，扬于大廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318076_comment'></div>某官学醇而识宏，德厚而才裕，尊王秉礼之大义，深于《春秋》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318076_comment'></div>救时行道之精忠，贯于日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318076_comment'></div>以少双寡二之望，为特立独行之儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318076_comment'></div>精神折冲，兼文武之略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318076_comment'></div>夙夜基宥，冠枢机之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318076_comment'></div>允具瞻之素孚，谓延登其已晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318076_comment'></div>栋隆不挠，硕果犹存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318076_comment'></div>南国是式，作尔庸，懋乃攸绩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318076_comment'></div>王事靡盬，不遑处，捍我于艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318076_comment'></div>欲经营四方以平夷，用奖率三军而兴汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318076_comment'></div>惟万民徯司马之入，而上宰逊王曾之来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318076_comment'></div>岂烦劝诵于经帷，咸望协熙于帝载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318076_comment'></div>矧今天变未弭，国步未宁，明黜陟所以制治保邦，修政事所以攘夷复境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318076_comment'></div>爰立作相，于敉图功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318076_comment'></div>元祐并命三贤，若纯仁之跻次辅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318076_comment'></div>绍兴总提二枋，若臣浚之督成师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318076_comment'></div>陟序崇阶，衍赋多邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318076_comment'></div>庶几真儒无敌之效，丕展良弼辅德之谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318076_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318076_comment'></div>待裴度而开延英，时惟旧人图任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318076_comment'></div>济房乔而断大事，尚冀乃僚同心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318076_comment'></div>三后协可以泽生民，众正开可以杜群枉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318076_comment'></div>指授当任则边氛静，处置得宜则国势强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318076_comment'></div>式固尔猷，克迈乃训。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1318076_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年6月己未</a>　草诰。作品：加李庭芝知枢密院事兼参知政事诰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年</a>　草诏。作品：李庭芝妻徐氏特封永国夫人诰。赐利西路安抚副使兼知涪州杨立诏。<div id='poem_1318132' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318132' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318132?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知枢密院事兼参知政事李庭芝妻徐氏特封永国夫人诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年6月己未）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318132")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318132_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318132'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318132'>敕：朕称宗祀，遹求敉功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318132_comment'></div>《常武》之修我戎，式倚筹帷之彦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318132_comment'></div>《殷雷》之劝以义，载嘉阃范之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318132_comment'></div>其锡纶言，用敷馂惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318132_comment'></div>具官某妻某氏，迪内则之训，蔼女士之芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318132_comment'></div>《鹊巢》夫人起家，助《召南》分陕之化；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318132_comment'></div>燕喜令妻受祉，集鲁邦膺狄之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318132_comment'></div>《采薇》之捷既闻，《彤管》之褒可后？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318132_comment'></div>宜其家而有誉，贵于室而特封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318132_comment'></div>翟茀鱼轩，赐沐浯溪之国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318132_comment'></div>鸾书象轴，增光衮路之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318132_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1318132_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318051' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318051' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318051?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐利西路安抚副使兼知涪州杨立诏<span class='inlineComment2'>（六月二十二日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年6月辛酉）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318051")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318051_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318051'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318051'>敕杨立：虏为不道，偷渡长江，似道督师，不战而溃，误国殄民，以至金陵、京口皆失守，妖氛延及近甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318051_comment'></div>冀四方忠臣义士，来救国难，以拯民命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318051_comment'></div>赖天之灵，辅臣协图，屏黜似道，蠲除蠹国害民之政，人心顿回，尽力战守，叛将凶酋，相继殄灭，然后宗社仅安，京师稍定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318051_comment'></div>天未悔祸，江陵之事又骇吾听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318051_comment'></div>盖邮传阻隔，未知似道已黜，是以人无固志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318051_comment'></div>惟卿智略辐辏，志气忼慨，秉忠仗义，董率精锐，进于三峡，奋勇鏖战，立功甚隽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318051_comment'></div>吾与嗣君闻之嘉叹，有臣如此，可以灭虏朝食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318051_comment'></div>望卿之来，以刻为岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318051_comment'></div>昔楚申包胥求救于秦，立庭墙勺饮不入口，况卿膺阃寄之重，必能投袂缨冠，赴国家之急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318051_comment'></div>已擢卿正廉车之任，其亟星驰露次，救我艰危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318051_comment'></div>或湖北路梗，盍取閒道，疾驰而来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318051_comment'></div>勤王奏功，吾于高爵懋赏无所吝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318051_comment'></div>故兹诏示。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1318051_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年6月辛酉</a>　草诰。作品：家铉翁依前直华文阁枢密副都承旨特授知临安府浙西安抚使诰。<div id='poem_1318099' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318099' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318099?labeling=true' target='_blank'>家铉翁依前直华文阁枢密副都承旨特授知临安府浙西安抚使诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年6月辛酉）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318099")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318099_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318099'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318099'>敕具官某：朕慨思时艰，迪简贤尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318099_comment'></div>商邑为四方之极，用谨固于本根；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318099_comment'></div>周官倡九牧之风，乃力辞于侍从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318099_comment'></div>有嘉廉逊，载锡宠褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318099_comment'></div>尔粹学融明，素履修洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318099_comment'></div>和平之政，如古循吏所称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318099_comment'></div>刚直之名，惟前文人是似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318099_comment'></div>世济其美，人皆曰贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318099_comment'></div>肆予更政化之初，命尔导宥密之命，咨日畿浩穰之寄，陟地官论思之联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318099_comment'></div>恬静之操不渝，忠谠之风可挹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318099_comment'></div>予欲成奠枕皇皇之绩，尔惟有游刃恢恢之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318099_comment'></div>强本折冲，尤难于欧、蔡承平之日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318099_comment'></div>流化自近，非但循赵、张发摘之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318099_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1318099_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年6月庚申</a>　复缴还曾渊子贬吉州録黄。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年6月癸亥</a>　曾渊子贬韶州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年7月</a>　除试尚书礼部侍郎，兼中书舍人，兼书行吏右，辞免，不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年7月庚午朔</a>　江西制置黄万石移治抚州，诏还隆兴府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年7月甲戌</a>　江西制置黄万石移治抚州，诏还隆兴府。草诏。作品：勉谕江西制置大使黄万石置司隆兴府诏。<div id='poem_1318050' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318050' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318050?labeling=true' target='_blank'>勉谕江西制置大使黄万石置司隆兴府诏<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月五日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年7月甲戌）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318050")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318050_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318050'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318050'>敕万石：昔晋庾翼移镇乐乡，王衍谓江渚有虞，不相接救，方岳重将，当居要害之地，为内外形势，言兵者韪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318050_comment'></div>今天堑失险，深入堂奥，南昌为江西一都会，襟带中流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318050_comment'></div>高庙命李纲为大使镇是邦，此中兴宏规也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318050_comment'></div>卿志虑忠实，才猷开济，属大事当一面，吾以纲之任命卿，精神折冲，人心恃以不恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318050_comment'></div>闻卿驻兵临川，气势犹未翕合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318050_comment'></div>商飙已动，分阴当惜，战守之计不容缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318050_comment'></div>卿其趣提师旅，开阃南昌，与守臣协图备御，乘机合谋，必以克复江池、肃清氛祲为期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318050_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「戎车既驾，四牡业业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318050_comment'></div>岂敢定居，一月三捷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318050_comment'></div>卿其懋哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318050_comment'></div>故兹勉谕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1318050_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年7月甲戌</a>　应麟请移贾似道鄰州。甲戌，移婺州。丁丑，徙建宁府。权直舍人方应发封还録黄，乞竄之岭南，先生与黄镛又言之，不从。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年7月辛巳</a>　草诏。作品：赐夏贵诏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年7月癸巳</a>　以夏贵知扬州，召李庭芝赴行在，夏贵不受代，李庭芝闭门自守。草诏。作品：赐李庭芝诏。<div id='poem_1318058' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318058' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318058?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐李庭芝诏<span class='inlineComment2'>（二十四日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年7月癸巳）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318058")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318058_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318058'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318058'>吾拥佑嗣君，遗大投艰于身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318058_comment'></div>丑虏凭陵，国步孔棘，妖巢狡窟，犹未扫除，西风已动，忧端方大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318058_comment'></div>卿文武为宪，精神折冲，分钺十馀年，威望具孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318058_comment'></div>卿尝有勤王之志，吾念淮壖为畿辅屏蔽，倚成攘夷复境之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318058_comment'></div>今虏氛未退，尤以根本为虑，运筹决胜，宜得知兵之儒，协赞庙谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318058_comment'></div>迩者命卿参预，意实在此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318058_comment'></div>久当方面，练习兵事，无踰卿者，用遵庆历召琦、仲淹故事，趣卿入辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318058_comment'></div>指授当任，可以破坚，处置得宜，可以平蔡，其功倍于临边矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318058_comment'></div>已命夏贵宣威两淮，趣其入维扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318058_comment'></div>贵到，卿即率良将劲兵，星驾来朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318058_comment'></div>惟时惟几，分阴不可缓，卿其念之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1318058_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年7月</a>　王爚嗾京学生刘九皋等言陈宜中擅权书，宜中径去，遣使四辈召之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年7月壬辰</a>　下九皋于临安狱。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年</a>　草诏。作品：赐左丞相陈宜中勉谕诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：原注七月二十四日。）</span>赐淮东制置大使李庭芝诏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（按：原注七月二十八日。）</span><div id='poem_1318054' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318054' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318054?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐左相陈宜中勉谕造阙诏<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月二十四日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年7月癸巳）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318054")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318054_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318054'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318054'>敕宜中：丑虏凭陵，奸臣溃败，惟卿屹然为宗社之柱石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318054_comment'></div>讨乱贼，去凶邪，收黎元之心，作将士之气，国势渐振，皆卿之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318054_comment'></div>彼何人斯，挟私肆毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318054_comment'></div>吾知此书诈也，卿何嫌何疑，翩然出关？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318054_comment'></div>命使者趣卿归造于朝，而出昼不少留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318054_comment'></div>吾与嗣君朝夕徯望，忘寝废食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318054_comment'></div>卿忠义贯日月，必恻然动心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318054_comment'></div>矧秋风已动，虏谋日深，朝堂仅一右相，科琐边事，惟卿明习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318054_comment'></div>守御孰缓孰急，将士孰勇孰怯，指授处置之方略，分阴不可缓，卿为国计，盍幡然而来？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318054_comment'></div>或不念吾老幼之茕疾，独不念先帝之殊遇乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318054_comment'></div>卿以安社稷自任，当危急存亡之秋，岂忍舍去？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318054_comment'></div>亟入政事堂，图所以攘夷复境之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318054_comment'></div>再命从臣勉谕，尚体吾恳切之意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1318054_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318046' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318046' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318046?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐淮东制置大使李庭芝奖谕诏<span class='inlineComment2'>（七月二十八日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年7月丁酉）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318046")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318046_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318046'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318046'>敕庭芝：惟天付予有家，冲眇未堪多难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318046_comment'></div>蛇豕荐食，覃及畿甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318046_comment'></div>维扬截然中居，若防制水，恃以无恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318046_comment'></div>实惟礼乐诗书之帅，秉忠忱，翰王略，且战且守，屡奏肤公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318046_comment'></div>迩者舟师不利，江氛未清，根本之谋，我用是急，趣卿入卫，强本折冲，庶几筹幄，可以决胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318046_comment'></div>奏章来谂，表撑里拓之虑甚密，申儆军实，招选劲兵，将有造国之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318046_comment'></div>朕惟宠嘉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318046_comment'></div>已命夏贵旬宣两淮，卿候贵开阃，亟率将士星驰来朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318046_comment'></div>国人望卿，如望岁焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318046_comment'></div>商飙已肃，分阴当惜，戒我师旅，不留不处，罔俾《常武》之功，专美有周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318046_comment'></div>故兹奖谕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1318046_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年7月戊戌</a>　遣使召陈宜中还朝，草诏。作品：再赐陈宜中诏。<div id='poem_1318055' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318055' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318055?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再赐陈宜中诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年7月戊戌）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318055")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318055_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318055'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318055'>吾自丞相出关，忧心如薰，屡遣使再下手诏，趣丞相造阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318055_comment'></div>闵闵如望岁，而未有来朝之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318055_comment'></div>谏臣抗疏，谓丞相当奸臣偾师之后，转危为安，勋在宗社，指授处置，诸将信服，狄难孔棘，此何时而可舍去？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318055_comment'></div>览之怃然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318055_comment'></div>维危急之秋，一木支厦，罔不曰艰大，二相协力扶持，庶克有济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318055_comment'></div>古社稷臣不轻于进退，矧受任艰难之际，不止身佩安危而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318055_comment'></div>前日之去，固知丞相之心有大不得已者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318055_comment'></div>吾既察奸诬之迹，盍幡然而来？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318055_comment'></div>都人之瞻徯至切，将帅之意向易睽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318055_comment'></div>其亟回公府，用图战守之计，迄成美功。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1318055_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年7月</a>　与右史徐宗仁乞追复饶虎臣原官，得旨，守资政殿学士致仕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年7月</a>　草诏。作品：汪立信特赠正奉大夫诰。<div id='poem_1318122' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318122' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318122?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汪立信特赠正奉大夫诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318122")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318122_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318122'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318122'>敕：名臣文武并尽，亦大惟艰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318122_comment'></div>良士旅力既愆，不卬自恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318122_comment'></div>骇闻遗札，悯锡襚章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318122_comment'></div>具官某谋猷川行，知略辏凑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318122_comment'></div>贤长城远矣，才兼牧御之能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318122_comment'></div>曰阃外制之，身佩藩翰之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318122_comment'></div>慨怀危难，倚任攘除，击楫之志未酬，听鼙之思何及！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318122_comment'></div>纳书裘邑，跻三品之荣阶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318122_comment'></div>鸣剑伊吾，想九原之生气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318122_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1318122_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年8月</a>　正谢，赐金带。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年8月壬寅</a>　加夏贵枢密副使、两淮宣抚大使。草制。作品：夏贵授两淮宣抚大使知扬州依前开府仪同三司宁武军节度使左军吾卫上将军枢密副使兼侍卫马军都指挥使加食邑食实封制。<div id='poem_1318078' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318078' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318078?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夏贵特授两淮宣抚大使知扬州依前开府仪同三司宁武军节度使左金吾卫上将军枢密副使兼侍卫马军都指挥使加食邑食实封如故制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年8月壬寅）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318078")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318078_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318078'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318078'>门下：听鼓鼙思帅臣，倚一贤而强本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318078_comment'></div>戒师旅率淮浦，兼两路以宣威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318078_comment'></div>朕逢时隐忧，注意宿望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318078_comment'></div>授西讨之略，方屡奏于肤公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318078_comment'></div>先元戎之行，趣往临于钜屏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318078_comment'></div>王言作命，士听无哗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318078_comment'></div>某官良实而忠纯，沈潜而果毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318078_comment'></div>属大事可当一面，草木莫不知名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318078_comment'></div>□方略无踰老臣，樽俎足以却敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318078_comment'></div>有厌难折冲之壮志，有忧国爱民之盛心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318078_comment'></div>慨王事之急则夜衣而行，愤狄难之炽则缨冠而往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318078_comment'></div>风声鹤唳，策淝水之奇勋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318078_comment'></div>士饱马腾，占郾城之胜气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318078_comment'></div>贰枢列于西辅，仪台视乎三公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318078_comment'></div>维元老之方叔，以饬师干；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318078_comment'></div>维黄发之尚父，以秉旄钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318078_comment'></div>戎容暨暨，趣咨筹幄之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318078_comment'></div>淮水汤汤，尤重广陵之镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318078_comment'></div>念阃寄分任则气势弱，必事权合一则臂指从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318078_comment'></div>欲表里撑拓之得宜，庶首尾运掉之相应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318078_comment'></div>昔高庙之复古，命世忠而捍城；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318078_comment'></div>兹宏建于使名，俾菑攘于外侮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318078_comment'></div>陕东西尽护于诸将，江南北严守于要冲，蔽遮甸畿，控御都会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318078_comment'></div>式固吾圉，亟为朕行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318078_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318078_comment'></div>来旬来宣，告成于王，既任召虎平夷之计；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318078_comment'></div>有严有翼，共武之服，益懋吉甫宪邦之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318078_comment'></div>威信孚可以辑人和，号令明可以作士气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318078_comment'></div>遹图耆定，汔济多艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318078_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1318078_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年8月丁巳</a>　陈宜中以母老辞，回永嘉。丁巳，遣使召。草诏。作品：勉谕陈宜中诏。<div id='poem_1318062' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318062' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318062?labeling=true' target='_blank'>勉谕陈宜中诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年8月丁巳）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318062")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318062_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318062'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318062'>吾惟艰危之时，卿以忠义之忱，扶持宗社，一日去位，吾如失左右手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318062_comment'></div>惠然肯来，再登右揆，用景祐名相茂典，以遂谦冲之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318062_comment'></div>国事日棘，人心易摇，非卿谁与镇安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318062_comment'></div>羽书狎至，诸将出师，非卿谁与指授？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318062_comment'></div>岂可以辞避之小节，忽安危之大计？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318062_comment'></div>俟边境肃清，国势底定，然后从容就养志之乐可也，今何如时，而欲辞位？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318062_comment'></div>趣承涣命，以副具瞻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1318062_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年8月</a>　加张世杰神龙卫四厢都指挥使，总督府诸兵，草诰。作品：张世杰依前保康军承宣使带行枢密都指挥使特授神龙卫四厢都指挥使诰。<div id='poem_1318107' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318107' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318107?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张世杰依前保康军承宣使带行枢密都承旨特授龙神卫四厢都指挥使诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1318107_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318107'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318107'>敕：修甲兵与偕行，既懋干方之略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318107_comment'></div>听鼓鼙而思帅，聿隆进律之褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318107_comment'></div>具官某果毅而尚谋，忠纯而好义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318107_comment'></div>励击楫清中原之志，首敌忾以献功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318107_comment'></div>膺推毂遣将军之权，独折冲而制胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318107_comment'></div>壮概为勤王之倡，雄棱期殄虏之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318107_comment'></div>朕方赫濯威声，将攘除于戎丑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318107_comment'></div>尔惟奖率义旅，庶清肃于江流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318107_comment'></div>载考中兴之名臣，尤重厢部之陟典，内以严勾陈太微之卫，外以澄金陵北固之氛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318107_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318107_comment'></div>定王国、奏肤公，式倚良翰之重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318107_comment'></div>在师中、承天宠，嗣颁懋赏之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318107_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1318107_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年8月</a>　草诰。作品：奖谕张世杰诏。<div id='poem_1318063' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318063' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318063?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奖谕张世杰诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318063")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318063_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318063'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318063'>卿首倡忠义，率旅勤王，屡收隽功，攘却外侮，英猷壮概，每怀嘉绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318063_comment'></div>叹虏谋叵测，□东淮之馈饷，窥右浙之腹心，我是用急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318063_comment'></div>卿进兵江浒，焚其聚粮，牵制虏势，使不得逞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318063_comment'></div>嘉乃茂绩，用锡褒书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318063_comment'></div>其率励三军，乘胜电击，扫清贼垒，以定王国。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1318063_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年8月戊午</a>　赵淇除大理少卿，先生封还録黄，言昔内外以宝玉献似道，淇兄弟为甚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年8月己未</a>　罢赵淇。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年8月甲子</a>　以文天祥为浙西江东制置使，兼知平江府。草诰。作品：文天祥依前权工部尚书都督府参议军事江西安抚使特授浙西江东制置使兼知平江府。<div id='poem_1318102' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318102' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318102?labeling=true' target='_blank'>文天祥依前权工部尚书都督府参赞军事江西安抚使特授浙西江东制置使兼知平江府诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年8月甲子）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318102")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318102_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318102'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318102'>敕：谋元帅、将中军，简在说礼崇诗之彦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318102_comment'></div>分六卿、倡九牧，时维制治保邦之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318102_comment'></div>朕疚怀艰危，注意英隽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318102_comment'></div>有嘉卫社之志，诞畀制阃之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318102_comment'></div>具官某硕大而光明，宏深而肃括。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318102_comment'></div>武文兼备，有经营四方之才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318102_comment'></div>忠义自将，有奖率三军之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318102_comment'></div>惟硕望冠龙甲之选，盖皇祖为燕翼之诒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318102_comment'></div>讨乱略以儆师，人百其勇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318102_comment'></div>追殊遇而欲报，朕知乃心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318102_comment'></div>资胸中甲兵之奇，付阃外弓钺之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318102_comment'></div>若高皇命重臣宅牧，合江浙以专征；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318102_comment'></div>若孝庙诏常伯夺情，念边疆之孔棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318102_comment'></div>总中权于方面，殿巨屏于吴门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318102_comment'></div>内以护日畿之本根，外以复天堑之险阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318102_comment'></div>规模有素，勋业可期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318102_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318102_comment'></div>元戎十乘先行，共武服而国定；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318102_comment'></div>师中三锡承宠，以众正而民从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318102_comment'></div>聿成攘狄之功，丕阐用儒之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318102_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1318102_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年8月</a>　天祥辞免，草诏。作品：赐文天祥辞免不允诏。<div id='poem_1318042' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318042' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318042?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐文天祥辞免依旧权工部尚书都督府参赞军事江西安抚使除浙西江东制置使知平江不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318042")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318042_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318042'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318042'>敕天祥：省所奏，具悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318042_comment'></div>朕未堪多难，疆圉孔棘，御事罔不曰艰大，天毖我成功所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318042_comment'></div>惟时魁儒，秉忠倡义，奖率三军，入卫社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318042_comment'></div>国势为之增重，人心恃以为安，精神折冲，文武是宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318042_comment'></div>若稽高庙，命臣颐浩开制阃于江浙，宏济中兴之业，耆定敉功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318042_comment'></div>卿器度才猷，克迈前哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318042_comment'></div>惟长江之险要未复，畿甸之备守当严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318042_comment'></div>命卿以太常伯兼领二使，表里撑拓，以固吾圉，东西运掉，以靖虏氛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318042_comment'></div>儒帅一临，士气百倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318042_comment'></div>用保乂我文祖受命民，兹惟丰芑诒谋之意，亟其祃牙，纾朕宵旰之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318042_comment'></div>所辞宜不允。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1318042_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年8月庚申</a>　草诰。作品：张起岩依前武功大夫復州团练使特升除带御器械知夔州兼夔路安抚副使诰。<div id='poem_1318105' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318105' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318105?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张起岩依前武功大夫复州团练使特升除带御器械知夔州兼夔路安抚副使诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年8月庚申）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318105")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318105_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318105'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318105'>敕具官某：朕眷蜀道以注怀，属夔门之谋帅，敉宁武功于西土，迪简安边之良将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318105_comment'></div>得猛士守四方，遹求固圉之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318105_comment'></div>尔谋老事壮，知深勇沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318105_comment'></div>宅牧犍为，暨暨捍城之略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318105_comment'></div>参华方面，洸洸敌忾之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318105_comment'></div>畴咨折冲，乃命改镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318105_comment'></div>肆颁进律之渥，明陟扈带之联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318105_comment'></div>其览平沙八阵之图，以护长江万里之险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318105_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1318105_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年8月庚申</a>　草诏。作品：赐知夔州张起岩奖谕诏。<div id='poem_1318047' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318047' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318047?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐知夔州张起岩奖谕诏<span class='inlineComment2'>（八月二十二日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年8月庚申）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318047")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318047_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318047'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318047'>敕起岩：朕惟圣人有金城，所恃者节义之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318047_comment'></div>惟德不明，奸臣误国，分阃守圉之臣，接踵叛降，长江失险，延及上流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318047_comment'></div>每叹国家三百馀年，仁厚涵育，岂惟一颜平原哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318047_comment'></div>自荆峡不守，蜀道未通，将士勤备御而不得抚劳，黎民苦兵革而不得拯救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318047_comment'></div>乃眷西顾，宵旰弗皇宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318047_comment'></div>湖南帅臣芾以卿所奏帛书来上，知卿忠忱义概，坚守夔门，誓与军民赤心图报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318047_comment'></div>中流砥柱，疾风劲草，于卿见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318047_comment'></div>方以久不闻蜀事为急，卿独间关险阻，驰奏于危急之冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318047_comment'></div>有臣如此，国势增重，彼负国卖降者真可愧死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318047_comment'></div>卿又纠率义旅，尅复开州，斩使焚书，誓以灭贼为期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318047_comment'></div>朕嘉叹不已，趣命授卿正任承宣使，领厢部之师，以示褒赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318047_comment'></div>天助者顺，师出有名，丑虏逆天，平殄有期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318047_comment'></div>朕已去奸进贤，改纪其政，中外人心，踊跃思奋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318047_comment'></div>卿其奖率军民，益严战守，如昔璘、玠之保蜀，敌忾献功，朕于节钺无所吝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318047_comment'></div>卿之忠义，旂常竹帛有光焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318047_comment'></div>故兹奖谕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1318047_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年8月</a>　草诰。作品：杨立依前右武大夫加□州观察史依旧知涪州诰。<div id='poem_1318113' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318113' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318113?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨立依前右武大夫特授□州观察使依旧知涪州诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318113")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318113_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318113'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318113'>敕：听鼓鼙，思将臣，欲济艰危之会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318113_comment'></div>儆师徒，讨乱略，盍优奖擢之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318113_comment'></div>其锡明纶，以旌壮概。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318113_comment'></div>具官某忠谊根于天性，知略习于边筹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318113_comment'></div>砥柱蜀道之冲，贤长城远矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318113_comment'></div>汤池涪川之险，曰将军制之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318113_comment'></div>独坚细柳之屯，屡奏《采薇》之捷，士气大振，虏胆为寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318113_comment'></div>修兵与偕行，久徯勤王之旅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318113_comment'></div>出车维其棘，趣收殄虏之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318113_comment'></div>宣力既多，陟明可后？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318113_comment'></div>武爵峻隮于左广，使名超进于廉车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318113_comment'></div>赏不踰时，益励熊罴之勇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318113_comment'></div>师直为壮，遂清蛇豕之氛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318113_comment'></div>亟成隽功，嗣封褒律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318113_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1318113_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年9月辛未</a>　加田谨贤福州观察使，杨邦宪利州观察使，趣入卫。草二诰。作品：田谨贤特授亲卫大夫福建观察使依旧知恩州兼御前诸军都统制诰。杨邦宪特授亲卫大夫利州观察使依旧知播州兼御前诸军都统制诰。<div id='poem_1318110' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318110' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318110?labeling=true' target='_blank'>田谨贤特授亲卫大夫福建观察使依旧知恩州兼御前诸军都统制诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年9月辛未）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318110")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318110_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318110'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318110'>敕：国家多难，正远臣敌忾之秋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318110_comment'></div>节义大闲，嘉良牧效忠之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318110_comment'></div>趣提师而入援，爰进律以示褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318110_comment'></div>具官某性行端纯，器资果毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318110_comment'></div>附众威敌而兼文武，如穰苴之善兵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318110_comment'></div>衔训嗣事以考度程，若宏正之济美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318110_comment'></div>奕世守封疆之固，一心坚忠孝之传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318110_comment'></div>愤猃狁之肆凶，率熊罴而奋勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318110_comment'></div>朕方驰羽檄以召勤王之士，尔乃飞驿书而励报国之忱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318110_comment'></div>击楫誓清，缨冠往救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318110_comment'></div>平原为金城之倡，恨未识真卿之贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318110_comment'></div>河西布玺书之明，尔用锡窦融之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318110_comment'></div>陟崇阶于亲卫，隮峻秩于廉车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318110_comment'></div>汝捍我于艰，其亟授桴鼓而进；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318110_comment'></div>功多有厚赏，以须赐旄钺之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318110_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1318110_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318111' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318111' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318111?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨邦宪特授亲卫大夫利州观察使依旧知播州兼御前诸军都统制诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年9月辛未）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318111")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318111_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318111'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318111'>敕：朕听鼓鼙而思帅，孰济时艰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318111_comment'></div>修戈矛与同仇，载嘉义概。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318111_comment'></div>爰趣援师之至，诞扬褒律之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318111_comment'></div>具官某植志忠纯，秉心宏毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318111_comment'></div>临机料敌，识明金版之六韬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318111_comment'></div>御众牧人，威憺玉关之万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318111_comment'></div>奕世同封疆之守，一忱坚节义之闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318111_comment'></div>愤蛇豕之肆凶，合熊罴而奋勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318111_comment'></div>朕每食不忘于钜鹿，尔惟志常驰于伊吾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318111_comment'></div>奖率劲兵，捍卫多难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318111_comment'></div>真卿未识，独倡平原之盟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318111_comment'></div>窦融来朝，宜锡河西之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318111_comment'></div>思加增秩，檄召勤王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318111_comment'></div>陟亲卫之崇阶，峻廉车之殊渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318111_comment'></div>天助者顺，亟其戒戎乘之行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318111_comment'></div>师克在和，□则有斋钺之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318111_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1318111_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年9月辛巳</a>　有事于明堂，以礼部侍郎眂滌濯九成。黎明，肆赦。撰文。作品：明堂大礼赦文首尾词。<span class='inlineComment2'>（原注九月十四日。）</span><div id='poem_1318036' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318036' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318036?labeling=true' target='_blank'>德祐元年明堂大礼赦文首词 尾词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年9月辛巳）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318036")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318036_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318036'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318036'>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318036_comment'></div>皇极敷言，于帝其训，敢专五福之膺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318036_comment'></div>《我将》既享，畏天之威，永保四方之乂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318036_comment'></div>尚赖股肱咸一德之辅，熊罴不二心之臣，合谋计安，攘狄复境，协成顺信之助，丕集升平之勋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1318036_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年9月</a>　以明堂恩数加封鄞县开国伯，食邑九百户。子昌世授承务郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年9月</a>　草诰。作品：常楙特授端明殿学士提领户部财用诰。<div id='poem_1318089' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318089' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318089?labeling=true' target='_blank'>常楙特授端明殿学士提领户部财用诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318089")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318089_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318089'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318089'>敕：八政食货为先，慨民生之寡遂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318089_comment'></div>九式制用有节，念兵费之孔殷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318089_comment'></div>欲斟酌于源流，必培护于根本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318089_comment'></div>淳化命总计之使，建炎重提纲之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318089_comment'></div>聿遵旧章，简畀硕彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318089_comment'></div>具官某缜密而栗，从容以和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318089_comment'></div>善教得民，有长者之风而不懦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318089_comment'></div>儒雅饬事，有能吏之才而不苛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318089_comment'></div>屡底绩于介藩，旋骞华于禁路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318089_comment'></div>论思蔼严徐之誉，铨综推裘马之公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318089_comment'></div>惟钱谷之入几何，懔兴师之弗给；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318089_comment'></div>而公私之积可痛，嗟足食之尤艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318089_comment'></div>颛其任则可以通有无，振其领则可以柅欺蠹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318089_comment'></div>陟承明秘殿之峻，治板部邦计之繁，视昔三司，冠仪八座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318089_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318089_comment'></div>国以义为利，朕方图损上益下之规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318089_comment'></div>财者人之心，尔勉行爱民厚俗之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318089_comment'></div>惟正是乂，其永有辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318089_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1318089_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年9月己丑53</a>　弟应凤由淮西制置司参议官，以文天祥荐召为太常博士，甫入国门而卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年9月庚寅</a>　草诰。作品：孙虎臣特赠太尉诰。<div id='poem_1318125' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318125' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318125?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙虎臣特赠太尉诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年9月庚寅）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318125")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318125_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318125'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318125'>敕：国家多难，慨无死封疆之臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318125_comment'></div>节义大闲，是为卫社稷之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318125_comment'></div>嗟忠臣之玉折，锡悯册以衮褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318125_comment'></div>具官某英概雄深，壮怀卓荦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318125_comment'></div>威谋制胜，早奏缚青宜结之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318125_comment'></div>猋勇冠军，常有封狼居胥之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318125_comment'></div>虏方投鞭而窥我，意欲折箠而笞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318125_comment'></div>江汤汤，武洸洸，属以讨叛之任，阵堂堂，旂正正，誓以灭虏为期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318125_comment'></div>乃俾守符，乃授齐钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318125_comment'></div>关羽待士卒之善，尚忍负之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318125_comment'></div>田布报君父之忠，惟有死耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318125_comment'></div>义重熊掌，身轻鸿毛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318125_comment'></div>旃裘闻之寒心，营垒莫不流涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318125_comment'></div>朕拊几以叹，听鼙而思，骇闻遗札之言，怅失名将之隽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318125_comment'></div>蜜印紫绶，追封尉府之崇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318125_comment'></div>直盖犀轩，纳书廞襚之饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318125_comment'></div>哀百身之莫赎，凛千载之如生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318125_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318125_comment'></div>存弗居绛侯勃之官，殁尚享段秀实之赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318125_comment'></div>谅尔毅魄，歆我恤章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318125_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1318125_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年9月</a>　草诏。作品：李芾特赠祕阁修撰枢密副都承旨依旧知潭州兼湖南安抚湖北镇抚使诏。<div id='poem_1318094' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318094' class='poemTitle
