南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318094")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318094_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318094'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318094'>敕具官某：十国为连有帅，莫重于艰难之日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318094_comment'></div>诸侯有功进律，莫先于守御之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318094_comment'></div>尔忠义绍于儒先，器能济于世美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318094_comment'></div>中立不倚，奸邪所忌，连蹇维谷，壮气不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318094_comment'></div>宅牧星沙，分阃乡部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318094_comment'></div>护风寒，奏月捷，精神折冲，使湘水无波，岳镇不摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318094_comment'></div>朕嘉乃勤，隮延阁䌷书之职，贰宥廷导旨之联，文武二事兼之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318094_comment'></div>时几孔棘，狡谋匪茹，惟事之备，以清氛祲，集敉功，用对扬我师中锡命之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318094_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1318094_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年10月辛亥</a>　张世杰为沿江制置副使，兼知江阴军，兼浙西策应使，草诰。作品：张世杰依前保康军承宣使带行枢密副都承旨特授沿江制置副使知江阴军兼浙西策应使诰。勉谕张世杰诰。<div id='poem_1318107' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318107' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318107?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张世杰依前保康军承宣使带行枢密都承旨特授龙神卫四厢都指挥使诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318107")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318107_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318107'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318107'>敕：修甲兵与偕行，既懋干方之略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318107_comment'></div>听鼓鼙而思帅，聿隆进律之褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318107_comment'></div>具官某果毅而尚谋，忠纯而好义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318107_comment'></div>励击楫清中原之志，首敌忾以献功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318107_comment'></div>膺推毂遣将军之权，独折冲而制胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318107_comment'></div>壮概为勤王之倡，雄棱期殄虏之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318107_comment'></div>朕方赫濯威声，将攘除于戎丑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318107_comment'></div>尔惟奖率义旅，庶清肃于江流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318107_comment'></div>载考中兴之名臣，尤重厢部之陟典，内以严勾陈太微之卫，外以澄金陵北固之氛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318107_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318107_comment'></div>定王国、奏肤公，式倚良翰之重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318107_comment'></div>在师中、承天宠，嗣颁懋赏之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318107_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1318107_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年10月戊午53</a>　奏请立济王后，加封赐谥。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年</a>　草诰。作品：杨立特授翊卫大夫依前□州观察使升带行御器械知涪州。陈文龙特授同知枢密兼权参知政事诰。尹玉特赠濠州团练使麻士龙特赠高州刺史诰。张起岩特授宁远军承宣使龙神卫四厢都指挥使。<div id='poem_1318115' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318115' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318115?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨立特授翊卫大夫依前□州观察使升带行御器械知涪州诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318115")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318115_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318115'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318115'>敕：多难维其棘，缅思蜀道之艰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318115_comment'></div>十乘以先行，式固涪江之守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318115_comment'></div>慨蛇豕食上国之惨，恃熊罴不二心之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318115_comment'></div>趣戒勤王之师，峻颁进律之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318115_comment'></div>某雄姿果毅，义概魁闳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318115_comment'></div>抚鸣剑驰伊吾，壮哉敌忾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318115_comment'></div>饬戎车伐猃狁，伟矣折冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318115_comment'></div>玉关憺其威名，金城恃以屏翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318115_comment'></div>辑宁五郡，保障一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318115_comment'></div>天降割于我家，重以投鞭断流之患；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318115_comment'></div>心罔不在王室，挺然缨冠救斗之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318115_comment'></div>遣将校而奉帛书，涉险阻而承羽檄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318115_comment'></div>闻者兴起，发于忠忱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318115_comment'></div>念江淮之巢窟未清，而荆益之襟喉犹梗，欲霆击而飙扫，盍卯命而辰行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318115_comment'></div>是用升翊卫于横班，隮扈带于迩列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318115_comment'></div>褒乃劲节，亟其疾驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318115_comment'></div>奖三军，攘奸凶，以报先帝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318115_comment'></div>辟四方，彻疆土，肇敏戎公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318115_comment'></div>投袂而来，侧席以俟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318115_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1318115_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318087' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318087' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318087?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈文龙特授中大夫同知枢密院事兼权参知政事诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年11月庚午）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318087")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318087_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318087'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318087'>敕：祈永命、开中兴，惟哲辅同心之助；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318087_comment'></div>诘戎兵、扬大烈，维世臣继美之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318087_comment'></div>永怀孝祖之圣谟，缅想乾道之贤佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318087_comment'></div>正色敢言之操，知为忠臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318087_comment'></div>赞元经远之猷，进贰宥府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318087_comment'></div>天毖我成功所，予迪惟前人光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318087_comment'></div>兹复见于魁儒，其聿遵于陟典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318087_comment'></div>具官某识明而才裕，学粹而器闳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318087_comment'></div>仁有勇、德有言，蹇蹇救时之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318087_comment'></div>和不流、中不倚，恢恢穆縡之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318087_comment'></div>由首谏以畴咨，登中枢而共济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318087_comment'></div>参翼《天保》、《采薇》之治，协图《蒸民》、《常武》之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318087_comment'></div>慨四郊多垒之未清，凛一日万几之孔棘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318087_comment'></div>若汛涛而求蒸楫，若支厦而萃良工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318087_comment'></div>趣隮淳化名臣之官，峻升元丰执政之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318087_comment'></div>乃兼鬷假，用乂多艰，进爵侯圭，增封邑采，以隆股肱之眷，以计社稷之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318087_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318087_comment'></div>子房决胜而运筹，盍益恢于长策；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318087_comment'></div>召公是似而锡祉，尚念绍于令名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318087_comment'></div>朕方笃绳武之思，尔克迈象贤之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318087_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1318087_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318127' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318127' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318127?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尹玉特赠濠州团练使麻士龙特赠高州刺史诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年11月癸酉）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318127")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318127_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318127'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318127'>敕具官某：见危授命者义之先，致果杀敌者忠之大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318127_comment'></div>迩者熊罴之士，进援毗陵，鼓三军，倡勇敢，尔玉以赣水之师，尔士龙以淮濆之旅，撄锋力战，殒于行阵，而丑虏之殄歼甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318127_comment'></div>尔身虽没，可以愧怯懦退却者，是用赠玉戎团之秩，赠士龙刺史之绶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318127_comment'></div>英魄如生，尚克厉此虏而剪灭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318127_comment'></div>仍录羽林之孤，俾忠义之臣咸劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318127_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1318127_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318108' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318108' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318108?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张起岩特授宁远军承宣使龙神卫四厢都指挥使依旧知夔州兼夔路安抚副使诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318108")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318108_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318108'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318108'>敕：艰危之际，恃节义为金城；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318108_comment'></div>忠良之臣，植封疆为砥柱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318108_comment'></div>孝宽之保玉壁，真卿之守平原，今见其人，朕嘉乃绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318108_comment'></div>具官某秉心纯实，立志雄刚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318108_comment'></div>草木知万福之名，帏幄决子房之胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318108_comment'></div>慨虏氛之甚恶，叹蜀道之至难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318108_comment'></div>细柳坚壁之威，镇安夔路；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318108_comment'></div>劲草疾风之操，克复开江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318108_comment'></div>诛伪使而焚其书，挫丑虏而夺之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318108_comment'></div>奏封来上，大节可嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318108_comment'></div>峻隮容宫之承流，班亚齐钺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318108_comment'></div>密联厢部之分卫，职近周庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318108_comment'></div>式昭褒赏之思，用为屏翰之劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318108_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318108_comment'></div>当一面属大事，朕不忘固圉之勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318108_comment'></div>奖三军定中原，尔益励折冲之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318108_comment'></div>遹收隽捷，嗣对宠光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318108_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1318108_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年11月</a>　除兼礼部尚书，辞免不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年11月甲申</a>　除礼部尚书，兼给事中,辞免不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年11月</a>　辞兼中书舍人，从之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年</a>　赠济王太师、尚书令，进封镇王，谥昭肃。令福王赵与芮择后奉祀，赐田万亩。遣应麟致祭，撰文。作品：祭济王文。<div id='poem_1318283' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318283' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318283?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭济王文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318283")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318283_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318283'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318283'>皇帝遣具位王应麟致祭于皇伯祖、故少保、保静镇潼军节度使、济王、赠太师尚书令、追封镇昭肃王之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318283_comment'></div>惟我理祖，因心则友，则友惟兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318283_comment'></div>惟王令德孝恭，为宋泰伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318283_comment'></div>权臣专政，追蹙王于淮南之冤，九原郁愤，踰五十载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318283_comment'></div>理宗笃叙天伦，哀念不忘，端平更化，亟命复爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318283_comment'></div>维继绝崇赠之典，以待后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318283_comment'></div>度考践阼，首攽追复之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318283_comment'></div>肆予冲人，继志有恪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318283_comment'></div>今逆虏犯顺，国步孔棘，氛祲迫于霅川，夙夜兢兢，思所以回上天悔祸之意，用仰成祖宗厚睦之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318283_comment'></div>赠王师垣端揆，进封大国，锡以令谥，命大宗正选宗属为王后，赐田万亩，俾奉烝尝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318283_comment'></div>仍戒有司，修崇王墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318283_comment'></div>英魂如在，歆我恤章，默相阴祐，亟殄丑虏，扶持宗社，保乂生民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318283_comment'></div>祖宗在天，实宠嘉之，王之春秋享祀，亦永永无斁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1318283_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年11月</a>　兼摄吏部尚书，草诰。作品：翁合特授试尚书礼部侍郎诰。<div id='poem_1318091' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318091' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318091?labeling=true' target='_blank'>翁合特授试尚书礼部侍郎诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（德祐元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318091")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318091_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318091'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318091'>敕：朕慨四维之未张，念多难之求济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318091_comment'></div>为国天地与并，必辨上下以定民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318091_comment'></div>典礼夙夜惟寅，必进英隽以强本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318091_comment'></div>乃眷橐班之旧，诞敷环召之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318091_comment'></div>某官内美修能，瑰意琦行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318091_comment'></div>韶鸣玉洁，渊哉实好斯文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318091_comment'></div>山立时行，纷独有此姱节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318091_comment'></div>羽仪侍从之列，斧藻副诰之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318091_comment'></div>驹皎皎以莫维，凤缥缥其高遰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318091_comment'></div>予未堪难，畴咨百君子之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318091_comment'></div>尔有嘉猷，申命小宗伯之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318091_comment'></div>肃治军之仪，汝翼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318091_comment'></div>□越绋之祭，汝明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318091_comment'></div>聿成樽俎折冲之功，匪曰笾豆司存之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318091_comment'></div>相见何晚，周五礼有待而行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318091_comment'></div>今急而求，鲁两生岂不能致？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318091_comment'></div>式克用乂，惠然来思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318091_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1318091_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年11月</a>　草诰。作品：赵孟传特授华文阁直学士沿海制置使知庆元府诰。<div id='poem_1318098' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318098' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318098?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赵孟传特授华文阁直学士沿海制置使知庆元府诰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318098")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318098_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318098'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318098'>敕：朕申儆豫防，畴咨良牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318098_comment'></div>师保世祚表海，聿怀宗老之遗芳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318098_comment'></div>孝恭尹兹东郊，迪简庭闻之令望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318098_comment'></div>我有明命，贲于价藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318098_comment'></div>具官某质厚而器闳，心醇而才裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318098_comment'></div>以仁者勇协赞去凶之谋，为同姓卿独坚守节之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318098_comment'></div>若昔理祖，眷尔前人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318098_comment'></div>京兆懋弹压之功，司徒敷宽和之教，绣游乡国，阃制沧溟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318098_comment'></div>迨今甘棠之馀思，复见裳华之趾美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318098_comment'></div>尹神皋而曳履，既振家声；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318098_comment'></div>即里社以分弓，俾践先职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318098_comment'></div>隮舜阁之邃直，耀汉绶之荣观，轶袁州再世之光，迈安阳奕叶之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318098_comment'></div>水犀之师，尔其练习；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318098_comment'></div>佩犊之民，尔其镇绥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318098_comment'></div>元帅说礼乐诗书，无忝象贤之助；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318098_comment'></div>州里行忠信笃敬，遹观报政之成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318098_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1318098_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年11月癸巳</a>　张世杰为浙西制置副使，兼知平江府，草制。作品：张世杰特授保康军节度使左金吾卫上将军浙西制置副使兼知平江府仍旧带行枢密都承旨扬州驻劄御前诸军都统行枢督府总统一应军马加食邑食实封制。<div id='poem_1318080' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318080' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318080?labeling=true' target='_blank'>张世杰特授保康军节度使左金吾卫上将军浙西制置副使兼知平江府仍旧带行枢密都承旨扬州驻劄御前诸军都统行枢督府总统一应军马加食邑食实封制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年3月乙酉）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318080")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318080_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318080'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318080'>门下：千里之内曰畿，莫首重乎根本之地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318080_comment'></div>十国为连有帅，莫兼严平弓钺之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318080_comment'></div>惟予一人，未堪多难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318080_comment'></div>出车王事棘矣，孰式遏于要冲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318080_comment'></div>跽毂将军制之，爰畴咨于宿望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318080_comment'></div>建淑旂而分阃，敷明綍以扬廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318080_comment'></div>某官雄毅而沈潜，忠良而笃实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318080_comment'></div>帷幄决子房之胜，方略运于韬钤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318080_comment'></div>草木知万福之名，威棱憺于边境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318080_comment'></div>矫矫冠军之勇，惓惓卫上之忱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318080_comment'></div>修戈矛与同仇，志殄歼于逆虏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318080_comment'></div>儆师徒讨乱略，躬奖率于颜行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318080_comment'></div>忾缀斿之阽危，首投袂而入援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318080_comment'></div>执讯获丑，《采薇》之捷屡书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318080_comment'></div>披雾清氛，前茅之气大振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318080_comment'></div>再念吴门之危急，尝劳师律之菑攘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318080_comment'></div>却敌贤于长城，微卿民其左衽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318080_comment'></div>今堂奥之寇寖迫，而藩篱之重当严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318080_comment'></div>稽中兴名将之成规，膺右浙制垣之重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318080_comment'></div>谨固保障则常润可复，汛扫妖祲则京师以宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318080_comment'></div>克壮其猷，用锡尔祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318080_comment'></div>斋坛授钺，领巨镇于房陵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318080_comment'></div>吾臣司金，盛戎容于缇骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318080_comment'></div>以危难之间受任，以节度之事付公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318080_comment'></div>兼升牧守之荣，益强屏翰之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318080_comment'></div>衍其采邑，明我茂恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318080_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318080_comment'></div>地利不如人和，朕遹求于多助；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318080_comment'></div>武服以定王国，尔趣奏于肤公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318080_comment'></div>三军同力，以收复宇之勋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318080_comment'></div>众志成城，以集安民之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318080_comment'></div>俾金汤之不耸，永带砺之有光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318080_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1318080_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年11月</a>　左丞相留梦炎用徐囊为御史，擢北降官员朱禩孙、黄万石等，缴奏。作品：缴驳留梦炎擢用徐囊黄万石疏。<div id='poem_1318182' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318182' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318182?labeling=true' target='_blank'>缴驳留梦炎擢用徐囊黄万石疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318182")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318182_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318182'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318182'>囊与梦炎同乡，有私人之嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318182_comment'></div>万石粗戾无学，南昌失守，误国罪大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318182_comment'></div>今方欲引以自助，善类为所搏噬者，必携持而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318182_comment'></div>吴浚贪墨轻躁，岂宜用之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318182_comment'></div>况梦炎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1318182", 1318182, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>舛令</span>慢谏，谠言弗敢告，今之卖降者，多其任用之士。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1318182_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年11月</a>　左丞相留梦炎用徐囊为御史，擢北降官员朱禩孙、黄万石等，缴奏，不报，再奏，作文。作品：乞罢疏。<div id='poem_1318183' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318183' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318183?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞罢疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1275年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318183")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318183_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318183'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318183'>因危急而紊纪纲，以偏见而咈公议，臣封驳不行，与大臣异论，势不当留。</div><div id='poem_sentence_0_1318183_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
金华
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d626bcb907c3403c9ea5324aa96631da_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d626bcb907c3403c9ea5324aa96631da");'><span id='d626bcb907c3403c9ea5324aa96631da_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1241&endYear=1242')">1241-1242年</a>，19-20岁</div><div id='d626bcb907c3403c9ea5324aa96631da' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1241&endYear=1241')">1241年7月，</a>　侍父婺州，学从王埜，习宏词科。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1241&endYear=1241')">1241年7？</a>　又从徐凤受学习。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1241&endYear=1241')">1241年</a>　应麟初登第时，认为当时读书人沽名钓誉，一旦高中，便将一切的理想抱负，国家的制度和历史都抛弃了，并不是国家所期望的学识渊博的人，故发愤誓以博学宏词科自见，不仅借藏书阁的书来读，而且一直以小册纳袖中，凡见典故异闻则笔录之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1242&endYear=1242')">1242年</a>　同年，史弥巩知婺州，与应麟父共事并且相处的很愉快。史弥巩有五子，能之、胄之皆与应麟是同年进士，及有之、肎之、育之都陪同。两家子弟相处融洽。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1242&endYear=1242')">1242年</a>　御史刘晋之诬衢州掾，应麟父撝秉公处之。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
柯城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='938e8c14cdcd4c169ef8fdd342672ddf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("938e8c14cdcd4c169ef8fdd342672ddf");'><span id='938e8c14cdcd4c169ef8fdd342672ddf_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1243&endYear=1244')">1243-1244年</a>，21-22岁</div><div id='938e8c14cdcd4c169ef8fdd342672ddf' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1243&endYear=1243')">1243年</a>　当地居民以应麟年少便轻视他，不按时缴纳赋税。应麟告郡守并用法律制裁他们，于是事情立刻解决，几个校尉想反叛，县令翁甫匆忙之中不知怎么办，应麟用道理说服了想反叛的校尉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1243&endYear=1243')">1243年</a>　父撝摄知婺州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1244')">1244年</a>　父撝以祕书丞知徽州，迁吏部郎中、崇政殿说书。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='f3109204761c4877a6b48d82e487dbb5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f3109204761c4877a6b48d82e487dbb5");'><span id='f3109204761c4877a6b48d82e487dbb5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1247')">1246-1247年</a>，24-25岁</div><div id='f3109204761c4877a6b48d82e487dbb5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年10月</a>　赴西安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年6月</a>　昌国令沈壑重建昌国学大成殿，作记。作品：重建昌国大成殿记。<div id='poem_1318237' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318237' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318237?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昌国州重建大成殿记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1247年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318237")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318237_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318237'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318237'>淳祐纪元之六年，圣上首善崇化，以四方风，绿字穗书，敷贲雍頖，庠声序音，丕冒出日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318237_comment'></div>昌国大夫沈睿始至，谒校宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318237_comment'></div>时礼殿之建适六十祀矣，朽蠹弗葺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318237_comment'></div>诸生进而言曰：「学肇基于县治之东，淳熙间王令沅迁于芙蓉洲西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318237_comment'></div>挹秀涵清，气势闳伟，俊人魁士，含章挺生，道原文脉，实系兹殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318237_comment'></div>盍鼎新之，对扬《云汉》作人之休德」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318237_comment'></div>君曰：「承流宣化，职也，敢不祗若」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318237_comment'></div>啬用鸠工，士驩趋之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318237_comment'></div>参预应公嘉其意，谂帅守颜公，佐以郡少府钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318237_comment'></div>经始于明年莫春，越季夏殿成，般尔献公，枚枚奕奕，貌象惟肖，如临沂泗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318237_comment'></div>侑坐啜食，端章俨䓇，降庭庭止，式礼莫愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318237_comment'></div>冠进衣逢，瞻仪兴敬，观摩丽习，文风蔼如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318237_comment'></div>明年，君入监左帑，相与祠于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318237_comment'></div>既十年，诸生思之，请著石章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318237_comment'></div>应麟鄞末学也，辞弗获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318237_comment'></div>尝读《临》之象曰：「君子以教思无穷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318237_comment'></div>夫泽上有地，犹君子之近民也，近民则教弥数，故《周官》族闾之读法，视州党尤密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318237_comment'></div>今之学郡修而邑弛，为吏者政急而化缓，期会讼狱，日鳃鳃畏，百适虑不越几案，而夫子宫墙漫不省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318237_comment'></div>健者舞知，怠者视荫，弁髦武城、蒲、密之言，而诿曰难治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318237_comment'></div>教化不明，醇浇朴散，治不愈难与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318237_comment'></div>然非独今日也，汉东京儒雅最盛，令长垂意学校者惟宋均、杨仁者著于传，何其慨寂寥哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318237_comment'></div>沈君能急所缓，喟然兴于学，可谓知本矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318237_comment'></div>昔孔子慨道不行，托兴于浮海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318237_comment'></div>是邦近天子之光，家诗书，人孝悌，吾道其行矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318237_comment'></div>县大夫虽不得宿其业以候道化之成，后之君子勿替引之，率时髦士规圣矩贤，毋以小成自画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318237_comment'></div>学必正大，志必高明，言必仁义，行必笃敬，进而经纶天下之大经，退而居贤德善俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318237_comment'></div>俾耆老搢绅顾瞻楹桷，肃然改容，曰：「此贤令教思之德也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318237_comment'></div>将见立于朝者为皋、稷，入其里者比邹、鲁，尚当墨笔以颂化民成俗之功云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1318237_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
苏州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f29ceaf1bd1b4aefbf612150416558d8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f29ceaf1bd1b4aefbf612150416558d8");'><span id='f29ceaf1bd1b4aefbf612150416558d8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1248&endYear=1252')">1248-1252年</a>，26-30岁</div><div id='f29ceaf1bd1b4aefbf612150416558d8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1248&endYear=1248')">1248年10月</a>　长洲宰将其县的花园命名为“茂苑”，茂苑即长洲苑，但非长洲宰所在之长洲，应麟就此向长洲宰进行了长洲之辨，初显博学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1248&endYear=1248')">1248年</a>　长子学良生，字茂章。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1248&endYear=1248')">1248年</a>　摹刻正月天申节放生池戒宰烹御札称，有表。作品：代进放生池御札摹本表。<div id='poem_1318169' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318169' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318169?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代进放生池御札摹本表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1248年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318169")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318169_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318169'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318169'>久道化成，配天其泽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318169_comment'></div>好生德洽，与物为春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318169_comment'></div>焜耀十行，涵濡万汇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318169_comment'></div>于穆仁皇之盛治，聿严景祐之圣谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318169_comment'></div>《湛露》宴饮之仪，自奉有节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318169_comment'></div>《行苇》忠厚之意，各得其宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318169_comment'></div>肫肫发育之仁，永永鸿长之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318169_comment'></div>恭惟命凝鼎正，德体乾元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318169_comment'></div>瑞纪流虹，茂膺必得寿之祉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318169_comment'></div>爱存避蚁，益普欲并生之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318169_comment'></div>恐朋酒杀羔之伤和，景正旦放鸠之示惠，推此一念，宜于亿年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318169_comment'></div>臣祗觌奎光，肃登琰刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318169_comment'></div>广充仁术，愿探孟子之忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318169_comment'></div>摹写宸章，敬上真卿之颂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1318169_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1249&endYear=1250')">1249-1250年</a>　在从事郎任上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1251&endYear=1251')">1251年</a>　应麟父王撝撰《舆服志》六卷，理宗赐御书“竹林汲古传忠”六字，应麟代撰谢赐表，吏部公因额其里居堂曰“汲古堂”，所撰文曰《汲古文集》。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1251&endYear=1251')">1251年2月乙未</a>　左丞相郑清之等上玉蝶、日历、会要及光宗宁宗《宝训》、宁宗《经武要略》，应麟作二表。作品：拟国史院进光宗宁宗宝训表。代宰臣以下贺奉安光宗宁宗宝训宁宗经武要略今上玉蝶日历会要礼成表。<div id='poem_1318166' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318166' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318166?labeling=true' target='_blank'>拟国史院进光宗宁宗宝训表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1251年2月乙未）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318166")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318166_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318166'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318166'>盛帝重光，垂百王之丕式；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318166_comment'></div>大君继序，辑二典之宏规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318166_comment'></div>萃篇目而胪分，晋严□而露奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318166_comment'></div>窃以大禹贻孙之则，著在《夏书》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318166_comment'></div>武王燕翼之谋，播于《周雅》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318166_comment'></div>允铄两朝之懿，于昭载籍之传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318166_comment'></div>光宗皇帝遹骏有声，严恭自度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318166_comment'></div>刚健以新其德，躬揽政机；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318166_comment'></div>精一而执厥中，心传道统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318166_comment'></div>宁宗皇帝始终典学，玄默化民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318166_comment'></div>无怠无荒，三十年之享国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318166_comment'></div>曰慈曰俭，六五帝以匹休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318166_comment'></div>作者圣，述者明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318166_comment'></div>显哉谟，承哉烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318166_comment'></div>丰功懋德，编之诗书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318166_comment'></div>美政嘉言，布在方策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318166_comment'></div>天开累洽，日阐大猷，抽金匮之缺遗，裒兰台之纪载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318166_comment'></div>粤若绍熙之嗣服，施于嘉定之守文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318166_comment'></div>任贤修己之远谟，立武攘夷之要略，写之琬琰，炳若丹青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318166_comment'></div>主善为师，恢至道，示轨范；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318166_comment'></div>有条不紊，扬洪烈，章缉熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318166_comment'></div>冠周史之宝书，轶楚臣之训典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318166_comment'></div>寅上西清之御，伫严东壁之储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318166_comment'></div>恭惟志笃昭功，治隆绳武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318166_comment'></div>念兹皇祖，鉴成宪以无愆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318166_comment'></div>迪惟前人，式历年而勿替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318166_comment'></div>聿追来孝，率乂棐彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318166_comment'></div>法二后之不敢康，作一艺而摛罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318166_comment'></div>用训丕德，其永孚休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318166_comment'></div>臣等载笔非长，总纲有愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318166_comment'></div>承明登进，又新天圣之盛仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318166_comment'></div>大清览观，愿举宝元之故事。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1318166_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1318137' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1318137' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1318137?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代宰臣以下贺奉安光宗皇帝宁宗皇帝宝训宁宗皇帝经武要略今上皇帝玉牒日历会要礼成表<span class='inlineComment2'>（词科所业）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1251年2月乙未）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29985, "南宋", "王应麟", "poem_title_1318137")'>王应麟</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1318137_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1318137'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1318137'>臣某等言：恭睹奉安光宗皇帝、宁宗皇帝《宝训》、宁宗皇帝《经武要略》、今上皇帝《玉牒》、《日历》、《会要》礼成者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1318137_comment'></div>文谟武烈，并扬二后之休；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1318137_comment'></div>汉典唐经，参著一王之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1318137_comment'></div>森宝储而日揭，粲缛礼以星陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1318137_comment'></div>臣某等欢抃欢抃、顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1318137_comment'></div>窃以鉴先宪、求多闻，《商书》垂范；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1318137_comment'></div>有常德、立武事，《周雅》纪功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1318137_comment'></div>迨开成标帝籍之名，暨鲁史谨策书之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1318137_comment'></div>至若观会通而行礼，尤先撮纪要以举纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1318137_comment'></div>兹萃进于一时，宜辑成于五典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1318137_comment'></div>允哲光皇之揖逊，于昭宁考之俭勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1318137_comment'></div>燕翼诒谋，焜耀亿万年之训；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1318137_comment'></div>攘夷复古，坚凝三十载之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1318137_comment'></div>有严论述于史筵，申命纂修于宥省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1318137_comment'></div>天启离明之治，日新贲象之文，洽美化于登三，焕鸿猷于袭六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1318137_comment'></div>瑶编温润，金鐀閟严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1318137_comment'></div>系日系时，裒嘉熙、淳祐之记注；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1318137_comment'></div>有伦有要，粹宝、绍、端平之宪章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1318137_comment'></div>讨裁分饬于群儒，尊阁载差于谷旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1318137_comment'></div>韶钧烨煜，羽卫葳蕤，绚缫采以展仪，瞻冕旒而执读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1318137_comment'></div>事该经纬，备清览于迩英；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1318137_comment'></div>瑞集图书，肃秘藏于广内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1318137_comment'></div>恭遇皇帝陛下心传精一，学懋缉熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1318137_comment'></div>道德风烈之庶几，遹追来孝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1318137_comment'></div>制度纪纲之能永，勿替历年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1318137_comment'></div>功光祖宗，政布方策，率彝章而由旧，据行事以鉴新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1318137_comment'></div>文武大略举焉，圣而继圣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1318137_comment'></div>礼乐庶事备矣，书不一书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1318137_comment'></div>臣等钦觌圣明，欣逢熙洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1318137_comment'></div>始于勤而治内外，愿骏惠于闳摹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1318137_comment'></div>祓厥文而作《春秋》，嗣铺张于伟绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1318137_comment'></div>臣等无任瞻天望圣、激切屏营之至，谨奉表称贺以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1318137_comment'></div>臣某等欢抃欢抃、顿首顿首，谨言<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1318137_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1318137'>「瞻天望圣」以下原脱，据右引补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1318137_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1318137'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_32_1318137_0'>⑴ 《四明文献集》卷三。又见《玉海》卷二○四《辞学指南》。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1318137_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1252&endYear=1252')">1252年</a>　理宗赐吏部公御制《周易徹章诗》，代撰谢赐表。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1252&endYear=1252')">1252年</a>　应麟父王撝以直祕阁知温州。<br /></div>
-----end

扬州

-----title
临海
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='90eee95cac1344b7a3b463ec0f0c153b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("90eee95cac1344b7a3b463ec0f0c153b");'><span id='90eee95cac1344b7a3b463ec0f0c153b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1262&endYear=1262')">1262年</a>，40岁</div><div id='90eee95cac1344b7a3b463ec0f0c153b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1262&endYear=1262')">1262年8月</a>　赴台州。<br /></div>
